Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa

# Khuddakanikāye

## Therāpadānapāḷi

#### (Paṭhamo bhāgo)

### 1. Buddhavaggo

#### 1. Buddhaapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Tathāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0001" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0001" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0001" /> jetavane vasantaṃ, apucchi vedehamunī nataṅgo;
```

```
‘‘Sabbaññubuddhā kira nāma honti, bhavanti te hetubhi kehi vīra’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesī, ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena;
```

```
‘‘Ye pubbabuddhesu <note>sabbabuddhesu (syā.)</note> katādhikārā, aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva sambodhimukhena dhīrā, ajjhāsayenāpi mahābalena;
```

```
Paññāya tejena sutikkhapaññā, sabbaññubhāvaṃ anupāpuṇanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Ahampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0002" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0002" /> pubbabuddhesu, buddhattamabhipatthayiṃ,
```

```
Manasāyeva hutvāna, dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Atha <pb ed="M" n="1.0002" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0001" /> buddhāpadānāni, suṇātha suddhamānasā;
```

```
Tiṃsapāramisampuṇṇā, dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Sambodhiṃ buddhaseṭṭhānaṃ, sasaṅghe lokanāyake;
```

```
Dasaṅgulī namassitvā, sirasā abhivādayiṃ <note>abhivādaye (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā buddhakhettesu, ratanā vijjantisaṅkhiyā;
```

```
Ākāsaṭṭhā ca bhūmaṭṭhā <note>bhummaṭṭhā (sī. syā.)</note>, manasā sabbamāhariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha rūpiyabhūmiyaṃ, pāsādaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Nekabhummaṃ ratanamayaṃ, ubbiddhaṃ nabhamuggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Vicittathambhaṃ sukataṃ, suvibhattaṃ mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Kanakamayasaṅghāṭaṃ, kontacchattehi maṇḍitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭhamā veḷuriyā bhūmi, vimalabbhasamā subhā;
```

```
Naḷinajalajākiṇṇā, varakañcanabhūmiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Pavāḷaṃsā pavāḷavaṇṇā, kāci lohitakā subhā;
```

```
Indagopakavaṇṇābhā, bhūmi obhāsatī disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Suvibhattā gharamukhā, niyyūhā sīhapañjarā;
```

```
Caturo vedikā jālā, gandhāveḷā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Nīlā pītā lohitakā, odātā suddhakāḷakā;
```

```
Kūṭāgāravarūpetā, sattaratanabhūsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Olokamayā <pb ed="P" n="1.0002" /> padumā, vāḷavihaṅgasobhitā;
```

```
Nakkhattatārakākiṇṇā, candasūrehi <note>candasuriyehi (sī. syā.)</note> maṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Hemajālena <pb ed="T" n="1.0003" /> sañchannā, soṇṇakiṅkiṇikāyutā;
```

```
Vātavegena kūjanti, soṇṇamālā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Mañjeṭṭhakaṃ lohitakaṃ, pītakaṃ haripiñjaraṃ;
```

```
Nānāraṅgehi sampītaṃ <note>saṃcittaṃ (syā.)</note>, ussitaddhajamālinī <note>māliniṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Na naṃ <note>nānā (sī. syā.)</note> bahūnekasatā, phalikā rajatāmayā;
```

```
Maṇimayā lohitaṅgā, masāragallamayā tathā;
```

```
Nānāsayanavicittā, saṇhakāsikasanthatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Kampalā <pb ed="M" n="1.0003" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0003" /> dukūlā cīnā, paṭṭuṇṇā paṇḍupāvurā;
```

```
Vividhattharaṇaṃ sabbaṃ, manasā paññapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Tāsu tāsveva bhūmīsu, ratanakūṭalaṅkataṃ;
```

```
Maṇiverocanā ukkā, dhārayantā sutiṭṭhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Sobhanti esikā thambhā, subhā kañcanatoraṇā;
```

```
Jambonadā sāramayā, atho rajatamayāpi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Nekā sandhī suvibhattā, kavāṭaggaḷacittitā;
```

```
Ubhato puṇṇaghaṭānekā, padumuppalasaṃyutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Atīte sabbabuddhe ca, sasaṅghe lokanāyake;
```

```
Pakativaṇṇarūpena, nimminitvā sasāvake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Tena dvārena pavisitvā, sabbe buddhā sasāvakā;
```

```
Sabbasoṇṇamaye pīṭhe, nisinnā ariyamaṇḍalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca etarahi atthi, buddhā loke anuttarā;
```

```
Atīte <pb ed="T" n="1.0004" /> vattamānā ca, bhavanaṃ sabbe samāhariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Paccekabuddhenekasate, sayambhū aparājite;
```

```
Atīte vattamāne ca, bhavanaṃ sabbe samāhariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Kapparukkhā bahū atthi, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā;
```

```
Sabbaṃ dussaṃ samāhantā, acchādemi ticīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Khajjaṃ bhojjaṃ sāyanīyaṃ, sampannaṃ pānabhojanaṃ;
```

```
Maṇimaye subhe patte, saṃpūretvā adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbavatthasamā hutvā, maṭṭhā <note>maṭṭā (sī.)</note> cīvarasaṃyutā;
```

```
Madhurā sakkharā ceva, telā ca madhuphāṇitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Tappitā paramannena, sabbe te ariyamaṇḍalā;
```

```
Ratanagabbhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0003" /> pavisitvā, kesarīva guhāsayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Mahārahamhi sayane, sīhaseyyamakappayuṃ;
```

```
Sampajānā samuṭṭhāya, sayane <note>seyye (syā.)</note> pallaṅkamābhujuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Gocaraṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0004" /> sabbabuddhānaṃ, jhānaratisamappitā;
```

```
Aññe dhammāni desenti, aññe kīḷanti iddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Aññe <pb ed="V" n="1.0004" /> abhiññā appenti, abhiññā vasibhāvitā;
```

```
Vikubbanā vikubbanti, aññenekasahassiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhāpi buddhe pucchanti, visayaṃ sabbaññumālayaṃ;
```

```
Gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ, paññāya vinibujjhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvakā buddhe pucchanti, buddhā pucchanti sāvake;
```

```
Aññamaññañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0005" /> pucchitvā <note>pucchanti (sī. syā.)</note>, aññoññaṃ byākaronti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhā paccekabuddhā ca, sāvakā paricārakā;
```

```
Evaṃ sakāya ratiyā, pāsādebhiramanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Chattā tiṭṭhantu ratanā, kañcanāveḷapantikā;
```

```
Muttājālaparikkhittā, sabbe dhārentu <note>dhārenti (ka.)</note> matthake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavantu ceḷavitānā, soṇṇatārakacittitā;
```

```
Vicittamalyavitatā, sabbe dhārentu matthake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Vitatā malyadāmehi, gandhadāmehi sobhitā;
```

```
Dussadāmaparikiṇṇā, ratanadāmabhūsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphābhikiṇṇā sucittā, surabhigandhabhūsitā;
```

```
Gandhapañcaṅgulikatā <note>gandhapañcaṅgulaṃ katā (aṭṭha.)</note>, hemacchadanachāditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Catuddisā pokkharañño, padumuppalasanthatā;
```

```
Sovaṇṇarūpā khāyantu, padmaṃreṇurajuggatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphantu pādapā sabbe, pāsādassa samantato;
```

```
Sayañca pupphā muñcitvā, gantvā bhavanamokiruṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Sikhino tattha naccantu, dibbahaṃsā pakūjare;
```

```
Karavīkā ca gāyantu, dijasaṅghā samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Bheriyo sabbā vajjantu, vīṇā sabbā rasantu <note>ravantu (sī. syā.)</note> tā;
```

```
Sabbā saṅgīti vattantu, pāsādassa samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā <pb ed="T" n="1.0006" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0005" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0004" /> buddhakhettamhi, cakkavāḷe tato pare;
```

```
Mahantā jotisampannā, acchinnā ratanāmayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṭṭhantu soṇṇapallaṅkā, dīparukkhā jalantu te;
```

```
Bhavantu ekapajjotā, dasasahassiparamparā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Gaṇikā lāsikā ceva, naccantu accharāgaṇā;
```

```
Nānāraṅgā padissantu, pāsādassa samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Dumagge <pb ed="V" n="1.0005" /> pabbatagge vā, sinerugirimuddhani;
```

```
Ussāpemi dhajaṃ sabbaṃ, vicittaṃ pañcavaṇṇikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Narā nāgā ca gandhabbā, sabbe devā upentu te;
```

```
Namassantā pañjalikā, pāsādaṃ parivārayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ kammaṃ, kattabbaṃ kiriyaṃ mama;
```

```
Kāyena vācā manasā, tidase sukataṃ kataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Ye sattā saññino atthi, ye ca sattā asaññino;
```

```
Kataṃ puññaphalaṃ mayhaṃ, sabbe bhāgī bhavantu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Yesaṃ kataṃ suviditaṃ, dinnaṃ puññaphalaṃ mayā;
```

```
Ye ca tattha <note>tasmiṃ (sī. ka.)</note> na jānanti, devā gantvā nivedayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbalokamhi <note>sabbe lokamhi (syā. ka.)</note> ye sattā, jīvantāhārahetukā;
```

```
Manuññaṃ bhojanaṃ sabbaṃ <note>sabbe (syā.)</note>, labhantu mama cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Manasā dānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, manasā pasādamāvahiṃ;
```

```
Pūjitā sabbasambuddhā, paccekā jinasāvakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="1.0007" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Duve bhave pajānāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi, manasā patthanāphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Devānaṃ adhiko homi, bhavāmi manujādhipo;
```

```
Rūpalakkhaṇasampanno, paññāya asamo bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Bhojanaṃ vividhaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, ratanañca anappakaṃ;
```

```
Vividhāni ca vatthāni, nabhā <note>nabhasā (syā.)</note> khippaṃ upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā <pb ed="M" n="1.0006" /> pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, dibbā bhakkhā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā <pb ed="P" n="1.0005" /> pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, ratanā sabbe upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā <pb ed="V" n="1.0006" /> pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe gandhā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ <note>yattha (syā.), yaññaṃ (ka.)</note> hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe yānā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe mālā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, alaṅkārā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā <pb ed="T" n="1.0008" /> pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbā kaññā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, madhusakkharā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Pathabyā pabbate ceva, ākāse udake vane;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi, sabbe khajjā upenti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Adhane addhika <note>addhike (syā.)</note> jane, yācake ca pathāvino;
```

```
Dadāmihaṃ <note>dadāmiha (sī.) dadāmi taṃ (syā.)</note> dānavaraṃ, sambodhivarapattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Nādento pabbataṃ selaṃ, gajjento bahalaṃ giriṃ;
```

```
Sadevakaṃ hāsayanto, buddho loke bhavāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Disā dasavidhā loke, yāyato natthi antakaṃ;
```

```
Tasmiñca disābhāgamhi, buddhakhettā asaṅkhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Pabhā pakittitā mayhaṃ, yamakā raṃsivāhanā;
```

```
Etthantare raṃsijālaṃ, āloko vipulo bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Ettake <pb ed="M" n="1.0007" /> lokadhātumhi, sabbe passantu maṃ janā;
```

```
Sabbe maṃ anuvattantu, yāva brahmanivesanaṃ <note>sabbeva sumanā hontu, sabbe maṃ anuvattare (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Visiṭṭhamadhunādena, amatabherimāhaniṃ;
```

```
Etthantare janā sabbe, suṇantu madhuraṃ giraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammameghena vassante, sabbe hontu anāsavā;
```

```
Yettha pacchimakā sattā, sotāpannā bhavantu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Datvā <pb ed="T" n="1.0009" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0007" /> dātabbakaṃ dānaṃ, sīlaṃ pūretvā asesato;
```

```
Nekkhammapāramiṃ gantvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇḍite <pb ed="P" n="1.0006" /> paripucchitvā, katvā vīriyamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Khantiyā pāramiṃ gantvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Katvā daḷhamadhiṭṭhānaṃ, saccapārami pūriya;
```

```
Mettāya pāramiṃ gantvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhālābhe sukhe dukkhe, sammāne cāvamānane <note>sammāne ca vimānane (ka.) sammānane vimānane (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbattha samako hutvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Kosajjaṃ bhayato disvā, vīriyaṃ cāpi khemato;
```

```
Āraddhavīriyā hotha, esā buddhānusāsanī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Vivādaṃ bhayato disvā, avivādañca khemato;
```

```
Samaggā sakhilā hotha, esā buddhānusāsanī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Pamādaṃ bhayato disvā, appamādañca khemato;
```

```
Bhāvethaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ, esā buddhānusāsanī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Samāgatā bahū buddhā, arahantā <note>arahanto (syā.)</note> ca sabbaso;
```

```
Sambuddhe arahante ca, vandamānā namassatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ acintiyā buddhā, buddhadhammā acintiyā;
```

```
Acintiye pasannānaṃ, vipāko hoti acintiyo’’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā attano buddhacariyaṃ sambhāvayamāno buddhāpadāniyaṃ <note>buddhacariyaṃ (sī.) buddhacaritaṃ (syā.)</note> nāma dhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthāti.

Buddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃ.

#### 2. Paccekabuddhaapadānaṃ

Atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0010" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0008" /> paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ suṇātha –

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Tathāgataṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0007" /> jetavane vasantaṃ, apucchi vedehamunī nataṅgo;
```

```
‘Paccekabuddhā kira nāma honti, bhavanti te hetubhi kehi vīra’ <note>dhīra (sī.) dhīrā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāha <pb ed="V" n="1.0008" /> sabbaññuvaro mahesī, ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena;
```

```
‘Ye pubbabuddhesu <note>sabbabuddhesu (syā. ka.)</note> katādhikārā, aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘‘Teneva saṃvegamukhena dhīrā, vināpi buddhehi sutikkhapaññā;
```

```
Ārammaṇenāpi parittakena, paccekabodhiṃ anupāpuṇanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbamhi lokamhi mamaṃ ṭhapetvā, paccekabuddhehi samova natthi;
```

```
Tesaṃ imaṃ vaṇṇapadesamattaṃ, vakkhāmahaṃ sādhu mahāmunīnaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sayameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0011" /> buddhānaṃ mahāisīnaṃ, sādhūni vākyāni madhūva <note>madhuṃva (sī.)</note> khuddaṃ;
```

```
Anuttaraṃ bhesajaṃ patthayantā, suṇātha sabbesu pasannacittā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paccekabuddhānaṃ samāgatānaṃ, paramparaṃ byākaraṇāni yāni;
```

```
Ādīnavo yañca virāgavatthuṃ, yathā ca bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sarāgavatthūsu <pb ed="M" n="1.0009" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0008" /> virāgasaññī, rattamhi lokamhi virattacittā;
```

```
Hitvā papañce jitaphanditāni <note>vidiya phanditāni (sī.) jitabandhitāni (ka.)</note>, tatheva bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃ;
```

```
Mettena cittena hitānukampī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃ;
```

```
Na puttamiccheyya kuto sahāyaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṃsaggajātassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0012" /> bhavanti snehā, snehanvayaṃ dukkhamidaṃ pahoti;
```

```
Ādīnavaṃ snehajaṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mitte suhajje anukampamāno, hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibaddhacitto;
```

```
Etaṃ bhayaṃ santhave pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vaṃso visālova yathā visatto, puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhā;
```

```
Vaṃse kaḷīrova asajjamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘‘Migo araññamhi yathā abaddho, yenicchakaṃ gacchati gocarāya;
```

```
Viññū naro seritaṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āmantanā <pb ed="M" n="1.0010" /> hoti sahāyamajjhe, vāse ca <note>vāse (sī. syā.) suttanipātepi ‘‘ca‘‘kāro natthi</note> ṭhāne gamane cārikāya;
```

```
Anabhijjhitaṃ seritaṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khiḍḍā <pb ed="T" n="1.0013" /> ratī hoti sahāyamajjhe, puttesu pemaṃ vipulañca hoti;
```

```
Piyavippayogaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0009" /> vijigucchamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cātuddiso <pb ed="V" n="1.0009" /> appaṭigho ca hoti, santussamāno itarītarena;
```

```
Parissayānaṃ sahitā achambhī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dussaṅgahā pabbajitāpi eke, atho gahaṭṭhā gharamāvasantā;
```

```
Appossukko paraputtesu hutvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘‘Oropayitvā gihibyañjanāni, sañchinnapatto yathā koviḷāro;
```

```
Chetvāna vīro gihibandhanāni, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃ caraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
```

```
Abhibhuyya sabbāni parissayāni, careyya tenattamano satīmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘‘No <pb ed="T" n="1.0014" /> ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃ caraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
```

```
Rājāva raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya, eko care mātaṅgaraññeva nāgo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘‘Addhā <pb ed="M" n="1.0011" /> pasaṃsāma sahāyasampadaṃ, seṭṭhā samā sevitabbā sahāyā;
```

```
Ete aladdhā anavajjabhojī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘‘Disvā suvaṇṇassa pabhassarāni, kammāraputtena suniṭṭhitāni;
```

```
Saṅghaṭṭamānāni duve bhujasmiṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evaṃ dutīyena sahā mamassa, vācābhilāpo abhisajjanā vā;
```

```
Etaṃ bhayaṃ āyatiṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kāmā <pb ed="P" n="1.0010" /> hi citrā madhurā manoramā, virūparūpena mathenti cittaṃ;
```

```
Ādīnavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ītī <pb ed="T" n="1.0015" /> ca gaṇḍo ca upaddavo ca, rogo ca sallañca bhayañca metaṃ;
```

```
Etaṃ bhayaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sītañca uṇhañca khudaṃ pipāsaṃ, vātātape ḍaṃsasarīsape <note>ḍaṃsasiriṃsape (sī. syā.)</note> ca;
```

```
Sabbānipetāni abhibbhavitvā <note>abhisaṃbhavitvā (suttanipāte)</note>, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nāgova yūthāni vivajjayitvā, sañjātakhandho padumī uḷāro;
```

```
Yathābhirantaṃ viharaṃ araññe, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhānataṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0012" /> saṅgaṇikāratassa, yaṃ phassaye <note>phussaye (syā.)</note> sāmayikaṃ vimuttiṃ;
```

```
Ādiccabandhussa vaco nisamma, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘‘Diṭṭhīvisūkāni upātivatto, patto niyāmaṃ paṭiladdhamaggo;
```

```
Uppannañāṇomhi anaññaneyyo, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nillolupo <pb ed="T" n="1.0016" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0010" /> nikkuho nippipāso, nimmakkha <note>nimmakkho (syā.)</note> niddhantakasāvamoho;
```

```
Nirāsayo <note>nirāsāso (ka.)</note> sabbaloke bhavitvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pāpaṃ sahāyaṃ parivajjayetha, anatthadassiṃ visame niviṭṭhaṃ;
```

```
Sayaṃ na seve pasutaṃ pamattaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bahussutaṃ dhammadharaṃ bhajetha, mittaṃ uḷāraṃ paṭibhānavantaṃ;
```

```
Aññāya <pb ed="P" n="1.0011" /> atthāni vineyya kaṅkhaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ kāmasukhañca loke, analaṅkaritvā anapekkhamāno;
```

```
Vibhūsaṭṭhānā virato saccavādī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘‘Puttañca dāraṃ pitarañca mātaraṃ, dhanāni dhaññāni ca bandhavāni;
```

```
Hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṅgo <pb ed="T" n="1.0017" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0013" /> eso parittamettha sokhyaṃ, appassādo dukkhamevettha bhiyyo;
```

```
Gaḷo <note>gāho (sī.) kaṇḍo (syā.) gāḷho (ka.)</note> eso iti ñatvā matimā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sandālayitvāna saṃyojanāni, jālaṃva bhetvā salilambucārī;
```

```
Aggīva daḍḍhaṃ anivattamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘‘Okkhittacakkhū na ca pādalolo, guttindriyo rakkhitamānasāno;
```

```
Anavassuto apariḍayhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ohārayitvā gihibyañjanāni, sañchannapatto yathā pārichatto;
```

```
Kāsāyavattho abhinikkhamitvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rasesu gedhaṃ akaraṃ alolo, anaññaposī sapadānacārī;
```

```
Kule kule appaṭibaddhacitto, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pahāya <pb ed="T" n="1.0018" /> pañcāvaraṇāni cetaso, upakkilese byapanujja sabbe;
```

```
Anissito chejja sinehadosaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vipiṭṭhikatvāna <pb ed="P" n="1.0012" /> sukhañca dukkhaṃ, pubbeva somanassadomanassaṃ;
```

```
Laddhānupekkhaṃ samathaṃ visuddhaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āraddhavīriyo <pb ed="M" n="1.0014" /> paramatthapattiyā, alīnacitto akusītavutti;
```

```
Daḷhanikkamo thāmabalūpapanno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisallānaṃ jhānamariñcamāno, dhammesu niccaṃ anudhammacārī;
```

```
Ādīnavaṃ sammasitā bhavesu, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘‘Taṇhakkhayaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0011" /> patthayamappamatto, aneḷamūgo sutavā satīmā;
```

```
Saṅkhātadhammo niyato padhānavā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sīhova <pb ed="T" n="1.0019" /> saddesu asantasanto, vātova jālamhi asajjamāno;
```

```
Padumaṃva toyena alimpamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sīho yathā dāṭhabalī pasayha, rājā migānaṃ abhibhuyya cārī;
```

```
Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mettaṃ upekkhaṃ karuṇaṃ vimuttiṃ, āsevamāno muditañca kāle;
```

```
Sabbena lokena avirujjhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṃ, sandālayitvāna saṃyojanāni;
```

```
Asantasaṃ jīvitasaṅkhayamhi, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhajanti <pb ed="M" n="1.0015" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0013" /> sevanti ca kāraṇatthā, nikkāraṇā dullabhā ajja mittā;
```

```
Attatthapaññā asucīmanussā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘‘Visuddhasīlā <pb ed="T" n="1.0020" /> suvisuddhapaññā, samāhitā jāgariyānuyuttā;
```

```
Vipassakā dhammavisesadassī, maggaṅgabojjhaṅgagate vijaññā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘‘Suññappaṇidhiñca tathānimittaṃ <note>suññatappaṇīhitañcānimittaṃ (sī.)</note>, āsevayitvā jinasāsanamhi;
```

```
Ye sāvakattaṃ na vajanti dhīrā, bhavanti paccekajinā sayambhū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahantadhammā bahudhammakāyā, cittissarā sabbadukkhoghatiṇṇā;
```

```
Udaggacittā paramatthadassī, sīhopamā khaggavisāṇakappā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘‘Santindriyā santamanā samādhī, paccantasattesu patippacārā <note>paccattagambhīramatappacārā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Dīpā parattha idha vijjalantā, paccekabuddhā satataṃ hitāme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pahīnasabbāvaraṇā janindā, lokappadīpā ghanakañcanābhā;
```

```
Nissaṃsayaṃ lokasudakkhiṇeyyā, paccekabuddhā satatappitāme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paccekabuddhānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0021" /> subhāsitāni, caranti lokamhi sadevakamhi;
```

```
Sutvā tathā ye na karonti bālā, caranti dukkhesu punappunaṃ te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paccekabuddhānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0016" /> subhāsitāni, madhuṃ yathā khuddamavassavantaṃ;
```

```
Sutvā tathā ye paṭipattiyuttā, bhavanti te saccadasā sapaññā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Paccekabuddhehi <pb ed="P" n="1.0014" /> jinehi bhāsitā, kathā <note>gāthā (sī. syā.)</note> uḷārā abhinikkhamitvā;
```

```
Tā sakyasīhena naruttamena, pakāsitā dhammavijānanatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Lokānukampāya <pb ed="V" n="1.0012" /> imāni tesaṃ, paccekabuddhāna vikubbitāni;
```

```
Saṃvegasaṅgamativaḍḍhanatthaṃ, sayambhusīhena pakāsitānī’’ti.
```

Paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃ.

#### 3-1. Sāriputtattheraapadānaṃ

Atha therāpadānaṃ suṇātha –

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0022" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0015" /> avidūre, lambako nāma pabbato;
```

```
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Uttānakūlā nadikā, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Susuddhapuḷinākiṇṇā, avidūre mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Asakkharā apabbhārā, sādu appaṭigandhikā;
```

```
Sandatī nadikā tattha, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhīlā makarā cettha, susumārā <note>suṃsumārā (sī. syā. )</note> ca kacchapā;
```

```
Caranti nadiyā tattha, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā <note>vajalā (sī. syā.) jalajā (pī.)</note> muñjarohitā;
```

```
Vaggaḷā <note>vaggulā (sī.) vagguḷā (syā.) maggurā (theragāthā)</note> papatāyantā, sobhayanti <note>papatāyanti, sobhayantā (ka.)</note> mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Ubho <pb ed="M" n="1.0017" /> kūlesu nadiyā, pupphino phalino dumā;
```

```
Ubhato abhilambantā, sobhayanti <note>abhilambanti sobhayantā (ka.)</note> mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Ambā sālā ca tilakā, pāṭalī sinduvārakā <note>sinduvārikā (bahūsu)</note>;
```

```
Dibbagandhā sampavanti, pupphitā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Campakā saḷalā nīpā <note>nimbā (ka.)</note>, nāgapunnāgaketakā;
```

```
Dibbagandhā sampavanti, pupphitā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Atimuttā <pb ed="T" n="1.0023" /> asokā ca, bhaginīmālā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Aṅkolā bimbijālā <note>bimbajālā (ka.)</note> ca, pupphitā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Ketakā <pb ed="P" n="1.0016" /> kandali <note>kadalī (syā.)</note> ceva, godhukā tiṇasūlikā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikārā <pb ed="V" n="1.0013" /> kaṇṇikā ca, asanā ajjunā bahū;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Punnāgā giripunnāgā, koviḷārā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhālakā ca kuṭajā, kadambā vakulā bahū;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Āḷakā isimuggā ca, kadalimātuluṅgiyo;
```

```
Gandhodakena saṃvaḍḍhā, phalāni dhārayanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Aññe pupphanti padumā, aññe jāyanti kesarī;
```

```
Aññe opupphā padumā, pupphitā taḷāke tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā, niddhāvanti mulāḷiyo;
```

```
Siṃghāṭipattamākiṇṇā, sobhanti taḷāke tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Nayitā ambagandhī ca, uttalī bandhujīvakā;
```

```
Dibbagandhā sampavanti, pupphitā taḷāke tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
```

```
Saṃgulā maggurā <note>maṅgurā (sī. ka.)</note> ceva, vasanti taḷāke tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhīlā <pb ed="T" n="1.0024" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0018" /> susumārā ca, tantigāhā ca rakkhasā;
```

```
Oguhā <note>ogāhā (syā.)</note> ajagarā ca, vasanti taḷāke tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Pārevatā ravihaṃsā, cakkavākā nadīcarā;
```

```
Kokilā sukasāḷikā, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Kukkutthakā kuḷīrakā, vane pokkharasātakā;
```

```
Dindibhā suvapotā ca, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Haṃsā <pb ed="P" n="1.0017" /> koñcā mayūrā ca, kokilā tambacūḷakā <note>tambacūḷikā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Pampakā jīvaṃjīvā ca, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Kosikā poṭṭhasīsā ca, kurarā senakā bahū;
```

```
Mahākāḷā ca sakuṇā, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Pasadā ca varāhā ca, camarā gaṇḍakā bahū <note>vakā bheraṇḍakā bahū (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Rohiccā sukapotā <note>suttapotā (syā.)</note> ca, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhabyagghā <pb ed="V" n="1.0014" /> ca dīpī ca, acchakokataracchakā;
```

```
Tidhā pabhinnamātaṅgā, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Kinnarā vānarā ceva, athopi vanakammikā;
```

```
Cetā ca luddakā ceva, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Tindukāni piyālāni, madhukā kāsumārayo <note>kāsamāriyo (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti, avidūre mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Kosambā <note>kosumbhā (sī. syā.)</note> saḷalā nimbā <note>saḷalā nīpā (sī. syā.) panasā ambā (?)</note>, sāduphalasamāyutā;
```

```
Dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti, avidūre mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Harītakā <pb ed="T" n="1.0025" /> āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā;
```

```
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phalāni dhārayanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Āluvā ca kaḷambā ca, biḷālītakkaḷāni ca;
```

```
Jīvakā sutakā ceva, bahukā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Assamassāvidūramhi, taḷākāsuṃ sunimmitā;
```

```
Acchodakā sītajalā, supatitthā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuppalasañchannā<pb ed="M" n="1.0019" />, puṇḍarīkasamāyutā;
```

```
Mandālakehi sañchannā, dibbagandho pavāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampanne, pupphite phalite vane;
```

```
Sukate assame ramme, viharāmi ahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlavā vatasampanno <note>vattasampanno (syā.)</note>, jhāyī jhānarato sadā;
```

```
Pañcābhiññābalappatto, suruci nāma tāpaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Catuvīsasahassāni, sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahu;
```

```
Sabbeva brāhmaṇā ete, jātimanto yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, sanighaṇṭusakeṭubhe;
```

```
Padakā veyyākaraṇā, sadhamme pāramiṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Uppātesu <pb ed="P" n="1.0018" /> nimittesu, lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā;
```

```
Pathabyā bhūmantalikkhe, mama sissā susikkhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Appicchā nipakā ete, appāhārā alolupā;
```

```
Lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyī <pb ed="T" n="1.0026" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0015" /> jhānaratā dhīrā, santacittā samāhitā;
```

```
Ākiñcaññaṃ patthayantā, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Abhiññāpāramippattā, pettike gocare ratā;
```

```
Antalikkhacarā dhīrā, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃvutā chasu dvāresu, anejā rakkhitindriyā;
```

```
Asaṃsaṭṭhā ca te dhīrā, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Pallaṅkena nisajjāya, ṭhānacaṅkamanena ca;
```

```
Vītināmenti te rattiṃ, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Rajanīye na rajjanti, dussanīye na dussare;
```

```
Mohanīye na muyhanti, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhiṃ vīmaṃsamānā te, vattanti niccakālikaṃ;
```

```
Pathaviṃ <note>paṭhaviṃ (sī. syā.)</note> te pakampenti, sārambhena durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Kīḷamānā ca te sissā, kīḷanti jhānakīḷitaṃ;
```

```
Jambuto phalamānenti, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Aññe <pb ed="M" n="1.0020" /> gacchanti goyānaṃ, aññe pubbavidehakaṃ <note>pubbavidehanaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Aññe ca uttarakuruṃ, esanāya durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Purato pesenti khāriṃ, pacchato ca vajanti te;
```

```
Catuvīsasahassehi, chāditaṃ hoti ambaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Aggipākī anaggī ca, dantodukkhalikāpi ca;
```

```
Asmena koṭṭitā keci, pavattaphalabhojanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Udakorohaṇā <pb ed="T" n="1.0027" /> keci, sāyaṃ pāto sucīratā;
```

```
Toyābhisecanakarā, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā, paṅkadantā rajassirā;
```

```
Gandhitā sīlagandhena, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘Pātova <pb ed="P" n="1.0019" /> sannipatitvā, jaṭilā uggatāpanā;
```

```
Lābhālābhaṃ pakittetvā, gacchanti ambare tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Etesaṃ pakkamantānaṃ, mahāsaddo pavattati;
```

```
Ajinacammasaddena, muditā honti devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Disodisaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0016" /> pakkamanti, antalikkhacarā isī;
```

```
Sake balenupatthaddhā, te gacchanti yadicchakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Pathavīkampakā ete, sabbeva nabhacārino;
```

```
Uggatejā duppasahā, sāgarova akhobhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Ṭhānacaṅkamino keci, keci nesajjikā isī;
```

```
Pavattabhojanā keci, mama sissā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Mettāvihārino ete, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Anattukkaṃsakā sabbe, na te vambhenti kassaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Sīharājāvasambhītā, gajarājāva thāmavā;
```

```
Durāsadā byagghāriva, āgacchanti mamantike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Vijjādharā devatā ca, nāgagandhabbarakkhasā;
```

```
Kumbhaṇḍā dānavā garuḷā, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Te <pb ed="T" n="1.0028" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0021" /> jaṭākhāribharitā, ajinuttaravāsanā;
```

```
Antalikkhacarā sabbe, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘Sadānucchavikā <note>tadānucchavikā (syā. ka.)</note> ete, aññamaññaṃ sagāravā;
```

```
Catubbīsasahassānaṃ, khipitasaddo na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘Pāde pādaṃ nikkhipantā, appasaddā susaṃvutā;
```

```
Upasaṅkamma sabbeva <note>sabbe te (syā.)</note>, sirasā vandare mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi sissehi parivuto, santehi ca tapassibhi;
```

```
Vasāmi assame tattha, jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘Isīnaṃ sīlagandhena, pupphagandhena cūbhayaṃ;
```

```
Phalīnaṃ phalagandhena, gandhito hoti assamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi, arati me na vijjati;
```

```
Sake sisse ovadanto, bhiyyo hāsaṃ labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphānaṃ pupphamānānaṃ, phalānañca vipaccataṃ;
```

```
Dibbagandhā pavāyanti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhimhā <pb ed="P" n="1.0020" /> vuṭṭhahitvā, ātāpī nipako ahaṃ;
```

```
Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, vanaṃ ajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘Uppāte <pb ed="V" n="1.0017" /> supine cāpi, lakkhaṇesu susikkhito;
```

```
Pavattamānaṃ <note>vattamānaṃ (ka.)</note> mantapadaṃ, dhārayāmi ahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, himavantamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā <pb ed="T" n="1.0029" /> himavantaṃ, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘Tamaddasāhaṃ sambuddhaṃ, sappabhāsaṃ manoramaṃ;
```

```
Indīvaraṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘Jalantaṃ dīparukkhaṃva, vijjutaṃ gagaṇe yathā;
```

```
Suphullaṃ sālarājaṃva, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0022" /> nāgo mahāvīro, dukkhassantakaro muni;
```

```
Imaṃ dassanamāgamma, sabbadukkhā pamuccare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Disvānāhaṃ devadevaṃ, lakkhaṇaṃ upadhārayiṃ;
```

```
Buddho nu kho na vā buddho, handa passāmi cakkhumaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassārāni cakkāni, dissanti caraṇuttame;
```

```
Lakkhaṇānissa disvāna, niṭṭhaṃ gacchiṃ tathāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna, sammajjitvānahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Atha pupphe samānetvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjayitvāna taṃ buddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, namassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘Yena ñāṇena sambuddho, viharati <note>viharittha (sī.), vihareti (ka.)</note> anāsavo;
```

```
Taṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘‘Samuddharasimaṃ <note>samuddharayimaṃ (syā.)</note> lokaṃ, sayambhū amitodaya;
```

```
Tava dassanamāgamma, kaṅkhāsotaṃ taranti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tuvaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0030" /> satthā ca ketu ca, dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Parāyaṇo <note>parāyano (syā. ka.)</note> patiṭṭhā ca, dīpo ca dvipaduttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sakkā samudde udakaṃ, pametuṃ āḷhakena vā;
```

```
Na tveva tava sabbaññu, ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhāretuṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0018" /> pathaviṃ sakkā, ṭhapetvā tulamaṇḍale;
```

```
Na tveva tava sabbaññu, ñāṇaṃ sakkā dharetave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ākāso <pb ed="P" n="1.0021" /> minituṃ sakkā, rajjuyā aṅgulena vā;
```

```
Na tveva tava sabbaññu, ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāsamudde udakaṃ, pathavī cākhilā jaṭaṃ <note>pathaviṃ cākhilañjahe (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Buddhañāṇaṃ upādāya, upamāto na yujjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, cittaṃ yesaṃ pavattati;
```

```
Antojālīkatā <note>antojālagatā (pī.)</note> ete, tava ñāṇamhi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yena <pb ed="M" n="1.0023" /> ñāṇena pattosi, kevalaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tena ñāṇena sabbaññu, maddasī paratitthiye’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Imā gāthā thavitvāna, suruci nāma tāpaso;
```

```
Ajinaṃ pattharitvāna, pathaviyaṃ nisīdi so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, ajjhogāḷho mahaṇṇave;
```

```
Accugato tāvadeva, girirājā pavuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘Tāva accuggato neru, āyato vitthato ca so;
```

```
Cuṇṇito aṇubhedena, koṭisatasahassaso <note>sahassiyo (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Lakkhe <pb ed="T" n="1.0031" /> ṭhapiyamānamhi, parikkhayamagacchatha;
```

```
Na tveva tava sabbaññu, ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhumacchikena jālena, udakaṃ yo parikkhipe;
```

```
Ye keci udake pāṇā, antojālīkatā siyuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva hi mahāvīra, ye keci puthutitthiyā;
```

```
Diṭṭhigahanapakkhandā <note>pakkhantā (sī. syā.)</note>, parāmāsena mohitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Tava suddhena ñāṇena, anāvaraṇadassinā;
```

```
Antojālīkatā ete, ñāṇaṃ te nātivattare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, anomadassī mahāyaso;
```

```
Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā, disaṃ olokayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassimunino, nisabho nāma sāvako;
```

```
Parivuto satasahassehi, santacittehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāsavehi <pb ed="V" n="1.0019" /> suddhehi, chaḷabhiññehi jhāyibhi;
```

```
Cittamaññāya buddhassa, upesi lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Antalikkhe ṭhitā tattha, padakkhiṇamakaṃsu te;
```

```
Namassantā pañjalikā, otaruṃ <note>oruhuṃ (syā.)</note> buddhasantike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisiditvā, sitaṃ pātukarī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Varuṇo <pb ed="M" n="1.0024" /> nāmupaṭṭhāko, anomadassissa satthuno;

```
Ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā, apucchi lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ko <pb ed="T" n="1.0032" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0022" /> nu kho bhagavā hetu, sitakammassa satthuno;

```
Na hi buddhā ahetūhi, sitaṃ pātukaronti te’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Bhikkhumajjhe nisīditvā, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo maṃ pupphena pūjesi, ñāṇañcāpi anutthavi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇotha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, sabbe devā samāgatā;
```

```
Saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te, sambuddhamupasaṅkamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dasasu lokadhātūsu, devakāyā mahiddhikā;
```

```
Saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te, sambuddhamupasaṅkamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthī assā rathā pattī, senā ca caturaṅginī;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhitūriyasahassāni, bheriyo samalaṅkatā;

Upaṭṭhissantimaṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘‘Soḷasitthisahassāni, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī, rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sahassakkhattuṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0033" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0020" /> devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ <note>asaṅkhayaṃ (syā. ka.) evamuparipi</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pacchime bhavasampatte <note>pacchimabhave sampatte (sī.)</note>, manussattaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Brāhmaṇī sāriyā nāma, dhārayissati kucchinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mātuyā <pb ed="M" n="1.0025" /> nāmagottena, paññāyissatiyaṃ naro;
```

```
Sāriputtoti nāmena, tikkhapañño bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘‘Asītikoṭī chaḍḍetvā, pabbajissatikiñcano;
```

```
Gavesanto santipadaṃ, carissati mahiṃ imaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘‘Apparimeyye ito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sāriputtoti nāmena, hessati aggasāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ayaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0023" /> bhāgīrathī <note>bhāgīrasī (syā. ka.)</note> gaṅgā, himavantā pabhāvitā;
```

```
Mahāsamuddamappeti, tappayantī mahodadhiṃ <note>mahodadhī (?) gaṅgādimahānadiyoti attho</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tathevāyaṃ sāriputto, sake tīsu visārado;
```

```
Paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā, tappayissati pāṇine <note>pāṇino (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘‘Himavantamupādāya, sāgarañca mahodadhiṃ;
```

```
Etthantare yaṃ pulinaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tampi sakkā asesena, saṅkhātuṃ gaṇanā yathā;
```

```
Na tveva sāriputtassa, paññāyanto bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘‘Lakkhe <pb ed="T" n="1.0034" /> ṭhapiyamānamhi, khīye gaṅgāya vālukā;
```

```
Na tveva sāriputtassa, paññāyanto bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāsamudde ūmiyo, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyā;
```

```
Tatheva sāriputtassa, paññāyanto na hessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā, hessati aggasāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ, sakyaputtena tādinā;
```

```
Anuvattessati sammā, vassento dhammavuṭṭhiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbametaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0021" /> abhiññāya, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘Aho <pb ed="M" n="1.0026" /> me sukataṃ kammaṃ, anomadassissa satthuno;
```

```
Yassāhaṃ kāraṃ <note>yassādhikāraṃ (syā.)</note> katvāna, sabbattha pāramiṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
```

```
Sumutto saravegova, kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto, nibbānaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Vicinaṃ titthiye sabbe, esāhaṃ saṃsariṃ bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi byādhito poso, pariyeseyya osadhaṃ;
```

```
Vicineyya vanaṃ <note>dhanaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> sabbaṃ, byādhito parimuttiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto, nibbānaṃ amataṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Abbokiṇṇaṃ <note>abbocchinnaṃ (aṭṭha.)</note> pañcasataṃ, pabbajiṃ isipabbajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṭābhārena <pb ed="T" n="1.0035" /> bharito, ajinuttaranivāsano;
```

```
Abhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā, brahmalokaṃ agacchihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘Natthi <pb ed="P" n="1.0024" /> bāhirake suddhi, ṭhapetvā jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ye keci buddhimā sattā, sujjhanti jinasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘Attakāramayaṃ <note>atthakāramayaṃ (ka.)</note> etaṃ, nayidaṃ itihītihaṃ;
```

```
Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto, kutitthe <note>kutitthaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> sañcariṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā sāratthiko poso, kadaliṃ chetvāna phālaye;
```

```
Na tattha sāraṃ vindeyya, sārena rittako hi so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva titthiyā loke, nānādiṭṭhī bahujjanā;
```

```
Asaṅkhatena rittāse, sārena kadalī yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhavasampatte, brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Mahābhogaṃ chaḍḍetvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

Paṭhamabhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Brāhmaṇo sañcayo <note>sañjayo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nāma, tassa mūle vasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvako <pb ed="M" n="1.0027" /> te mahāvīra, assaji nāma brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Durāsado uggatejo, piṇḍāya caratī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Tamaddasāsiṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0022" /> sappaññaṃ, muniṃ mone samāhitaṃ;
```

```
Santacittaṃ mahānāgaṃ, suphullaṃ padumaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā <pb ed="T" n="1.0036" /> me cittamuppajji, sudantaṃ suddhamānasaṃ;
```

```
Usabhaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ, arahāyaṃ bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Pāsādiko iriyati, abhirūpo susaṃvuto;
```

```
Uttame damathe danto, amatadassī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃnūnāhaṃ uttamatthaṃ, puccheyyaṃ tuṭṭhamānasaṃ;
```

```
So me puṭṭho kathessati, paṭipucchāmahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍapātaṃ <note>piṇḍacāraṃ (syā.)</note> carantassa, pacchato agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Okāsaṃ paṭimānento, pucchituṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Vīthintare anuppattaṃ, upagantvāna pucchahaṃ;
```

```
‘Kathaṃ gottosi tvaṃ vīra, kassa sissosi mārisa’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘So me puṭṭho viyākāsi, asambhītova kesarī;
```

```
‘Buddho loke samuppanno, tassa sissomhi āvuso’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kīdisaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0025" /> te mahāvīra, anujāta mahāyasa;
```

```
Buddhassa sāsanaṃ dhammaṃ, sādhu me kathayassu bho’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘So me puṭṭho kathī sabbaṃ, gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Taṇhāsallassa hantāraṃ, sabbadukkhāpanūdanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ye dhammā hetuppabhavā, tesaṃ hetuṃ tathāgato āha;
```

```
Tesañca yo nirodho, evaṃ vādī mahāsamaṇo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ vissajjite pañhe, paṭhamaṃ phalamajjhagaṃ;
```

```
Virajo vimalo āsiṃ, sutvāna jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvāna <pb ed="T" n="1.0037" /> munino vākyaṃ, passitvā dhammamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Pariyogāḷhasaddhammo, imaṃ gāthamabhāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘‘Eseva <pb ed="M" n="1.0028" /> dhammo yadi tāvadeva, paccabyathapadamasokaṃ;
```

```
Adiṭṭhaṃ abbhatītaṃ, bahukehi kappanahutehi’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Svāhaṃ dhammaṃ gavesanto, kutitthe sañcariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, kālo me nappamajjituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Tositohaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0023" /> assajinā, patvāna acalaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Sahāyakaṃ gavesanto, assamaṃ agamāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Dūratova mamaṃ disvā, sahāyo me susikkhito;
```

```
Iriyāpathasampanno <note>iriyāpathaṃ mamaṃ disvā (ka.)</note>, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pasannamukhanettosi, munibhāvova dissati;
```

```
Amatādhigato kacci, nibbānamaccutaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘‘Subhānurūpo āyāsi, āneñjakārito viya;
```

```
Dantova dantadamatho <note>dantovuttamadamatho (sī.) dantova danta damathe (syā.)</note>, upasantosi brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘‘Amataṃ mayādhigataṃ, sokasallāpanūdanaṃ;
```

```
Tvampi taṃ adhigacchesi <note>adhigacchāhi (sī.), adhigacchehi (syā.), adhigatosi (?)</note>, gacchāma buddhasantikaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhūti so paṭissutvā, sahāyo me susikkhito;
```

```
Hatthena hatthaṃ gaṇhitvā, upagamma <note>upāgami (sī.), upāgamma (syā.)</note> tavantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Ubhopi pabbajissāma, sakyaputta tavantike;
```

```
Tava sāsanamāgamma, viharāma anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Kolito <pb ed="T" n="1.0038" /> iddhiyā seṭṭho, ahaṃ paññāya pārago;
```

```
Ubhova ekato hutvā, sāsanaṃ sobhayāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Apariyositasaṅkappo<pb ed="P" n="1.0026" />, kutitthe sañcariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tava dassanamāgamma, saṅkappo pūrito mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Pathaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya, pupphanti samaye dumā;
```

```
Dibbagandhā sampavanti, tosenti sabbapāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Tathevāhaṃ mahāvīra, sakyaputta mahāyasa;
```

```
Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya, samayesāmi pupphituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Vimuttipupphaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0029" /> esanto, bhavasaṃsāramocanaṃ;
```

```
Vimuttipupphalābhena, tosemi sabbapāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi, ṭhapetvāna mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Paññāya sadiso natthi, tava puttassa cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Suvinītā ca te sissā, parisā ca susikkhitā;
```

```
Uttame damathe dantā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyī <pb ed="V" n="1.0024" /> jhānaratā dhīrā, santacittā samāhitā;
```

```
Munī moneyyasampannā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Appicchā nipakā dhīrā, appāhārā alolupā;
```

```
Lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Āraññikā dhutaratā, jhāyino lūkhacīvarā;
```

```
Vivekābhiratā dhīrā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭipannā <pb ed="T" n="1.0039" /> phalaṭṭhā ca, sekhā phalasamaṅgino;
```

```
Āsīsakā <note>āsiṃsakā (sī. syā.)</note> uttamatthaṃ, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘Sotāpannā ca vimalā, sakadāgāmino ca ye;
```

```
Anāgāmī ca arahā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Satipaṭṭhānakusalā, bojjhaṅgabhāvanāratā;
```

```
Sāvakā te bahū sabbe, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhipādesu kusalā, samādhibhāvanāratā;
```

```
Sammappadhānānuyuttā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatā;
```

```
Paññāya pāramiṃ pattā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Edisā te mahāvīra, tava sissā susikkhitā;
```

```
Durāsadā uggatejā, parivārenti taṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi sissehi parivuto, saññatehi tapassibhi;
```

```
Migarājāvasambhīto, uḷurājāva sobhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘Pathaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya, ruhanti dharaṇīruhā;
```

```
Vepullataṃ pāpuṇanti, phalañca dassayanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘Pathavīsadiso <pb ed="M" n="1.0030" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0027" /> tvaṃsi, sakyaputta mahāyasa;
```

```
Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya, labhanti amataṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘Sindhu sarassatī ceva, nadiyo candabhāgikā;
```

```
Gaṅgā ca yamunā ceva, sarabhū ca atho mahī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘Etāsaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0040" /> sandamānānaṃ, sāgaro sampaṭicchati;
```

```
Jahanti purimaṃ nāmaṃ, sāgaroteva ñāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Tathevime <pb ed="V" n="1.0025" /> catubbaṇṇā, pabbajitvā tavantike;
```

```
Jahanti purimaṃ nāmaṃ, buddhaputtāti ñāyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi cando vimalo, gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyā;
```

```
Sabbe tāragaṇe loke, ābhāya atirocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra, parivuto devamānuse;
```

```
Ete sabbe atikkamma, jalasi sabbadā tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘Gambhīre uṭṭhitā ūmī, na velamativattare;
```

```
Sabbā velaṃva phusanti <note>sabbāva velaṃ phusanti (sī.), sabbā velaṃ paphussanti (syā.)</note>, sañcuṇṇā vikiranti tā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva titthiyā loke, nānādiṭṭhī bahujjanā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ vāditukāmā te, nātivattanti taṃ muniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘Sace ca taṃ pāpuṇanti, paṭivādehi cakkhuma;
```

```
Tavantikaṃ upāgantvā, sañcuṇṇāva bhavanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi udake jātā, kumudā mandālakā bahū;
```

```
Upalimpanti <note>upalippanti (?)</note> toyena, kaddamakalalena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva bahukā sattā, loke jātā virūhare;
```

```
Aṭṭitā rāgadosena, kaddame kumudaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi padumaṃ jalajaṃ, jalamajjhe virūhati;
```

```
Na so limpati toyena, parisuddho hi kesarī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva <pb ed="T" n="1.0041" /> tvaṃ mahāvīra, loke jāto mahāmuni;
```

```
Nopalimpasi lokena, toyena padumaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi rammake māse, bahū pupphanti vārijā;
```

```
Nātikkamanti taṃ māsaṃ, samayo pupphanāya so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva <pb ed="M" n="1.0031" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0026" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0028" /> tvaṃ mahāvīra, pupphito te vimuttiyā;
```

```
Sāsanaṃ nātivattanti, padumaṃ vārijaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Supupphito sālarājā, dibbagandhaṃ pavāyati;
```

```
Aññasālehi parivuto, sālarājāva sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra, buddhañāṇena pupphito;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghaparivuto, sālarājāva sobhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi selo himavā, osadho sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Nāgānaṃ asurānañca, devatānañca ālayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra, osadho viya pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Anusiṭṭhā mahāvīra, tayā kāruṇikena te;
```

```
Ramanti dhammaratiyā, vasanti tava sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Migarājā yathā sīho, abhinikkhamma āsayā;
```

```
Catuddisānuviloketvā <note>viloketvā (sī. syā.), nuloketvā (ka.)</note>,
```

Tikkhattuṃ abhinādati.

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe migā uttasanti, migarājassa gajjato;
```

```
Tathā hi jātimā eso, pasū tāseti sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘Gajjato <pb ed="T" n="1.0042" /> te mahāvīra, vasudhā sampakampati;
```

```
Bodhaneyyāvabujjhanti, tasanti mārakāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘Tasanti titthiyā sabbe, nadato te mahāmuni;
```

```
Kākā senāva vibbhantā, migaraññā yathā migā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci gaṇino loke, satthāroti pavuccare;
```

```
Paramparāgataṃ dhammaṃ, desenti parisāya te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘Na hevaṃ tvaṃ mahāvīra, dhammaṃ desesi pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sāmaṃ saccāni bujjhitvā, kevalaṃ bodhipakkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘Āsayānusayaṃ ñatvā, indriyānaṃ balābalaṃ;
```

```
Bhabbābhabbe viditvāna, mahāmeghova gajjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkavāḷapariyantā<pb ed="M" n="1.0032" />, nisinnā parisā bhave;
```

```
Nānādiṭṭhī vicinantā <note>vicintenti (syā.), vicinantaṃ (ka.)</note>, vimaticchedanāya taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbesaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0029" /> cittamaññāya, opammakusalo muni;
```

```
Ekaṃ pañhaṃ kathentova, vimatiṃ chindasi <note>chindi (syā. ka.)</note> pāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘Upatissasadiseheva, vasudhā pūritā bhave;
```

```
Sabbeva te pañjalikā, kittayuṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘Kappaṃ vā te kittayantā, nānāvaṇṇehi kittayuṃ;
```

```
Parimetuṃ na sakkeyyuṃ <note>na kappeyyuṃ (syā.), na pappeyyuṃ (ka.)</note>, appameyyo tathāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāsakena <pb ed="V" n="1.0027" /> thāmena, kittito hi mayā jino;
```

```
Kappakoṭīpi kittentā, evameva pakittayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘Sace <pb ed="T" n="1.0043" /> hi koci devo vā, manusso vā susikkhito;
```

```
Pametuṃ parikappeyya, vighātaṃva labheyya so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya, sakyaputta mahāyasa;
```

```
Paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘Titthiye sampamaddāmi, vattemi jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Dhammasenāpati ajja, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
```

```
Sukhitto saravegova, kilese jhāpayī mama <note>jhāpayiṃ mama (syā.), jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘Yo koci manujo bhāraṃ, dhāreyya matthake sadā;
```

```
Bhārena dukkhito assa, bhārehi bharito tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘Ḍayhamāno tīhaggīhi, bhavesu saṃsariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Bharito bhavabhārena, giriṃ uccārito yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘Oropito ca me bhāro, bhavā ugghāṭitā mayā;
```

```
Karaṇīyaṃ kataṃ sabbaṃ, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi, ṭhapetvā sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Ahaṃ aggomhi paññāya, sadiso me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhimhi <pb ed="M" n="1.0033" /> sukusalo, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato;
```

```
Icchamāno cahaṃ ajja, sahassaṃ abhinimmine.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘Anupubbavihārassa<pb ed="P" n="1.0030" />, vasībhūto mahāmuni;
```

```
Kathesi sāsanaṃ mayhaṃ, nirodho sayanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbacakkhu <pb ed="T" n="1.0044" /> visuddhaṃ me, samādhikusalo ahaṃ;
```

```
Sammappadhānānuyutto, bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvakena hi pattabbaṃ, sabbameva kataṃ mayā;
```

```
Lokanāthaṃ ṭhapetvāna, sadiso me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘Samāpattīnaṃ kusalo <note>samāpattinayakusalo (sī.)</note>, jhānavimokkhāna khippapaṭilābhī;
```

```
Bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato, sāvakaguṇapāramigatosmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvakaguṇenapi <pb ed="V" n="1.0028" /> phussena <note>sāvakaguṇaphussena (syā.)</note>, buddhiyā parisuttamabhāravā <note>purisuttamagāravā (syā.), purisuttamabhāravā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Yaṃ saddhāsaṅgahitaṃ <note>saddhāya saṅgahitaṃ (sī.), saddāsaṅgahitaṃ (syā.)</note> cittaṃ, sadā sabrahmacārīsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhatavisova sappo, chinnavisāṇova usabho;
```

```
Nikkhittamānadappova <note>dabbova (ka.)</note>, upemi garugāravena gaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
‘‘Yadi rūpinī bhaveyya, paññā me vasumatīpi <note>vasumatī (sī. ka.) vasupatīnaṃ (syā.)</note> na sameyya;
```

```
Anomadassissa <note>anomadassi (?)</note> bhagavato, phalametaṃ ñāṇathavanāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
‘‘Pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ, sakyaputtena tādinā;
```

```
Anuvattemahaṃ sammā, ñāṇathavanāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
‘‘Mā me kadāci pāpiccho, kusīto hīnavīriyo;
```

```
Appassuto anādaro <note>anācāro (sabbattha) theragā. 987 passitabbā</note>, sameto ahu katthaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto ca medhāvī, sīlesu susamāhito;
```

```
Cetosamathānuyutto, api muddhani tiṭṭhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Appicchā hotha santuṭṭhā, jhāyī jhānaratā sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
‘‘Yamahaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0045" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0034" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0031" /> paṭhamaṃ disvā, virajo vimalo ahuṃ;
```

```
So me ācariyo dhīro, assaji nāma sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vāhasā ajja, dhammasenāpatī ahuṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha pāramiṃ patvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
‘‘Yo me ācariyo āsi, assaji nāma sāvako;
```

```
Yassaṃ disāyaṃ vasati, ussīsamhi karomahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
‘‘Mama kammaṃ saritvāna, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
<note>imā dve gāthāyo syāmapotthake na santi</note>
```

Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā.

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ <note>imā dve gāthāro syāmapotthake na santi</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0029" /> catasso <note>catasso ca (sī.)</note>, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāriputto thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sāriputtattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 3-2. Mahāmoggallānattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Vihāsi himavantamhi, devasaṅghapurakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
‘‘Varuṇo nāma nāmena, nāgarājā ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Kāmarūpī vikubbāmi, mahodadhinivāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅgaṇiyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0046" /> gaṇaṃ hitvā, tūriyaṃ paṭṭhapesahaṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā, vādesuṃ accharā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
‘‘Vajjamānesu <pb ed="M" n="1.0035" /> tūresu, devā tūrāni <note>turiyesu, devā turiyāni (sī. syā.)</note> vajjayuṃ;
```

```
Ubhinnaṃ saddaṃ sutvāna, buddhopi sampabujjhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§379.</p>

```
‘‘Nimantetvāna sambuddhaṃ, sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ;
```

```
Āsanaṃ paññapetvāna, kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§380.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāsavasahassehi, parivuto lokanāyako;
```

```
Obhāsento disā sabbā, bhavanaṃ me upāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§381.</p>

```
‘‘Upaviṭṭhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0032" /> mahāvīraṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Sabhikkhusaṅghaṃ tappesiṃ <note>santappesiṃ (syā.), tappemi (ka.)</note>, annapānenahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§382.</p>

```
‘‘Anumodi mahāvīro, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§383.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo so <note>yaṃ so (ka.)</note> saṅghaṃ apūjesi, buddhañca lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tena cittappasādena, devalokaṃ gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§384.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattasattatikkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ aṭṭhasataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§385.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Bhogā asaṅkhiyā tassa, uppajjissanti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§386.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aparimeyye <pb ed="V" n="1.0030" /> ito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena <note>nāmena (sī.)</note>, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§387.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nirayā <pb ed="T" n="1.0047" /> so cavitvāna, manussataṃ gamissati;
```

```
Kolito nāma nāmena, brahmabandhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§388.</p>

```
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, kusalamūlena codito;
```

```
Gotamassa bhagavato, dutiyo hessati sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§389.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§390.</p>

```
‘‘Pāpamittopanissāya, kāmarāgavasaṃ gato;
```

```
Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, ghātayiṃ duṭṭhamānaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§391.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0036" /> yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, nirayaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Pāpakammasamaṅgitā, bhinnasīso marāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§392.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Idhāpi ediso mayhaṃ, maraṇakāle bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§393.</p>

```
‘‘Pavivekamanuyutto, samādhibhāvanārato;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§394.</p>

```
‘‘Dharaṇimpi sugambhīraṃ, bahalaṃ duppadhaṃsiyaṃ;
```

```
Vāmaṅguṭṭhena khobheyyaṃ, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§395.</p>

```
‘‘Asmimānaṃ na passāmi, māno mayhaṃ na vijjati;
```

```
Sāmaṇere upādāya, garucittaṃ karomahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§396.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, yaṃ kammamabhinīhariṃ;
```

```
Tāhaṃ bhūmimanuppatto, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§397.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0048" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0033" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāmoggallāno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mahāmoggallānattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3-3. Mahākassapattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§398.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0031" /> bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Nibbute lokanāthamhi, pūjaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§399.</p>

```
‘‘Udaggacittā janatā, āmoditapamoditā;
```

```
Tesu saṃvegajātesu, pīti me udapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§400.</p>

```
‘‘Ñātimitte samānetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
```

```
Parinibbuto mahāvīro, handa pūjaṃ karomase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§401.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhūti te paṭissutvā, bhiyyo hāsaṃ janiṃsu me;
```

```
Buddhasmiṃ lokanāthamhi, kāhāma puññasañcayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§402.</p>

```
‘‘Agghiyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0037" /> sukataṃ katvā, satahatthasamuggataṃ;
```

```
Diyaḍḍhahatthapatthaṭaṃ, vimānaṃ nabhamuggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§403.</p>

```
‘‘Katvāna hammiyaṃ tattha, tālapantīhi cittitaṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, cetiyaṃ pūjayuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§404.</p>

```
‘‘Aggikkhandhova <pb ed="T" n="1.0049" /> jalito, kiṃsuko iva <note>sālarājāva (sī.)</note> phullito;
```

```
Indalaṭṭhīva ākāse, obhāseti catuddisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§405.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, katvāna kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna, tidasaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§406.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassayuttaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0034" /> hayavāhiṃ, dibbayānamadhiṭṭhito;
```

```
Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, sattabhūmaṃ samuggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§407.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārasahassāni, sabbasoṇṇamayā ahuṃ;
```

```
Jalanti sakatejena, disā sabbā pabhāsayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§408.</p>

```
‘‘Santi aññepi niyyūhā, lohitaṅgamayā tadā;
```

```
Tepi jotanti ābhāya, samantā caturo disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§409.</p>

```
‘‘Puññakammābhinibbattā, kūṭāgārā sunimmitā;
```

```
Maṇimayāpi jotanti, disā dasa <note>disodisaṃ (syā.)</note> samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§410.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ ujjotamānānaṃ, obhāso vipulo ahu;
```

```
Sabbe deve abhibhomi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§411.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi<pb ed="V" n="1.0032" />, ubbiddho nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, pathaviṃ āvasiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§412.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva bhaddake kappe, tiṃsakkhattuṃ ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Sakakammābhiraddhomhi, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§413.</p>

```
‘‘Sattaratanasampanno, catudīpamhi issaro;
```

```
Tatthāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, indalaṭṭhīva uggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§414.</p>

```
‘‘Āyāmato <pb ed="T" n="1.0050" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0038" /> catubbīsaṃ, vitthārena ca dvādasa;
```

```
Rammaṇaṃ <note>rammakaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> nāma nagaraṃ, daḷhapākāratoraṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§415.</p>

```
‘‘Āyāmato pañcasataṃ, vitthārena tadaḍḍhakaṃ;
```

```
Ākiṇṇaṃ janakāyehi, tidasānaṃ puraṃ viya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§416.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā sūcighare sūcī, pakkhittā paṇṇavīsati;
```

```
Aññamaññaṃ paghaṭṭenti, ākiṇṇaṃ hoti laṅkataṃ <note>taṃ tadā (sī.), satatā (syā.), saṅkaraṃ (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§417.</p>

```
‘‘Evampi nagaraṃ mayhaṃ, hatthissarathasaṃkulaṃ;
```

```
Manussehi sadākiṇṇaṃ, rammaṇaṃ nagaruttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§418.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, puna devattanaṃ gato <note>punapi devataṅgato (ka.)</note>.
```

```
Bhave pacchimake mayhaṃ, ahosi kulasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§419.</p>

```
‘‘Brāhmaññakulasambhūto<pb ed="P" n="1.0035" />, mahāratanasañcayo;
```

```
Asītikoṭiyo hitvā, hiraññassāpi pabbajiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§420.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākassapo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mahākassapattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 3-4. Anuruddhattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§421.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0051" /> bhagavantāhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Vūpakaṭṭhaṃ viharantaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§422.</p>

```
‘‘Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhamayācahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§423.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampa <pb ed="V" n="1.0033" /> mahāvīra, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Padīpaṃ te padassāmi, rukkhamūlamhi jhāyato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§424.</p>

```
‘‘Adhivāsesi so dhīro, sayambhū vadataṃ varo;
```

```
Dumesu vinivijjhitvā, yantaṃ yojiyahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§425.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassavaṭṭiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0039" /> pādāsiṃ, buddhassa lokabandhuno;
```

```
Sattāhaṃ pajjalitvāna, dīpā vūpasamiṃsu me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§426.</p>

```
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, vimānamupapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§427.</p>

```
‘‘Upapannassa devattaṃ, byamhaṃ āsi sunimmitaṃ;
```

```
Samantato pajjalati, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§428.</p>

```
‘‘Samantā <pb ed="P" n="1.0036" /> yojanasataṃ, virocesimahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Sabbe deve abhibhomi, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§429.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0052" /> devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Na maṃ kecītimaññanti, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§430.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Divā rattiñca passāmi, samantā yojanaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§431.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassalokaṃ ñāṇena, passāmi satthu sāsane;
```

```
Dibbacakkhumanuppatto, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§432.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, tiṃsakappasahassito;
```

```
Tassa dīpo mayā dinno, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§433.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anuruddho thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Anuruddhattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 3-5. Puṇṇamantāṇiputtattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§434.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Purakkhatomhi sissehi, upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§435.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="V" n="1.0034" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mama kammaṃ pakittesi, saṅkhittena mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§436.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0040" /> dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, abhivādetvāna satthuno;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, pakkamiṃ <note>pakkāmiṃ (sī. syā.)</note> dakkhiṇāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§437.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhittena <pb ed="T" n="1.0053" /> suṇitvāna, vitthārena abhāsayiṃ <note>adesayiṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbe sissā attamanā, sutvāna mama bhāsato;
```

```
Sakaṃ diṭṭhiṃ vinodetvā, buddhe cittaṃ pasādayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§438.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhittenapi desemi, vitthārena tathevahaṃ <note>desesiṃ vitthārenapi bhāsayiṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Abhidhammanayaññūhaṃ<pb ed="P" n="1.0037" />, kathāvatthuvisuddhiyā;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ viññāpetvāna, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§439.</p>

```
‘‘Ito pañcasate kappe, caturo suppakāsakā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, catudīpamhi issarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§440.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇo mantāṇiputto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Puṇṇamantāṇiputtattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 3-6. Upālittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§441.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, sujāto nāma brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Asītikoṭinicayo, pahūtadhanadhaññavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§442.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, sadhamme pāramiṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§443.</p>

```
‘‘Paribbājā <pb ed="T" n="1.0054" /> ekasikhā <note>ekabhikkhā (ka.)</note>, gotamā
```

Buddhasāvakā <note>sabbatthapi evameva dissati</note>.

```
Carakā tāpasā ceva, caranti mahiyā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§444.</p>

```
‘‘Tepi maṃ parivārenti, brāhmaṇo vissuto iti;
```

```
Bahujjano maṃ pūjeti, nāhaṃ pūjemi kiñcanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§445.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjārahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0041" /> na passāmi, mānatthaddho ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Buddhoti vacanaṃ natthi, tāva nuppajjate jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§446.</p>

```
‘‘Accayena <pb ed="V" n="1.0035" /> ahorattaṃ, padumuttaranāmako <note>nāyako (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā, loke uppajji cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§447.</p>

```
‘‘Vitthārike bāhujaññe, puthubhūte ca sāsane;
```

```
Upāgami tadā buddho, nagaraṃ haṃsasavhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§448.</p>

```
‘‘Pitu atthāya <pb ed="P" n="1.0038" /> so buddho, dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā;
```

```
Tena kālena parisā, samantā yojanaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§449.</p>

```
‘‘Sammato manujānaṃ so, sunando nāma tāpaso;
```

```
Yāvatā buddhaparisā, pupphehacchādayī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§450.</p>

```
‘‘Catusaccaṃ pakāsente, seṭṭhe ca <note>heṭṭhā ca (ka.)</note> pupphamaṇḍape;
```

```
Koṭisatasahassānaṃ, dhammābhisamayo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§451.</p>

```
‘‘Sattarattindivaṃ buddho, vassetvā dhammavuṭṭhiyo;
```

```
Aṭṭhame divase patte, sunandaṃ kittayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§452.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, saṃsaranto ayaṃ bhave;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ pavaro hutvā, bhavesu saṃsarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§453.</p>

```
‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi<pb ed="T" n="1.0055" />, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§454.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Mantāṇiputto puṇṇoti, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§455.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ kittayi sambuddho, sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ tadā;
```

```
Hāsayanto janaṃ sabbaṃ, dassayanto sakaṃ balaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§456.</p>

```
‘‘Katañjalī namassanti, sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ janā;
```

```
Buddhe kāraṃ karitvāna, sodhesi gatimattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§457.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me ahu saṅkappo, sutvāna munino vacaṃ;
```

```
Ahampi kāraṃ kassāmi, yathā passāmi gotamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§458.</p>

```
‘‘Evāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0042" /> cintayitvāna, kiriyaṃ cintayiṃ mama;
```

```
Kyāhaṃ kammaṃ ācarāmi, puññakkhette anuttare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§459.</p>

```
‘‘Ayañca pāṭhiko bhikkhu, sabbapāṭhissa sāsane;
```

```
Vinaye agganikkhitto, taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthaye ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§460.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0036" /> me amitaṃ bhogaṃ, akkhobhaṃ sāgarūpamaṃ;
```

```
Tena bhogena buddhassa, ārāmaṃ māpaye ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§461.</p>

```
‘‘Sobhanaṃ nāma ārāmaṃ, nagarassa puratthato;
```

```
Kiṇitvā <note>kītvā (sī.), kitvā (ka.)</note> satasahassena, saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§462.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgāre <pb ed="P" n="1.0039" /> ca pāsāde, maṇḍape hammiye guhā;
```

```
Caṅkame sukate katvā, saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§463.</p>

```
‘‘Jantāgharaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0056" /> aggisālaṃ, atho udakamāḷakaṃ;
```

```
Nhānagharaṃ māpayitvā, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§464.</p>

```
‘‘Āsandiyo pīṭhake ca, paribhoge ca bhājane;
```

```
Ārāmikañca bhesajjaṃ, sabbametaṃ adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§465.</p>

```
‘‘Ārakkhaṃ paṭṭhapetvāna, pākāraṃ kārayiṃ daḷhaṃ;
```

```
Mā naṃ koci viheṭhesi, santacittāna tādinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§466.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassenāvāsaṃ <note>āvāsaṃ satasahassena (sī.), āvāse satasahasse (syā.)</note>, saṅghārāme amāpayiṃ;
```

```
Vepullaṃ taṃ māpayitvā <note>vepullataṃ pāpayitvā (sī.)</note>, sambuddhaṃ upanāmayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§467.</p>

```
‘‘Niṭṭhāpito mayārāmo, sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muni;
```

```
Niyyādessāmi taṃ vīra <note>te vīra (sī.), taṃ dhīra (syā.)</note>, adhivāsehi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§468.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, adhivāsesi nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§469.</p>

```
‘‘Adhivāsanamaññāya, sabbaññussa mahesino;
```

```
Bhojanaṃ paṭiyādetvā, kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§470.</p>

```
‘‘Ārocitamhi kālamhi, padumuttaranāyako;
```

```
Khīṇāsavasahassehi, ārāmaṃ me upāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§471.</p>

```
‘‘Nisinnaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0043" /> kālamaññāya, annapānena tappayiṃ;
```

```
Bhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§472.</p>

```
‘‘Kīto satasahassena, tattakeneva kārito;
```

```
Sobhano nāma ārāmo, sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§473.</p>

```
‘‘Iminārāmadānena<pb ed="T" n="1.0057" />, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Bhave nibbattamānohaṃ, labhāmi mama patthitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§474.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0037" /> sambuddho, saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§475.</p>

```
‘‘Yo so buddhassa pādāsi, saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§476.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthī <pb ed="P" n="1.0040" /> assā rathā pattī, senā ca caturaṅginī;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§477.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi tūrasahassāni <note>turiyasahassāni (sī. syā.)</note>, bheriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§478.</p>

```
‘‘Chaḷasītisahassāni, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§479.</p>

```
‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§480.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§481.</p>

```
‘‘Devarājena pattabbaṃ, sabbaṃ paṭilabhissati;
```

```
Anūnabhogo hutvāna, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§482.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī, rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§483.</p>

```
‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi<pb ed="T" n="1.0058" />, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§484.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0044" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Upāli nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§485.</p>

```
‘‘Vinaye pāramiṃ patvā, ṭhānāṭhāne ca kovido;
```

```
Jinasāsanaṃ dhārento, viharissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§486.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§487.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyyupādāya, patthemi tava sāsanaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§488.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="V" n="1.0038" /> sūlāvuto poso, rājadaṇḍena tajjito;
```

```
Sūle sātaṃ avindanto, parimuttiṃva icchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§489.</p>

```
‘‘Tathevāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0059" /> mahāvīra, bhavadaṇḍena tajjito;
```

```
Kammasūlāvuto santo, pipāsāvedanaṭṭito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§490.</p>

```
‘‘Bhave sātaṃ na vindāmi, ḍayhanto tīhi aggibhi;
```

```
Parimuttiṃ gavesāmi, yathāpi rājadaṇḍito.
```
