<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Mama uggajjanaṃ sutvā, abhirūhi mahāmuni;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, tāresiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Nadiyā <pb ed="T" n="1.0114" /> pārime tīre, siddhattho lokanāyako;
```

```
Assāsesi mamaṃ tattha, amataṃ pāpuṇissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Tamhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0078" /> kāyā cavitvāna, devalokaṃ āgacchahaṃ;
```

```
Dibbasukhaṃ anubhaviṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Sattakkhattuñca <pb ed="M" n="1.0089" /> devindo, devarajjamakāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tīṇikkhattuṃ cakkavattī, mahiyā issaro ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Vivekamanuyuttohaṃ<pb ed="P" n="1.0080" />, nipako ca susaṃvuto;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, tāresiṃ yaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, taraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttiyo <note>uttiriyo (sī.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Uttiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Ekañjalikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe;
```

```
Vipassiṃ satthavāhaggaṃ, naravaraṃ vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Adantadamanaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0115" /> tādiṃ, mahāvādiṃ mahāmatiṃ;
```

```
Disvā pasanno sumano, ekañjalimakāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yamañjaliṃ kariṃ <note>yaṃ añjalimakariṃ (syā.), añjalimakariṃ (ka.)</note> tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, añjalissa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekañjaliko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekañjalikattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Khomadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="M" n="1.0090" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0079" /> bandhumatiyā, ahosiṃ vāṇijo tadā;
```

```
Teneva dāraṃ posemi, ropemi bījasampadaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Rathiyaṃ paṭipannassa, vipassissa mahesino;
```

```
Ekaṃ khomaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, kusalatthāya satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="P" n="1.0081" /> kappe, yaṃ khomamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, khomadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Sattarase <note>sattavīse (sī. syā.)</note> ito kappe, eko sindhavasandhano;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, catudīpamhi issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0116" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khomadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Khomadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Susūti upavāno ca, saraṇo sīlagāhako;
```

```
Annasaṃsāvako khomadāyī ca, daseva tatiye gaṇe;
```

```
Añjalī khomadāyī ca, daseva tatiye gaṇe;
```

```
Pañcālīsītisataṃ vuttā, gāthāyo sabbapiṇḍitā.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Subhūtivaggo tatiyo.</trailer>

Catutthabhāṇavāraṃ.

### 4. Kuṇḍadhānavaggo

#### 1. Kuṇḍadhānattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Sattāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0091" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0080" /> paṭisallīnaṃ, sayambhuṃ aggapuggalaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Vuṭṭhitaṃ kālamaññāya, padumuttaraṃ mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Mahantiṃ kadalīkaṇṇiṃ, gahetvā upagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā <pb ed="T" n="1.0117" /> <note>paṭiggahesi (syā. ka.)</note> bhagavā, sabbaññū <note>taṃ phalaṃ (sī.)</note> lokanāyako;
```

```
Mama cittaṃ pasādento, paribhuñji mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Paribhuñjitvā sambuddho, satthavāho anuttaro;
```

```
Sakāsane nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="1.0082" /> ca santi samitāro <note>ye vasanti sametāro (sī.)</note>, yakkhā imamhi pabbate;
```

```
Araññe bhūtabhabyāni <note>bhūtagaṇā sabbe (syā.)</note>, suṇantu vacanaṃ mama’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Yo so buddhaṃ upaṭṭhāsi, migarājaṃva kesariṃ <note>migarājāva kesarī (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ekādasañcakkhattuṃ, so <note>soyamekādasakkhattuṃ (sī.)</note> devarājā bhavissati;
```

```
Catutiṃsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘‘Akkositvāna samaṇe, sīlavante anāsave;
```

```
Pāpakammavipākena, nāmadheyyaṃ labhissati <note>bhavissati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Kuṇḍadhānoti nāmena, sāvako so bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Pavivekamanuyutto, jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ;
```

```
Tosayitvāna satthāraṃ, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvakehi <pb ed="M" n="1.0092" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0081" /> <note>sāvakaggehi (sī.)</note> parivuto, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, salākaṃ gāhayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Ekaṃsaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0118" /> cīvaraṃ katvā, vanditvā lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Vadataṃ varassa purato, paṭhamaṃ aggahesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena bhagavā, dasasahassīkampako;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Vīriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṇḍadhāno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kuṇḍadhānattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Sāgatattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Sobhito <pb ed="P" n="1.0083" /> nāma nāmena, ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā;
```

```
Purakkhato sasissehi, ārāmaṃ agamāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
```

```
Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma, aṭṭhāsi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Tamaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, dantaṃ dantapurakkhataṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci pādapā sabbe, mahiyā te virūhare;
```

```
Buddhimanto <pb ed="T" n="1.0119" /> tathā sattā, ruhanti jinasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Satthavāhosi sappañño, mahesi bahuke jane;
```

```
Vipathā uddharitvāna, pathaṃ ācikkhase tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Danto <pb ed="M" n="1.0093" /> dantaparikiṇṇo <note>purakkhato (syā.)</note>, jhāyī jhānaratehi ca;
```

```
Ātāpī pahitattehi, upasantehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṅkato parisāhi, puññañāṇehi sobhati;
```

```
Pabhā niddhāvate tuyhaṃ, sūriyodayane yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacittaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0082" /> disvāna, mahesī padumuttaro;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo so hāsaṃ janetvāna, mamaṃ kittesi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, devaloke ramissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tusitā hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsane pabbajissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, arahattaṃ <note>tuṭṭhahaṭṭhaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> labhissati;
```

```
Sāgato nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
```

```
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0084" /> viharamānohaṃ, tejodhātūsu kovido;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0120" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāgato thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sāgatattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Mahākaccānattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaranāthassa, padumaṃ nāma cetiyaṃ;
```

```
Silāsanaṃ <note>sīhāsanaṃ (ka.)</note> kārayitvā, suvaṇṇenābhilepayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanāmayachattañca, paggayha vāḷabījaniṃ <note>vāḷabījanī (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, lokabandhussa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā <pb ed="M" n="1.0094" /> devatā bhummā <note>bhūmā (ka.)</note>, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā;
```

```
Ratanāmayachattānaṃ, vipākaṃ kathayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca sabbaṃ suṇissāma, kathayantassa satthuno;
```

```
Bhiyyo hāsaṃ janeyyāma, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Hemāsane nisīditvā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghaparibyūḷho <note>paribbūḷho (sī.)</note>, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yenidaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0083" /> āsanaṃ dinnaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ ratanāmayaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0121" /> devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, ābhāyābhibhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘‘Manussalokamāgantvā, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Pabhassaroti nāmena, uggatejo bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘‘Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ, sataraṃsīva uggato;
```

```
Samantā aṭṭharatanaṃ, ujjotissati khattiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tusitā <pb ed="P" n="1.0085" /> hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Kaccāno nāma nāmena, brahmabandhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, arahā hessatināsavo;
```

```
Gotamo lokapajjoto, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṃkhittapucchitaṃ <note>saṃkhittaṃ pucchitaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> pañhaṃ, vitthārena kathessati;
```

```
Kathayanto ca taṃ pañhaṃ, ajjhāsayaṃ <note>ajjhāsaṃ (sī.), abbhāsaṃ (ka.)</note> pūrayissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Aḍḍhe kule abhijāto, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
```

```
Ohāya dhanadhaññāni, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃkhittenapi pucchante, vitthārena kathemahaṃ;
```

```
Ajjhāsayaṃ tesaṃ pūremi, tosemi dvipaduttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Tosito <pb ed="M" n="1.0095" /> me mahāvīro, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0122" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākaccāno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mahākaccānattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Kāḷudāyittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa<pb ed="V" n="1.0084" />, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Addhānaṃ paṭipannassa, carato cārikaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha, uppalaṃ mallikañcahaṃ;
```

```
Paramannaṃ gahetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paribhuñji mahāvīro, paramannaṃ subhojanaṃ;
```

```
Tañca pupphaṃ gahetvāna, janassa sampadassayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Iṭṭhaṃ kantaṃ <note>kantayidaṃ (syā.)</note>, piyaṃ loke, jalajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Sudukkaraṃ kataṃ tena, yo me pupphaṃ adāsidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="P" n="1.0086" /> pupphamabhiropesi, paramannañcadāsi me;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dasa aṭṭha cakkhattuṃ <note>dasa caṭṭhakkhattuṃ (sī.), dasamaṭṭhakkhattuṃ (syā.)</note> so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Uppalaṃ padumañcāpi, mallikañca taduttari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘‘Assa <pb ed="T" n="1.0123" /> puññavipākena, dibbagandhasamāyutaṃ;
```

```
Ākāse chadanaṃ katvā, dhārayissati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ pañcasataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena <note>nāmena (sī. syā. ka.)</note>, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sakakammābhiraddho <pb ed="M" n="1.0096" /> so, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Sakyānaṃ nandijanano, ñātibandhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisambhidamanuppattaṃ, katakiccamanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Gotamo lokabandhu taṃ <note>so (sī.)</note>, etadagge ṭhapessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padhānapahitatto so, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Udāyī nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Rāgo <pb ed="V" n="1.0085" /> doso ca moho ca, māno makkho ca dhaṃsito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Tosayiñcāpi sambuddhaṃ, ātāpī nipako ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasādito <note>pamodito (sī.)</note> ca sambuddho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0124" /> sudaṃ āyasmā kāḷudāyī thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Kāḷudāyītherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Mogharājattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī <pb ed="P" n="1.0087" /> tu bhagavā, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghaparibyūḷho, rathiyaṃ paṭipajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Sissehi samparivuto, gharamhā abhinikkhamiṃ;
```

```
Nikkhamitvānahaṃ tattha, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Abhivādiya sambuddhaṃ, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā rūpino sattā, arūpī vā asaññino;
```

```
Sabbe te tava ñāṇamhi, anto honti samogadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhumacchikajālena<pb ed="M" n="1.0097" />, udakaṃ yo parikkhipe;
```

```
Ye keci udake pāṇā, antojāle bhavanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Yesañca cetanā atthi, rūpino ca arūpino;
```

```
Sabbe te tava ñāṇamhi, anto honti samogadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ, andhakārasamākulaṃ;
```

```
Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, kaṅkhāsotaṃ taranti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Avijjānivute loke, andhakārena otthaṭe;
```

```
Tava <pb ed="T" n="1.0125" /> ñāṇamhi jotante, andhakārā padhaṃsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Tuvaṃ cakkhūsi sabbesaṃ, mahātamapanūdano;
```

```
Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, nibbāyati bahujjano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Puṭakaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0086" /> pūrayitvāna <note>pīṭharaṃ (sī.), putaraṃ (syā.)</note>, madhukhuddamaneḷakaṃ;
```

```
Ubho hatthehi paggayha, upanesiṃ mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhi mahāvīro, sahatthena mahā isī;
```

```
Bhuñjitvā tañca sabbaññū, vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, atthadassī narāsabho;
```

```
Mama cittaṃ pasādento, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yenidaṃ thavitaṃ ñāṇaṃ, buddhaseṭṭho ca thomito;
```

```
Tena cittappasādena, duggatiṃ so na gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘‘Catuddasañcakkhattuṃ <note>catusaṭṭhiñca (syā.)</note> so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ aṭṭhasataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañceva <pb ed="P" n="1.0088" /> satakkhattuñca <note>atha pañcasatakkhattuṃ (sī.)</note>, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ asaṅkheyyaṃ, mahiyā kārayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsane pabbajissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ atthaṃ, ñāṇena vicinissati;
```

```
Mogharājāti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tīhi <pb ed="M" n="1.0098" /> vijjāhi sampannaṃ, katakiccamanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Gotamo <pb ed="T" n="1.0126" /> satthavāhaggo, etadagge ṭhapessati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Hitvā mānusakaṃ yogaṃ, chetvāna bhavabandhanaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0127" /> sudaṃ āyasmā mogharājo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Mogharājattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Adhimuttattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute lokanāthamhi, atthadassīnaruttame;
```

```
Upaṭṭhahiṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Nimantetvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0087" /> bhikkhusaṅghaṃ <note>saṃgharatanaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, ujubhūtaṃ samāhitaṃ;
```

```
Ucchunā maṇḍapaṃ katvā, bhojesiṃ saṅghamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe satte abhibhomi <note>atibhomi (sī. ka.)</note>, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ucchudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā adhimutto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Adhimuttattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Lasuṇadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="P" n="1.0089" />, tāpaso āsahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Lasuṇaṃ upajīvāmi, lasuṇaṃ mayhabhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Khāriyo <pb ed="M" n="1.0099" /> pūrayitvāna, saṅghārāmamagacchahaṃ;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, saṅghassa lasuṇaṃ adaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassissa naraggassa, sāsane niratassahaṃ;
```

```
Saṅghassa lasuṇaṃ datvā, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, lasuṇaṃ yamadaṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, lasuṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lasuṇadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Lasuṇadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Āyāgadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute <pb ed="T" n="1.0128" /> lokanāthamhi, sikhimhi vadataṃ vare;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, avandiṃ thūpamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Vaḍḍhakīhi <pb ed="V" n="1.0088" /> kathāpetvā, mūlaṃ datvānahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, āyāgaṃ kārapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭha kappāni devesu, abbokiṇṇaṃ <note>abbocchinnaṃ (sī.)</note> vasiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Avasesesu kappesu, vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsariṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Kāye visaṃ na kamati, satthāni na ca hanti me;
```

```
Udakehaṃ na miyyāmi, āyāgassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Yadicchāmi ahaṃ vassaṃ, mahāmegho pavassati;
```

```
Devāpi me vasaṃ enti, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Sattaratanasampanno, tisakkhattuṃ ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Na maṃ kecāvajānanti, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse <pb ed="P" n="1.0090" /> ito kappe, āyāgaṃ yamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, āyāgassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0100" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āyāgadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Āyāgadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Dhammacakkikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0129" /> bhagavato, sīhāsanassa sammukhā;
```

```
Dhammacakkaṃ me ṭhapitaṃ, sukataṃ viññuvaṇṇitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Cāruvaṇṇova sobhāmi, sayoggabalavāhano;
```

```
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, anuyantā bahujjanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhitūriyasahassehi, paricāremahaṃ sadā;
```

```
Parivārena sobhāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ cakkaṃ ṭhapayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dhammacakkassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Ito ekādase kappe, aṭṭhāsiṃsu janādhipā;
```

```
Sahassarājanāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0089" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhammacakkiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Dhammacakkikattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Kapparukkhiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, thūpaseṭṭhassa sammukhā;
```

```
Vicittadusse lagetvā <note>laggetvā (sī. syā.)</note>, kapparukkhaṃ ṭhapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0130" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0101" /> yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sobhayanto mama dvāraṃ, kapparukkho patiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Ahañca <pb ed="P" n="1.0091" /> parisā ceva, ye keci mama vassitā <note>nissitā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Tamhā dussaṃ gahetvāna, nivāsema mayaṃ sadā <note>tadā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ rukkhaṃ ṭhapayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kapparukkhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Ito ca sattame kappe, suceḷā aṭṭha khattiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kapparukkhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kapparukkhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Kuṇḍadhānavaggo catuttho.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kuṇḍasāgatakaccānā, udāyī mogharājako;
```

```
Adhimutto lasuṇado, āyāgī dhammacakkiko;
```

```
Kapparukkhī ca dasamo, gāthā dvayadasasataṃ <note>gāthāyo dvādasasataṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

### 5. Upālivaggo

#### 1. Bhāgineyyupālittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāsavasahassehi<pb ed="T" n="1.0131" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0102" />, parivuto <note>pareto (ka. aṭṭha)</note> lokanāyako;
```

```
Vivekamanuyutto so, gacchate paṭisallituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Ajinena nivatthohaṃ, tidaṇḍaparidhārako;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghaparibyūḷhaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Ekaṃsaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0092" /> ajinaṃ katvā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāṇḍajā ca saṃsedā, opapātī jalābujā;
```

```
Kākādipakkhino sabbe, antalikkhacarā sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci pāṇabhūtatthi, saññino vā asaññino;
```

```
Sabbe te tava ñāṇamhi, anto honti samogadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Gandhā ca pabbateyyā ye, himavantanaguttame;
```

```
Sabbe te tava sīlamhi, kalāyapi na yujjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Mohandhakārapakkhando, ayaṃ loko sadevako;
```

```
Tava ñāṇamhi jotante, andhakārā vidhaṃsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā atthaṅgate sūriye, honti sattā tamogatā;
```

```
Evaṃ buddhe anuppanne, hoti loko tamogato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Yathodayanto ādicco, vinodeti tamaṃ sadā;
```

```
Tatheva tvaṃ buddhaseṭṭha, viddhaṃsesi tamaṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Padhānapahitattosi<pb ed="T" n="1.0132" />, buddho loke sadevake;
```

```
Tava kammābhiraddhena, tosesi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sabbaṃ anumoditvā, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī dhīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Abbhuggantvāna <pb ed="V" n="1.0091" /> sambuddho, mahesi padumuttaro;
```

```
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Yenidaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0103" /> thavitaṃ ñāṇaṃ, opammehi samāyutaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārasañca khattuṃ so, devarājā bhavissati;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ tisataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tusitā hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Hīnova jātiyā santo, upāli nāma hessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘‘So <pb ed="P" n="1.0093" /> pacchā pabbajitvāna, virājetvāna pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tuṭṭho ca gotamo buddho, sakyaputto mahāyaso;
```

```
Vinayādhigataṃ tassa, etadagge ṭhapessati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāyāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0133" /> pabbajito, katakicco anāsavo;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā cānukampī maṃ, vinayehaṃ visārado;
```

```
Sakakammābhiraddho ca, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃvuto pātimokkhamhi, indriyesu ca pañcasu;
```

```
Dhāremi vinayaṃ sabbaṃ, kevalaṃ ratanākaraṃ <note>ratanaggharaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Mamañca guṇamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upālithero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhāgineyyupālittherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Soṇakoḷivisattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassissa <pb ed="M" n="1.0104" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0092" /> munino, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Sudhāya lepanaṃ katvā, caṅkamaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Nānāvaṇehi pupphehi, caṅkamaṃ santhariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Ākāse vitānaṃ katvā, bhojayiṃ buddhamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Añjaliṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0134" /> paggahetvāna, abhivādetvāna subbataṃ <note>pupphakaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Dīghasālaṃ bhagavato, niyyādesimahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
```

```
Paṭiggahesi bhagavā, anukampāya cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvāna sambuddho, dakkhiṇeyyo sadevake;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo so haṭṭhena cittena, dīghasālaṃ adāsi <note>akāsi (sī.)</note> me;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘‘Imassa <pb ed="P" n="1.0094" /> maccukālamhi, puññakammasamaṅgino;
```

```
Sahassayuttassaratho, upaṭṭhissati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena yānenayaṃ poso, devalokaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Anumodissare devā, sampatte kusalabbhave <note>kusale bhave (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahārahaṃ byamhaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, ratanamattikalepanaṃ;
```

```
Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ, byamhaṃ ajjhāvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Pañcavīsati kappāni, devarājā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Yasodharasanāmā <note>yasedharā samānā (sī.)</note> te, sabbepi ekanāmakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dve sampattī anubhotvā, vaḍḍhetvā <note>cinitvā (syā.)</note> puññasañcayaṃ;
```

```
Aṭṭhavīsatikappamhi, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tatrāpi <pb ed="T" n="1.0135" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0105" /> byamhaṃ pavaraṃ, vissakammena māpitaṃ;
```

```
Dasasaddāvivittaṃ taṃ, puramajjhāvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aparimeyye <pb ed="V" n="1.0093" /> ito kappe, bhūmipālo mahiddhiko;
```

```
Okkāko nāma nāmena, rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘‘Soḷasitthisahassānaṃ, sabbāsaṃ pavarā ca sā <note>pavarāva yā (syā.), pavarā piyā (?)</note>;
```

```
Abhijātā khattiyānī, nava putte janessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nava putte janetvāna, khattiyānī marissati;
```

```
Taruṇī ca piyā kaññā, mahesittaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘‘Okkākaṃ tosayitvāna, varaṃ kaññā labhissati;
```

```
Varaṃ laddhāna sā kaññā, putte pabbājayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pabbājitā ca te sabbe, gamissanti naguttamaṃ;
```

```
Jātibhedabhayā sabbe, bhaginīhi vasissare <note>saṃvasissare (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ekā ca kaññā byādhīhi, bhavissati parikkhatā <note>purakkhatā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Mā no jāti pabhijjīti, nikhaṇissanti khattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khattiyo nīharitvāna, tāya saddhiṃ vasissati;
```

```
Bhavissati tadā bhedo, okkākakulasambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tesaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0095" /> pajā bhavissanti, koḷiyā nāma jātiyā;
```

```
Tattha mānusakaṃ bhogaṃ, anubhossatinappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna, devalokaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Tatrāpi pavaraṃ byamhaṃ, labhissati manoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devalokā <pb ed="T" n="1.0136" /> cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Āgantvāna manussattaṃ, soṇo nāma bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, padahaṃ satthu sāsane;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anantadassī bhagavā, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Visesaññū mahāvīro, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Vuṭṭhamhi <pb ed="M" n="1.0106" /> deve caturaṅgulamhi, tiṇe anileritaaṅgaṇamhi;
```

```
Ṭhatvāna yogassa payuttatādino, tatottariṃ pāramatā na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Uttame damathe danto, cittaṃ me supaṇīhitaṃ;
```

```
Bhāro me ohito sabbo, nibbutomhi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅgīraso <pb ed="V" n="1.0094" /> mahānāgo, abhijātova kesarī;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇo koḷiviso <note>koḷiyavesso (sī. syā.), koṭikaṇṇo (ka.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Soṇakoḷivisattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Kāḷigodhāputtabhaddiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarasambuddhaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0137" />, mettacittaṃ mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Upeti janatā sabbā, sabbalokagganāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Sattukañca baddhakañca <note>vatthaṃ senāsanañceva (sī.), sattukañca padakañca (sī. aṭṭha.), sattukañca pavākañca (syā.)</note>, āmisaṃ pānabhojanaṃ;
```

```
Dadanti satthuno sabbe, puññakkhette anuttare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ahampi <pb ed="P" n="1.0096" /> dānaṃ dassāmi, devadevassa tādino;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ nimantetvā, saṅghampi ca anuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Uyyojitā mayā cete, nimantesuṃ tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Kevalaṃ bhikkhusaṅghañca, puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassapallaṅkaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ gonakatthataṃ;
```

```
Tūlikāpaṭalikāya, khomakappāsikehi ca;
```

```
Mahārahaṃ paññāpayiṃ, āsanaṃ buddhayuttakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="1.0107" /> lokavidū, devadevo narāsabho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghaparibyūḷho, mama dvāramupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ, lokanāthaṃ yasassinaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, abhināmayiṃ saṅgharaṃ <note>sakaṃ gharaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhūnaṃ satasahassaṃ, buddhañca lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, paramannena tappayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe <pb ed="T" n="1.0138" /> nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yenidaṃ āsanaṃ dinnaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ gonakatthataṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Catusattatikkhattuṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0095" /> so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Anubhossati sampattiṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ sahassaṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati;
```

```
Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbāsu bhavayonīsu, uccākulī <note>uccākule (ka.)</note> bhavissati;
```

```
So ca pacchā pabbajitvā, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Bhaddiyo nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vivekamanuyuttomhi, pantasenanivāsahaṃ;
```

```
Phalañcādhigataṃ sabbaṃ, cattaklesomhi ajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mama sabbaṃ <note>kammaṃ (?)</note> abhiññāya, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0097" /> sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddiyo kāḷigodhāya putto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhaddiyassa kāḷigodhāya puttattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Sanniṭṭhāpakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Araññe <pb ed="T" n="1.0139" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0108" /> kuṭikaṃ katvā, vasāmi pabbatantare;
```

```
Lābhālābhena santuṭṭho, yasena ayasena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi <note>bhikkhusatasahassehi (syā.)</note>, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahānāgaṃ <note>mahāvīraṃ (sī.)</note>, jalajuttamanāmakaṃ;
```

```
Tiṇasantharaṃ <note>tiṇattharaṃ (ka.)</note> paññāpetvā, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, āmaṇḍaṃ pānīyañcahaṃ;
```

```
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtassa, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe <note>satasahasse ito kappe (sī.)</note>, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, āmaṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatālīsakappamhi, eko āsiṃ arindamo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0096" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sanniṭṭhāpako <note>sannidhāpako (sī.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sanniṭṭhāpakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Pañcahatthiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho <pb ed="T" n="1.0140" /> nāma sambuddho, gacchate antarāpaṇe;
```

```
Okkhittacakkhu <note>khittacakkhu (ka. sī. ka.)</note> mitabhāṇī, satimā saṃvutindriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca uppalahatthāni, āveḷatthaṃ ahaṃsu me;
```

```
Tena buddhaṃ apūjesiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Āropitā <pb ed="P" n="1.0098" /> ca te pupphā, chadanaṃ assu satthuno;
```

```
Samādhiṃsu <note>saṃsāviṃsu (sī.)</note> mahānāgaṃ, sissā ācariyaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi<pb ed="M" n="1.0109" />, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Ito vīsakappasate, ahesuṃ pañca khattiyā;
```

```
Hatthiyā nāma nāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcahatthiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pañcahatthiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Padumacchadaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute lokanāthamhi, vipassimhaggapuggale;
```

```
Suphullapadumaṃ gayha, citamāropayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Āropite <pb ed="T" n="1.0141" /> ca citake, vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami;
```

```
Ākāse chadanaṃ <note>ākāsacchadanaṃ (sī.)</note> katvā, citakamhi adhārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Sattatālīsito <pb ed="V" n="1.0097" /> kappe, padumissaranāmako;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumacchadaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Padumacchadaniyattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Sayanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, mettacittassa tādino;
```

```
Sayanaggaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, dussabhaṇḍehi <note>dussabhaṇḍena (syā.)</note> atthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahesi <pb ed="M" n="1.0110" /> bhagavā, kappiyaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Uṭṭhāya sayanā <note>āsanā (sī.)</note> tamhā, vehāsaṃ uggamī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="P" n="1.0099" /> kappe, yaṃ sayanamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapaññāsito <pb ed="T" n="1.0142" /> kappe, varako <note>varuṇo (sī. syā.)</note> devasavhayo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sayanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sayanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Caṅkamanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassissa munino, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Iṭṭhakāhi cinitvāna, caṅkamaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Uccato pañcaratanaṃ, caṅkamaṃ sādhumāpitaṃ;
```

```
Āyāmato hatthasataṃ, bhāvanīyyaṃ manoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahesi bhagavā, atthadassī naruttamo;
```

```
Hatthena pulinaṃ gayha, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā <pb ed="V" n="1.0098" /> pulinadānena, caṅkamaṃ sukatena ca;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannaṃ, pulinaṃ anubhossati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tīṇi kappāni devesu, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Anubhossati sampattiṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘‘Manussalokamāgantvā<pb ed="T" n="1.0143" />, rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati;
```

```
Tikkhattuṃ cakkavattī ca, mahiyā so bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, caṅkamassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0111" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā caṅkamanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Caṅkamanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Subhaddattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="P" n="1.0100" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Janataṃ uddharitvāna, nibbāyati mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbāyante ca sambuddhe, dasasahassi kampatha;
```

```
Janakāyo mahā āsi, devā sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Candanaṃ pūrayitvāna, tagarāmallikāhi ca;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, āropayiṃ <note>ālepesiṃ (sī.), āropesiṃ (syā.)</note> naruttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
```

```
Nipannakova sambuddho, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0144" /> me pacchimake kāle, gandhamālena <note>gandhamallena (syā. ka.) napuṃsakekattaṃ manasikātabbaṃ</note> chādayi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ito cuto ayaṃ poso, tusitakāyaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Tattha rajjaṃ karitvāna, nimmānaṃ so gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘‘Eteneva upāyena, datvā mālaṃ <note>malyaṃ (sī.), mallaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> varuttamaṃ;
```

```
Sakakammābhiraddho so, sampattiṃ anubhossati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘‘Punāpi <pb ed="V" n="1.0099" /> tusite kāye, nibbattissatiyaṃ naro;
```

```
Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna, manussattaṃ gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sakyaputto mahānāgo, aggo loke sadevake;
```

```
Bodhayitvā bahū satte, nibbāyissati cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="1.0112" /> sopagato santo, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ, pañhaṃ pucchissati tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hāsayitvāna sambuddho, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
```

```
Puññakammaṃ pariññāya, saccāni vivarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āraddho ca ayaṃ pañho, tuṭṭho ekaggamānaso;
```

```
Satthāraṃ abhivādetvā, pabbajjaṃ yācayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pasannamānasaṃ disvā, sakakammena tositaṃ;
```

```
Pabbājessati so buddho, aggamaggassa kovido.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vāyamitvānayaṃ poso, sammāsambuddhasāsane;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

Pañcamabhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbakammena <pb ed="T" n="1.0145" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0101" /> saṃyutto, ekaggo susamāhito;
```

```
Buddhassa oraso putto, dhammajomhi sunimmito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammarājaṃ upagamma, apucchiṃ pañhamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Kathayanto ca me pañhaṃ, dhammasotaṃ upānayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ dhammamaññāya, vihāsiṃ sāsane rato;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, jalajuttamanāyako;
```

```
Nibbāyi anupādāno, dīpova telasaṅkhayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Sattayojanikaṃ āsi, thūpañca ratanāmayaṃ;
```

```
Dhajaṃ tattha apūjesiṃ, sabbabhaddaṃ manoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Kassapassa ca buddhassa, tisso nāmaggasāvako;
```

```
Putto me oraso āsi, dāyādo jinasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa hīnena manasā, vācaṃ bhāsiṃ abhaddakaṃ;
```

```
Tena kammavipākena, pacchā me āsi bhaddakaṃ <note>pacchime addasaṃ jinaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Upavattane <pb ed="V" n="1.0100" /> sālavane, pacchime sayane muni;
```

```
Pabbājesi mahāvīro, hito kāruṇiko jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjeva <pb ed="M" n="1.0113" /> dāni pabbajjā, ajjeva upasampadā;
```

```
Ajjeva parinibbānaṃ, sammukhā dvipaduttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0146" /> sudaṃ āyasmā subhaddo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Subhaddattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Cundattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Agghiyaṃ kārayitvāna, jātipupphehi chādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Niṭṭhāpetvāna taṃ pupphaṃ, buddhassa upanāmayiṃ;
```

```
Pupphāvasesaṃ paggayha, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ<pb ed="P" n="1.0102" />, buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, pupphagghiyamupānayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Vitiṇṇakaṅkho sambuddho, tiṇṇoghehi purakkhato;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dibbagandhaṃ pavāyantaṃ, yo me pupphagghiyaṃ adā;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ito cuto ayaṃ poso, devasaṅghapurakkhato;
```

```
Jātipupphehi parikiṇṇo, devalokaṃ gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ tassa, sovaṇṇañca maṇīmayaṃ;
```

```
Byamhaṃ pātubhavissati, puññakammappabhāvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘‘Catusattatikkhattuṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0147" /> so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Anubhossati sampattiṃ, accharāhi purakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pathabyā rajjaṃ tisataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati;
```

```
Pañcasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dujjayo <pb ed="V" n="1.0101" /> nāma nāmena, hessati manujādhipo;
```

```
Anubhotvāna taṃ puññaṃ, sakakammaṃ apassito <note>sakakammūpasaṃhito (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vinipātaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0114" /> agantvāna, manussattaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Hiraññaṃ tassa <note>hiraññassa ca (sī. ka.)</note> nicitaṃ, koṭisatamanappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nibbattissati yonimhi, brāhmaṇe so bhavissati;
```

```
Vaṅgantassa suto dhīmā, sāriyā oraso piyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘‘So ca pacchā pabbajitvā, aṅgīrasassa sāsane;
```

```
Cūḷacundoti <note>cūlacundoti (sī.)</note> nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sāmaṇerova so santo, khīṇāsavo bhavissati;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhahiṃ mahāvīraṃ, aññe ca pesale bahū;
```

```
Bhātaraṃ me cupaṭṭhāsiṃ, uttamatthassa pattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Bhātaraṃ me upaṭṭhitvā, dhātuṃ pattamhi ohiya <note>opiya (sī.), ociya (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ upanāmesiṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Ubho <pb ed="P" n="1.0103" /> hatthehi paggayha, buddho loke sadevake;
```

```
Sandassayanto taṃ dhātuṃ, kittayi aggasāvakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Cittañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0148" /> suvimuttaṃ me, saddhā mayhaṃ patiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidānuppattā, vimokkhāpi ca phassitā <note>paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cundo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Cundattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Upālivaggo pañcamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Upāli soṇo bhaddiyo, sanniṭṭhāpakahatthiyo;
```

```
Chadanaṃ seyyacaṅkamaṃ, subhaddo cundasavhayo;
```

```
Gāthāsataṃ satālīsaṃ <note>ca tālīsaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, catasso ca taduttari.
```

### 6. Bījanivaggo

#### 1. Vidhūpanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa<pb ed="M" n="1.0115" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0102" />, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Bījanikā <note>vījanikā (sī. syā.)</note> mayā dinnā, dvipadindassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhamabhivādetvā, pakkamiṃ uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Bījaniṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0149" /> paggahetvāna, satthā lokagganāyako <note>loke anuttaro (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito santo, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā bījanidānena, cittassa paṇidhīhi <note>cetanāpaṇidhīhi (aññattha)</note> ca;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, vinipātaṃ na gacchati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, cetoguṇasamāhito;
```

```
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi, bījamānasanāmakā;
```

```
Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="1.0104" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vidhūpanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Vidhūpanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Sataraṃsittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Ubbiddhaṃ selamāruyha, nisīdi purisuttamo;
```

```
Pabbatassāvidūramhi, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Upaviṭṭhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0103" /> mahāvīraṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘‘Esa <pb ed="T" n="1.0150" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0116" /> buddho mahāvīro, varadhammappakāsako;
```

```
Jalati aggikhandhova, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāsamuddova‘kkhubbho <note>’kkhobho (sī. syā.)</note>, aṇṇavova duruttaro;
```

```
Migarājāvasambhīto <note>chambhito (ka.)</note>, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, padumuttaranāyako;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yenāyaṃ <note>yenāhaṃ (ka.)</note> añjalī dinno, buddhaseṭṭho ca thomito;
```

```
Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, aṅgīrasasanāmako;
```

```
Vivaṭṭacchado <note>vivatthacchaddo (sī.)</note> sambuddho, uppajjissati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sataraṃsīti nāmena, arahā so bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Sataraṃsimhi nāmena, pabhā niddhāvate mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi, caturo rāmanāmakā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="1.0105" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0151" /> sudaṃ āyasmā sataraṃsi thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sataraṃsittherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Sayanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, sabbalokānukampino;
```

```
Sayanaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="1.0117" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0104" /> sayanadānena, sukhette bījasampadā;
```

```
Bhogā nibbattare tassa, sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Ākāse seyyaṃ kappemi, dhāremi pathaviṃ imaṃ;
```

```
Pāṇesu me issariyaṃ, sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcakappasahassamhi, aṭṭha āsuṃ mahātejā <note>mahāvarā (sī.), mahāvīrā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Catuttiṃse kappasate, caturo ca mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sayanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sayanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Gandhodakiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa<pb ed="T" n="1.0152" />, mahābodhimaho ahu;
```

```
Vicittaṃ ghaṭamādāya, gandhodakamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Nhānakāle ca bodhiyā, mahāmegho pavassatha;
```

```
Ninnādo ca mahā āsi, asaniyā phalantiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Tenevāsanivegena, tattha kālaṅkato <note>kālakato (sī. syā.)</note> ahaṃ <note>ahuṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Devaloke ṭhito santo, imā gāthā abhāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aho <pb ed="P" n="1.0106" /> buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthusampadā;
```

```
Kaḷevaraṃ <note>kalebaraṃ (sī.)</note> me patitaṃ, devaloke ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, satabhūmaṃ samuggataṃ;
```

```
Kaññāsatasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ābādhā me na vijjanti, soko mayhaṃ na vijjati;
```

```
Pariḷāhaṃ na passāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhavīse kappasate, rājā saṃvasito ahuṃ;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0118" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhodakiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Gandhodakiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Opavayhattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa<pb ed="T" n="1.0153" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0105" />, ājānīyamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Niyyādetvāna sambuddhe <note>sambuddhaṃ (sī. ka.)</note>, agamāsiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Devalo nāma nāmena, satthuno aggasāvako;
```

```
Varadhammassa dāyādo, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Sapattabhāro bhagavā, ājāneyyo na kappati;
```

```
Tava saṅkappamaññāya, adhivāsesi cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Agghāpetvā vātajavaṃ, sindhavaṃ sīghavāhanaṃ;
```

```
Padumuttarabuddhassa, khamanīyamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ <note>deve ca mānuse bhave (sī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Khamanīyaṃ vātajavaṃ, cittaṃ nibbattate <note>ājānīyā vātajavā, vitti nibbattare (syā.), khamanīyā vātajavā, cittā nibbattare (sī.)</note> mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0107" /> tesaṃ suladdhaṃva, ye labhantupasampadaṃ;
```

```
Punapi payirupāseyyaṃ, buddho loke sace bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhavīsatikkhattuṃhaṃ, rājā āsiṃ mahabbalo;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambusaṇḍassa <note>jambudīpassa (syā.), jambumaṇḍassa (ka.)</note> jambuissaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Pattosmi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Catutiṃsasahassamhi, mahātejosi khattiyo;
```

```
Sataratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0154" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0119" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā opavayho thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Opavayhattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Saparivārāsanattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, piṇḍapātaṃ adāsahaṃ;
```

```
Gantvā kiliṭṭhakaṃ ṭhānaṃ <note>taṃ bhojanaṭṭhānaṃ (sī.)</note>, mallikāhi parikkhitaṃ <note>parikkhipiṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Tamhāsanamhi <pb ed="V" n="1.0106" /> āsīno, buddho lokagganāyako;
```

```
Akittayi piṇḍapātaṃ, ujubhūto samāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddake khette, bījaṃ appampi ropitaṃ;
```

```
Sammā dhāraṃ pavecchante, phalaṃ toseti kassakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Tathevāyaṃ piṇḍapāto, sukhette ropito tayā;
```

```
Bhave nibbattamānamhi, phalaṃ te <note>nibbattamānaṃ hi, phalato (sī.)</note> tosayissati <note>tappayissati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
```

```
Piṇḍapātaṃ gahetvāna, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃvuto pātimokkhasmiṃ, indriyesu ca pañcasu;
```

```
Pavivekamanuyutto, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0155" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0108" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saparivārāsano thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Saparivārāsanattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Pañcadīpakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, sabbabhūtānukampino;
```

```
Saddahitvāna <note>susaṇṭhahitvā (sī.)</note> saddhamme, ujudiṭṭhi ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Padīpadānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0120" /> pādāsiṃ, parivāretvāna bodhiyaṃ;
```

```
Saddahanto padīpāni, akariṃ tāvade ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Ākāse ukkaṃ dhārenti, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Tirokuṭṭaṃ tiroselaṃ, samatiggayha pabbataṃ;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, dassanaṃ anubhomahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammāvasesena, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, dvipadindassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Catuttiṃse kappasate, satacakkhusanāmakā;
```

```
Rājāhesuṃ mahātejā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0156" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0107" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcadīpako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pañcadīpakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Dhajadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, bodhiyā pādaputtame;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, dhajamāropayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Patitapattāni gaṇhitvā, bahiddhā chaḍḍayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Antosuddhaṃ bahisuddhaṃ, adhimuttamanāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, avandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Padumuttaro <pb ed="P" n="1.0109" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha;
```

```
‘‘‘Iminā dhajadānena, upaṭṭhānena cūbhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ so na gacchati;
```

```
Devesu devasobhagyaṃ, anubhossatinappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anekasatakkhattuñca<pb ed="M" n="1.0121" />, rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati;
```

```
Uggato nāma nāmena, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sampattiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0157" /> anubhotvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsanebhiramissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Padhānapahitattomhi, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapaññāsasahasse, kappe uggatasavhayo <note>savhayā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Paññāsasatasahasse, khattiyo meghasavhayo <note>khattiyā khemasavhayā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhajadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Dhajadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Padumattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Catusaccaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0108" /> pakāsento, varadhammappavattako;
```

```
Vassate <note>vasseti (?)</note> amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ, nibbāpento mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Sadhajaṃ <note>sadaṇḍaṃ (sī.)</note> padumaṃ gayha, aḍḍhakose ṭhito ahaṃ;
```

```
Padumuttaramunissa, pahaṭṭho ukkhipimambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Āgacchante ca padume, abbhuto āsi tāvade;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, paggaṇhi vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Karaseṭṭhena <pb ed="T" n="1.0158" /> paggayha, jalajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yenidaṃ padumaṃ khittaṃ, sabbaññumhi vināyake <note>sabbaññutamanāyake (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0122" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0110" /> devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ sattasataṃ, vasudhaṃ āvasissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tattha pattaṃ gaṇetvāna, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Ākāsato pupphavuṭṭhi, abhivassissatī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma nāmena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Nikkhamitvāna kucchimhā, sampajāno patissato;
```

```
Jātiyā pañcavassohaṃ, arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Padumattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Asanabodhiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā <pb ed="T" n="1.0159" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0109" /> sattavassohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Tissassāhaṃ bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, ropayiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Asano nāmadheyyena, dharaṇīruhapādapo;
```

```
Pañcavasse paricariṃ, asanaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphitaṃ pādapaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ kammaṃ pakittento, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Tisso tadā so sambuddho, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yenāyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0123" /> ropitā bodhi, buddhapūjā ca sakkatā;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappāni devesu, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Catusaṭṭhi cakkhattuṃ so, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tusitā <pb ed="P" n="1.0111" /> hi cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Dve sampattī anubhotvā, manussatte ramissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padhānapahitatto so, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Vivekamanuyuttohaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0160" />, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, bodhiṃ ropesahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bodhiropassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Catusattatito kappe, daṇḍasenoti vissuto;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī tadā ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Tesattatimhito kappe, sattāhesuṃ mahīpatī;
```

```
Samantanemināmena, rājāno cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsatito <pb ed="V" n="1.0110" /> kappe, puṇṇako nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā asanabodhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Asanabodhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Bījanivaggo chaṭṭho.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Bījanī sataraṃsī ca, sayanodakivāhiyo;
```

```
Parivāro padīpañca, dhajo padumapūjako;
```

```
Bodhi ca dasamo vutto, gāthā dvenavuti tathā.
```

### 7. Sakacintaniyavaggo

#### 1. Sakacintaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Pavanaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0161" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0124" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0111" /> kānanaṃ disvā, appasaddamannāvilaṃ;
```

```
Isīnaṃ anuciṇṇaṃva, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Thūpaṃ katvāna pulinaṃ <note>veḷunā (aṭṭha.), veḷinaṃ (syā.)</note>, nānāpupphaṃ samokiriṃ;
```

```
Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, nimmitaṃ abhivandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Sattaratanasampanno<pb ed="P" n="1.0112" />, rājā raṭṭhamhi issaro;
```

```
Sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ, pupphapūjāyidaṃ <note>thūpapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ <note>thūpapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Asītikappenantayaso, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, catudīpamhi issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sakacintaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sakacintaniyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Avopupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Vihārā abhinikkhamma, abbhuṭṭhahiya <note>abbhuṭṭhāsi ca (syā. ka.)</note> caṅkame;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāsanto, deseti <note>desento (syā. ka.)</note> amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Sikhissa <pb ed="T" n="1.0162" /> giramaññāya, buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Nānāpupphaṃ gahetvāna, ākāsamhi samokiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="1.0112" /> kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse <pb ed="M" n="1.0125" /> ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ito vīsatikappamhi, sumedho nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā avopupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Avopupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Paccāgamaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Sindhuyā <pb ed="P" n="1.0113" /> nadiyā tīre, cakkavāko ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Suddhasevālabhakkhohaṃ, pāpesu ca susaññato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase;
```

```
Tuṇḍena sālaṃ paggayha, vipassissābhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0163" /> saddhā tathāgate, acalā supatiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Tena cittappasādena, duggatiṃ so na gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
```

```
Vihaṅgamena santena, subījaṃ ropitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ <note>pupphapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Sucārudassanā nāma, aṭṭhete ekanāmakā;
```

```
Kappe sattarase āsuṃ, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paccāgamaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Paccāgamaniyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Parappasādakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Usabhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0126" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0113" /> pavaraṃ vīraṃ, mahesiṃ vijitāvinaṃ;
```

```
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ, ko disvā nappasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Himavāvāparimeyyo, sāgarova duruttaro;
```

```
Tatheva jhānaṃ buddhassa, ko disvā nappasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Vasudhā yathāppameyyā, cittā vanavaṭaṃsakā;
```

```
Tatheva <pb ed="T" n="1.0164" /> sīlaṃ buddhassa, ko disvā nappasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Anilañjasāsaṅkhubbho <note>anilajova asaṅkhobho (sī.)</note>, yathākāso asaṅkhiyo;
```

```
Tatheva ñāṇaṃ buddhassa, ko disvā nappasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Imāhi <pb ed="P" n="1.0114" /> catugāthāhi, brāhmaṇo senasavhayo;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thavitvāna, siddhatthaṃ aparājitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutikappāni, duggatiṃ nupapajjatha;
```

```
Sugatiṃ sukhasampattiṃ <note>sugatīsu susumpattiṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, anubhosimanappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, thavitvā lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, thomanāya <note>thomanassa (syā.)</note> idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasamhi kappamhi, caturo āsumuggatā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā parappasādako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Parappasādakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Bhisadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Vessabhū nāma nāmena, isīnaṃ tatiyo ahu;
```

```
Kānanaṃ vanamogayha, vihāsi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Bhisamuḷālaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0165" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0127" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0114" /> gaṇhitvā, agamaṃ buddhasantikaṃ;
```

```
Tañca buddhassa pādāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Karena ca parāmaṭṭho, vessabhūvarabuddhinā;
```

```
Sukhāhaṃ nābhijānāmi, samaṃ tena kutottariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Carimo vattate mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Hatthināgena santena, kusalaṃ ropitaṃ mayā <note>nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Samodhānā ca rājāno, soḷasa manujādhipā;
```

```
Kappamhi cuddase <note>terase (sī. syā.)</note> āsuṃ, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhisadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhisadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Sucintitattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Giriduggacaro <pb ed="P" n="1.0115" /> āsiṃ, abhijātova kesarī;
```

```
Migasaṅghaṃ vadhitvāna, jīvāmi pabbatantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī <pb ed="T" n="1.0166" /> tu bhagavā, sabbaññū vadataṃ varo;
```

```
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi pabbatuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Pasadañca migaṃ hantvā, bhakkhituṃ samupāgamiṃ;
```

```
Bhagavā tamhi samaye, bhikkhamāno <note>sikkhācāro (syā.)</note> upāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Varamaṃsāni paggayha, adāsiṃ tassa satthuno;
```

```
Anumodi mahāvīro, nibbāpento mamaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="1.0115" /> cittappasādena, giriduggaṃ pavisiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pītiṃ uppādayitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Etena <pb ed="M" n="1.0128" /> maṃsadānena, cittassa paṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Pannarase kappasate, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Avasesesu kappesu, kusalaṃ cintitaṃ <note>nicitaṃ (sī.), karitaṃ (syā.)</note> mayā;
```

```
Teneva maṃsadānena, buddhānussaraṇena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhattiṃsamhi kappamhi, aṭṭha dīghāyunāmakā;
```

```
Saṭṭhimhito kappasate, duve varuṇanāmakā <note>saraṇanāmakā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucintito thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sucintitattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Vatthadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Pakkhijāto <pb ed="T" n="1.0167" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0116" /> tadā āsiṃ, supaṇṇo garuḷādhipo;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ gandhamādanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Jahitvā garuḷavaṇṇaṃ, māṇavakaṃ adhārayiṃ;
```

```
Ekaṃ vatthaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, dvipadindassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca dussaṃ paṭiggayha, buddho lokagganāyako;
```

```
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā vatthadānena, cittassa paṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Pahāya garuḷaṃ yoniṃ, devaloke ramissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī tu bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Vatthadānaṃ pasaṃsitvā, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Bhave nibbattamānamhi, honti me vatthasampadā;
```

```
Ākāse chadanaṃ hoti, vatthadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Aruṇavā <pb ed="M" n="1.0129" /> <note>aruṇakā (sī.), aruṇasā (syā.)</note> satta janā, cakkavattī mahabbalā;
```

```
Chattiṃsatimhi āsiṃsu, kappamhi manujādhipā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0116" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vatthadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Vatthadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Ambadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī <pb ed="T" n="1.0168" /> bhagavā, nisinno pabbatantare;
```

```
Mettāya aphari loke, appamāṇe nirūpadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Kapi ahaṃ tadā āsiṃ, himavante naguttame;
```

```
Disvā anomadassiṃ taṃ <note>anomaṃ amitaṃ (sī.), anomamadhitaṃ (syā.)</note>, buddhe cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Avidūre himavantassa, ambāsuṃ phalino tadā;
```

```
Tato pakkaṃ gahetvāna, ambaṃ samadhukaṃ adaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0117" /> me buddho viyākāsi, anomadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Iminā madhudānena, ambadānena cūbhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Sattapaññāsakappamhi, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Avasesesu kappesu, vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Khepetvā pāpakaṃ kammaṃ, paripakkāya buddhiyā;
```

```
Vinipātamagantvāna, kilese jhāpayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Damena uttamenāhaṃ, damitomhi mahesinā;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Sattasattatikappasate, ambaṭṭhajasanāmakā;
```

```
Catuddasa te rājāno, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0169" /> sudaṃ āyasmā ambadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ambadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Sumanattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Sumano <pb ed="M" n="1.0130" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0117" /> nāma nāmena, mālākāro ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Ubho hatthehi paggayha, sumanaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Imāya pupphapūjāya, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ <note>pupphapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Chabbīsatimhi kappamhi, cattārosuṃ mahāyasā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, rājāno cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumano thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sumanattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Pupphacaṅkoṭiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Abhītarūpaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0170" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0118" /> sīhaṃva, garuḷaggaṃva pakkhinaṃ;
```

```
Byagghūsabhaṃva pavaraṃ, abhijātaṃva kesariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Sikhiṃ tilokasaraṇaṃ, anejaṃ aparājitaṃ;
```

```
Nisinnaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Caṅkoṭake <note>caṅgoṭake (sī.)</note> ṭhapetvāna, anojaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Saha caṅkoṭakeneva, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ samokiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, dvipadinda narāsabha;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Sampuṇṇe <pb ed="M" n="1.0131" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0118" /> tiṃsakappamhi, devabhūtisanāmakā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, pañcāsuṃ cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphacaṅkoṭiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pupphacaṅkoṭiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Sakacintaniyavaggo sattamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sakacintī <pb ed="T" n="1.0171" /> avopupphī, sapaccāgamanena ca;
```

```
Parappasādī bhisado, sucinti vatthadāyako.
```

```
Ambadāyī ca sumano, pupphacaṅkoṭakīpi ca;
```

```
Gāthekasattati vuttā, gaṇitā atthadassibhi.
```

### 8. Nāgasamālavaggo

#### 1. Nāgasamālattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Apāṭaliṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0132" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0119" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0119" /> ahaṃ pupphaṃ, ujjhitaṃ sumahāpathe;
```

```
Thūpamhi abhiropesiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, thūpapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Ito pannarase kappe, bhūmiyo <note>pupphiyo (syā.)</note> nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nāgasamālo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Nāgasamālattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Padasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Akkantañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0172" /> padaṃ disvā, tissassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, pade cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, padasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Ito sattamake kappe, sumedho nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavatī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Padasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Buddhasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Dumagge <pb ed="M" n="1.0133" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0120" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0120" /> paṃsukūlikaṃ, laggaṃ disvāna satthuno;
```

```
Tato tamañjaliṃ katvā, paṃsukūlaṃ avandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="T" n="1.0173" /> catutthake kappe, dumasārosi khattiyo;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Buddhasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Bhisāluvadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Kānanaṃ vanamogayha, vasāmi vipine ahaṃ;
```

```
Vipassiṃ addasaṃ buddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Bhisāluvañca pādāsiṃ, udakaṃ hatthadhovanaṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā sirasā pāde, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, bhisāluvamadaṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Ito tatiyake kappe, bhisasammatakhattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0174" /> sudaṃ āyasmā bhisāluvadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhisāluvadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

Chaṭṭhabhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 5. Ekasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Khaṇḍo <pb ed="V" n="1.0121" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0134" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0121" /> nāmāsi nāmena, vipassissaggasāvako;
```

```
Ekā bhikkhā mayā dinnā, lokāhutipaṭiggahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, dvipadinda narāsabha;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekabhikkhāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Cattālīsamhito kappe, varuṇo nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Tiṇasantharadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre, mahājātassaro ahu;
```

```
Satapattehi sañchanno, nānāsakuṇamālayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Tamhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0175" /> nhatvā ca pitvā <note>pītvā (sī. syā.)</note> ca, avidūre vasāmahaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
```

```
Abbhato oruhitvāna, bhūmiyaṃṭhāsi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Visāṇena <note>lāyanena (syā.)</note> tiṇaṃ gayha, nisīdanamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Nisīdi bhagavā tattha, tisso lokagganāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, avandi lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Paṭikuṭiko <note>ukkuṭiko (syā. ka.)</note> apasakkiṃ, nijjhāyanto mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, nimmānaṃ upapajjahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, santharassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="M" n="1.0135" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0122" /> dutiyake kappe, miga <note>mitta (syā.)</note> sammatakhattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0122" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇasantharadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Tiṇasantharadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Sūcidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, sambuddho lokanāyako;
```

```
Sumedho nāma nāmena, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```
