<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0176" /> kañcanavaṇṇassa, dvipadindassa tādino;
```

```
Pañca sūcī mayā dinnā, sibbanatthāya cīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva sūcidānena, nipuṇatthavipassakaṃ;
```

```
Tikkhaṃ lahuñca phāsuñca, ñāṇaṃ me udapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Dvipadādhipatī nāma, rājāno caturo ahuṃ;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sūcidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sūcidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Pāṭalipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Seṭṭhiputto <pb ed="M" n="1.0136" /> tadā āsiṃ, sukhumālo sukhedhito;
```

```
Ucchaṅge pāṭalipupphaṃ, katvāna <note>katvā taṃ (sī. syā.)</note> abhisaṃhariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Haṭṭho <pb ed="T" n="1.0177" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0123" /> haṭṭhena cittena, pupphehi abhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Tissaṃ lokaviduṃ nāthaṃ, naradevaṃ namassahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute <pb ed="V" n="1.0123" /> ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Ito tesaṭṭhikappamhi, abhisammatanāmako;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭalipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pāṭalipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Ṭhitañjaliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
```

```
Tattha addasaṃ <note>tatthaddasāsiṃ (sī. syā.)</note> sambuddhaṃ, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthāhaṃ añjaliṃ katvā, pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho;
```

```
Avidūre nisinnassa, niyake paṇṇasanthare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me asanīpāto, matthake nipatī tadā;
```

```
Sohaṃ maraṇakālamhi, akāsiṃ punarañjaliṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute <pb ed="T" n="1.0178" /> ito kappe, añjaliṃ akariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, añjalissa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Catupaṇṇāsakappamhi, migaketusanāmako;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ṭhitañjaliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ṭhitañjaliyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Tipadumiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="1.0137" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0124" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Danto dantaparivuto, nagarā nikkhamī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="V" n="1.0124" /> haṃsavatiyaṃ, ahosiṃ māliko tadā;
```

```
Yaṃ tattha uttamaṃ toṇi, padmapupphāni <note>uttamaṃ pupphaṃ, tīṇi pupphāni (sī.)</note> aggahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, paṭimaggantarāpaṇe;
```

```
Saha <note>sohaṃ (sī.)</note> disvāna sambuddhaṃ, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ me imehi pupphehi, rañño upanitehi me;
```

```
Gāmaṃ vā gāmakhettaṃ vā, sahassaṃ vā labheyyahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Adantadamanaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0179" /> vīraṃ, sabbasattasukhāvahaṃ;
```

```
Lokanāthaṃ pūjayitvā, lacchāmi amataṃ dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
```

```
Tīṇi lohitake gayha, ākāse ukkhipiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Mayā ukkhittamattamhi, ākāse patthariṃsu te;
```

```
Dhāriṃsu matthake tattha, uddhaṃvaṇṭā adhomukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci manujā disvā, ukkuṭṭhiṃ sampavattayuṃ;
```

```
Devatā antalikkhamhi, sādhukāraṃ pavattayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Accheraṃ loke uppannaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā;
```

```
Sabbe dhammaṃ suṇissāma, pupphānaṃ vāhasā mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Vīthiyañhi ṭhito santo, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo so buddhaṃ apūjesi, rattapadmehi <note>rattapadumehi (sī. syā.)</note> māṇavo;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Tiṃsakappāni <note>tiṃsakkhattuñca (syā.)</note> devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāvitthārikaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0138" /> nāma, byamhaṃ hessati tāvade;
```

```
Tiyojanasatubbiddhaṃ, diyaḍḍhasatavitthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cattārisatasahassāni<pb ed="P" n="1.0125" />, niyyūhā ca sumāpitā;
```

```
Kūṭāgāravarūpetā, mahāsayanamaṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘‘Koṭisatasahassiyo<pb ed="T" n="1.0180" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0125" />, parivāressanti accharā;
```

```
Kusalā naccagītassa, vāditepi padakkhiṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etādise byamhavare, nārīgaṇasamākule;
```

```
Vassissati pupphavasso, dibbo <note>pada (ka.)</note> lohitako sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhittikhīle nāgadante, dvārabāhāya toraṇe;
```

```
Cakkamattā lohitakā, olambissanti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pattena pattasañchanne, antobyamhavare imaṃ;
```

```
Attharitvā pārupitvā, tuvaṭṭissanti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhavanaṃ parivāretvā, samantā satayojane;
```

```
Tepi padmā <note>te visuddhā (sī. syā.)</note> lohitakā, dibbagandhaṃ pavāyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sampattiyo duve bhutvā, anīti anupaddavo;
```

```
Sampatte pariyosāne, nibbānaṃ pāpuṇissati’ <note>phassayissati (sī.), passayissati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Sudiṭṭho vata me buddho, vāṇijjaṃ supayojitaṃ;
```

```
Padmāni tīṇi pūjetvā, anubhosiṃ tisampadā <note>anubhūyanti sampadā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Ajja me dhammappattassa, vippamuttassa sabbaso;
```

```
Supupphitaṃ lohitakaṃ, dhārayissati matthake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Mama kammaṃ kathentassa, padumuttarasatthuno;
```

```
Satapāṇasahassānaṃ, dhammābhisamayo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="T" n="1.0181" /> kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tipadumānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="1.0139" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0126" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0126" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tipadumiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Tipadumiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Nāgasamālavaggo aṭṭhamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Nāgasamālo padasaññī, saññakāluvadāyako;
```

```
Ekasaññī tiṇasanthāro, sūcipāṭalipupphiyo;
```

```
Ṭhitañjalī tipadumī, gāthāyo pañcasattati.
```

### 9. Timiravaggo

#### 1. Timirapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre<pb ed="T" n="1.0182" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0140" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0127" />, anusotaṃ vajāmahaṃ;
```

```
Nisinnaṃ samaṇaṃ disvā, vippasannamanāvilaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā <note>pasādesiṃ (syā.)</note>, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Tārayissati tiṇṇoyaṃ, dantoyaṃ damayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Assāsissati assattho, santo ca samayissati;
```

```
Mocayissati mutto ca, nibbāpessati nibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, siddhatthassa mahesino;
```

```
Gahetvā timirapupphaṃ, matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ <note>tadā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, pakkāmiṃ aparaṃ disaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Aciraṃ gatamattaṃ maṃ, migarājā viheṭhayi;
```

```
Papātamanugacchanto, tattheva papatiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ <note>buddhapūjāyidaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Chappaññāsamhi <pb ed="P" n="1.0127" /> kappamhi, sattevāsuṃ mahāyasā <note>mahārahā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā <pb ed="T" n="1.0183" /> sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā timirapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Timirapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Gatasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā <pb ed="M" n="1.0141" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0128" /> sattavassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Avandiṃ satthuno pāde, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Sattanaṅgalakīpupphe, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tissaṃ buddhaṃ samuddissa, anantaguṇasāgaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Sugatānugataṃ maggaṃ, pūjetvā haṭṭhamānaso;
```

```
Añjaliñca <note>añjalissa (ka.)</note> tadākāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Ito aṭṭhamake kappe, tayo aggisikhā ahu;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gatasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Gatasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Nipannañjalikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Rukkhamūle <pb ed="T" n="1.0184" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0128" /> nisinnohaṃ, byādhito paramena ca;
```

```
Paramakāruññapattomhi, araññe kānane ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampaṃ upādāya, tisso satthā upesi maṃ;
```

```
Sohaṃ nipannako santo, sire katvāna añjaliṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, sabbasattānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ vandiṃ purisuttamaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="M" n="1.0142" /> pañcamake kappe, pañcevāsuṃ mahāsikhā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0129" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nipannañjaliko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Nipannañjalikattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Adhopupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Abhibhū nāma so bhikkhu, sikhino aggasāvako;
```

```
Mahānubhāvo tevijjo, himavantaṃ upāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Ahampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0185" /> himavantamhi, ramaṇīyassame isi;
```

```
Vasāmi appamaññāsu, iddhīsu ca tadā vasī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Pakkhijāto viyākāse, pabbataṃ adhivattayiṃ <note>abhipatthayiṃ (syā.), abhimatthayiṃ (ka.), adhivatthayinti pabbatassa upari gacchintiattho</note>;
```

```
Adhopupphaṃ gahetvāna, āgacchiṃ <note>agacchiṃ (ka.)</note> pabbataṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Satta pupphāni gaṇhitvā, matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Ālokite <note>ālokito (syā.)</note> ca vīrena, pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Āvāsaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0129" /> abhisambhosiṃ, patvāna assamaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, pāyāsiṃ <note>pāvisiṃ (sī.)</note> pabbatantaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Ajagaro maṃ pīḷesi, ghorarūpo mahabbalo;
```

```
Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā adhopupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Adhopupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Raṃsisaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate <pb ed="M" n="1.0143" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0130" /> himavantamhi, vāsaṃ kappesahaṃ pure;
```

```
Ajinuttaravāsohaṃ, vasāmi pabbatantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0186" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0130" /> sambuddhaṃ, sataraṃsiṃva bhāṇumaṃ;
```

```
Vanantaragataṃ disvā, sālarājaṃva pupphitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Raṃsyā <note>raṃse (syā. ka.)</note> cittaṃ pasādetvā, vipassissa mahesino;
```

```
Paggayha añjaliṃ vandiṃ, sirasā ukkuṭī <note>sirasā ukkuṭiko (syā.), sirasukkuṭiko (ka.)</note> ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, raṃsisaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṃsisaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Raṃsisaññakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Dutiyaraṃsisaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate himavantamhi, vākacīradharo ahaṃ;
```

```
Caṅkamañca samārūḷho, nisīdiṃ pācināmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate sugataṃ disvā, phussaṃ jhānarataṃ tadā;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, raṃsyā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, raṃsisaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0187" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṃsisaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Dutiyaraṃsisaññakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Phaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate <pb ed="M" n="1.0144" /> himavantamhi, kharājinadharo ahaṃ;
```

```
Phussaṃ jinavaraṃ disvā, phalahattho phalaṃ adaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Yamahaṃ phalamadāsiṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Bhave nibbattamānamhi, phalaṃ nibbattate mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0131" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Phaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Saddasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate <pb ed="T" n="1.0188" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0131" /> himavantamhi, vasāmi paṇṇasanthare;
```

```
Phussassa dhammaṃ bhaṇato, sadde cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Saddasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Bodhisiñcakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassissa bhagavato, mahābodhimaho ahu;
```

```
Pabbajjupagato santo, upagacchiṃ ahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Kusumodakamādāya<pb ed="M" n="1.0145" />, bodhiyā okiriṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Mocayissati no mutto, nibbāpessati nibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ bodhimabhisiñcayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bodhisiñcāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Tettiṃse <pb ed="T" n="1.0189" /> vattamānamhi, kappe āsuṃ janādhipā;
```

```
Udakasecanā nāma, aṭṭhete cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhisiñcako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bodhisiñcakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Padumapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Pokkharavanaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0132" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0132" /> paviṭṭho, bhañjanto padumānihaṃ;
```

```
Tatthaddasaṃ phussaṃ buddhaṃ <note>addasaṃ phussasambuddhaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Padumapupphaṃ gahetvāna, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pāpakammaṃ saritvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, manasā saṃvutena ca;
```

```
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Padumābhāsanāmā ca, aṭṭhārasa mahīpatī;
```

```
Aṭṭhārasesu kappesu, aṭṭhatālīsamāsisuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0190" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0146" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Padumapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Timiravaggo navamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Timiranaṅgalīpuppha, nippannañjaliko adho;
```

```
Dve raṃsisaññī phalado, saddasaññī ca secako;
```

```
Padmapupphī ca gāthāyo, chappaññāsa pakittitā.
```

### 10. Sudhāvaggo

#### 1. Sudhāpiṇḍiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjārahe <pb ed="M" n="1.0147" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0133" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0133" /> pūjayato, buddhe yadi va sāvake;
```

```
Papañcasamatikkante, tiṇṇasokapariddave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Te tādise pūjayato, nibbute akutobhaye;
```

```
Na sakkā puññaṃ saṅkhātuṃ, imettamapi <note>idammattanti (sī.), imetthamapi (ka.)</note> kenaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnamapi dīpānaṃ, issaraṃ yodha kāraye;
```

```
Ekissā pūjanāyetaṃ, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0191" /> naraggassa, cetiye phalitantare;
```

```
Sudhāpiṇḍo mayā dinno, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, paṭisaṅkhārassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Ito tiṃsatikappamhi, paṭisaṅkhārasavhayā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, terasa cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sudhāpiṇḍiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sudhāpiṇḍiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Sucintikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Tissassa lokanāthassa, suddhapīṭhamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, buddhassādiccabandhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase <pb ed="V" n="1.0134" /> <note>aṭṭhatiṃse (sī. syā.)</note> ito kappe, rājā āsiṃ mahāruci;
```

```
Bhogo ca vipulo āsi, sayanañca anappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0148" /> buddhassa datvāna, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, pubbe sukatamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute <pb ed="T" n="1.0192" /> ito kappe, yaṃ pīṭhamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pīṭhadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhatiṃse ito kappe, tayo te cakkavattino;
```

```
Ruci uparuci ceva, mahāruci tatiyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucintiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sucintikattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Aḍḍhaceḷakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Tissassāhaṃ bhagavato, upaḍḍhadussamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Paramakāpaññapattomhi <note>paramakāruññapattomhi (syā. ka.)</note>, duggatena <note>duggandhena (sī.)</note> samappito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Upaḍḍhadussaṃ datvāna, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ;
```

```
Avasesesu kappesu, kusalaṃ kāritaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute <pb ed="P" n="1.0134" /> ito kappe, yaṃ dussamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dussadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Ekūnapaññāsakappamhi <note>ekapaññāsakappamhi (syā.)</note>, rājāno cakkavattino;
```

```
Samantacchadanā nāma, bāttiṃsāsuṃ <note>khattiyāsuṃ (syā. ka.)</note> janādhipā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0193" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aḍḍhaceḷako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Aḍḍhaceḷakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Sūcidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Kammārohaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0149" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0135" /> pure āsiṃ, bandhumāyaṃ puruttame;
```

```
Sūcidānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, vipassissa mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Vajiraggasamaṃ ñāṇaṃ, hoti kammena tādisaṃ;
```

```
Virāgomhi vimuttomhi <note>vibhavomhi vibhattomhi (ka.)</note>, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Atīte <pb ed="P" n="1.0135" /> ca bhave sabbe, vattamāne canāgate <note>atītā ca bhavā sabbe, vattamānā ca’nāgatā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ñāṇena viciniṃ sabbaṃ, sūcidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, sattāsuṃ vajiravhayā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sūcidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sūcidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Gandhamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0194" /> bhagavato, gandhathūpaṃ akāsahaṃ;
```

```
Sumanehi paṭicchannaṃ, buddhānucchavikaṃ kataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ, buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ;
```

```
Indīvaraṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Byagghūsabhaṃva pavaraṃ, abhijātaṃva kesariṃ;
```

```
Nisinnaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvā satthuno pāde, pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho;
```

```
Catunnavutito kappe, gandhamālaṃ yato adaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhe katassa kārassa, phalenāhaṃ visesato;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Cattārīsamhi ekūne, kappe āsiṃsu soḷasa;
```

```
Devagandhasanāmā te, rājāno cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0150" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0136" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Gandhamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Tipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="T" n="1.0195" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0136" /> pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ <note>brahā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Pāṭaliṃ haritaṃ disvā, tīṇi pupphāni okiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Patitapattāni <note>sattapattāni (sī.), satapattāni (ka.), sukkhapaṇṇāni (syā.)</note> gaṇhitvā, bahi chaḍḍesahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Antosuddhaṃ bahisuddhaṃ, suvimuttaṃ anāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pāṭaliṃ abhivādetvā, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ bodhimabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bodhipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Samantapāsādikā nāma, terasāsiṃsu rājino;
```

```
Ito tettiṃsakappamhi <note>tiṃsatikappamhi (syā.)</note>, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Tipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Madhupiṇḍikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Vipine <pb ed="T" n="1.0196" /> <note>vivane (syā. aṭṭha.)</note> kānane disvā, appasadde nirākule;
```

```
Siddhatthaṃ isinaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbutattaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0151" /> <note>nibbutaggaṃ (ka.), nibbūtikaṃ (syā.)</note> mahānāgaṃ, nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā;
```

```
Osadhiṃva virocantaṃ, devasaṅghanamassitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Vitti mamāhu tāvade <note>vitti me pāhunā tāva (sī. syā.)</note>, ñāṇaṃ uppajji tāvade;
```

```
Vuṭṭhitassa samādhimhā, madhuṃ datvāna satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0137" /> satthuno pāde, pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho;
```

```
Catuttiṃsamhi kappamhi, rājā āsiṃ sudassano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Madhu bhisehi savati, bhojanamhi ca tāvade;
```

```
Madhuvassaṃ pavassittha, pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="P" n="1.0137" /> kappe, yaṃ madhuṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Catuttiṃse ito kappe, cattāro te sudassanā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0197" /> sudaṃ āyasmā madhupiṇḍiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Madhupiṇḍikattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Senāsanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, adāsiṃ paṇṇasantharaṃ;
```

```
Samantā upahārañca, kusumaṃ okiriṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Pāsādevaṃ guṇaṃ rammaṃ <note>pāsāde ca guhaṃ rammaṃ (syā.)</note>, anubhomi mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Mahagghāni ca pupphāni, sayanebhisavanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭāmi, vicitte pupphasanthate;
```

```
Pupphavuṭṭhi ca sayane, abhivassati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="M" n="1.0152" /> kappe, adāsiṃ paṇṇasantharaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, santharassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṇasantharakā nāma, sattete cakkavattino;
```

```
Ito te pañcame kappe, uppajjiṃsu janādhipā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="1.0138" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā senāsanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Senāsanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Veyyāvaccakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassissa <pb ed="T" n="1.0198" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0138" /> bhagavato, mahāpūgagaṇo ahu;
```

```
Veyyāvaccakaro āsiṃ, sabbakiccesu vāvaṭo <note>byāvaṭo (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Deyyadhammo ca me natthi, sugatassa mahesino;
```

```
Avandiṃ satthuno pāde, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, veyyāvaccaṃ akāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, veyyāvaccassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Ito ca aṭṭhame kappe, rājā āsiṃ sucintito;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā veyyāvaccako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Veyyāvaccakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Buddhupaṭṭhākattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassissa bhagavato, ahosiṃ saṅkhadhammako;
```

```
Niccupaṭṭhānayuttomhi, sugatassa mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhānaphalaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0199" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0153" /> passa, lokanāthassa tādino;
```

```
Saṭṭhitūriyasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="P" n="1.0139" /> kappe, upaṭṭhahiṃ mahāisiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Catuvīse <note>catunavute (syā.)</note> ito kappe, mahānigghosanāmakā;
```

```
Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhupaṭṭhāko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Buddhupaṭṭhākattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

Sudhāvaggo dasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sudhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0139" /> sucinti ceḷañca, sūcī ca gandhamāliyo;
```

```
Tipupphiyo madhusenā, veyyāvacco cupaṭṭhako;
```

```
Samasaṭṭhi ca gāthāyo, asmiṃ vagge pakittitā.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Buddhavaggo hi paṭhamo, sīhāsani subhūti ca;
```

```
Kuṇḍadhāno upāli ca, bījanisakacinti ca.
```

```
Nāgasamālo <pb ed="T" n="1.0200" /> timiro, sudhāvaggena te dasa;
```

```
Catuddasasatā gāthā, pañcapaññāsameva ca.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Buddhavaggadasakaṃ.</trailer>

Paṭhamasatakaṃ samattaṃ.

### 11. Bhikkhadāyivaggo

#### 1. Bhikkhadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0154" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0140" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0140" /> sambuddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Pavarā <note>pavanā (syā.)</note> abhinikkhantaṃ, vanā nibbanamāgataṃ <note>vānā nibbānamāgataṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ, siddhatthassa mahesino;
```

```
Paññāya upasantassa, mahāvīrassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Padenānupadāyantaṃ <note>padenānupadāyanto (sī. syā.)</note>, nibbāpente mahājanaṃ;
```

```
Uḷārā vitti me jātā, buddhe ādiccabandhune <note>vitti me pāhunā tāva, buddhassādiccabandhuno (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Sattāsītimhito kappe, mahāreṇu sanāmakā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, sattete cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0201" /> sudaṃ āyasmā bhikkhadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhikkhadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ñāṇasaññikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ, nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā;
```

```
Tidhāpabhinnaṃ mātaṅgaṃ, kuñjaraṃva mahesinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā, uḷurājaṃva pūritaṃ;
```

```
Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ apassahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Ñāṇe <pb ed="M" n="1.0155" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0141" /> cittaṃ pasādetvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, siddhatthamabhivādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Tesattatimhito kappe, soḷasāsuṃ naruttamā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="1.0141" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇasaññiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ñāṇasaññikattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Uppalahatthiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Tivarāyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0202" /> nivāsīhaṃ, ahosiṃ māliko tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, siddhatthaṃ lokapūjitaṃ <note>lokanāyakaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, pupphahatthamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Yattha yatthupapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Anubhomi phalaṃ iṭṭhaṃ, pubbe sukatamattano;
```

```
Parikkhitto sumallehi, pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ <note>buddhapūjāyidaṃ (sī.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutupādāya, ṭhapetvā vattamānakaṃ;
```

```
Pañcarājasatā tattha, najjasamasanāmakā <note>najjupamasanāmakā (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uppalahatthiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Uppalahatthiyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Padapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0156" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0142" /> bhagavato, jātipupphamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Pādesu satta pupphāni, hāsenokiritāni me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="1.0203" /> kammenahaṃ ajja, abhibhomi narāmare;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="P" n="1.0142" /> kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Samantagandhanāmāsuṃ, terasa cakkavattino;
```

```
Ito pañcamake kappe, cāturantā janādhipā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Padapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Muṭṭhipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Sudassanoti nāmena, mālākāro ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Jātipupphaṃ gahetvāna, pūjayiṃ padumuttaraṃ;
```

```
Visuddhacakkhu sumano, dibbacakkhuṃ samajjhagaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Etissā pupphapūjāya, cittassa paṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Soḷasāsiṃsu <pb ed="T" n="1.0204" /> rājāno, devuttarasanāmakā;
```

```
Chattiṃsamhi ito kappe, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā muṭṭhipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Muṭṭhipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Udakapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0157" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0143" /> sambuddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase;
```

```
Ghatāsanaṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇinā udakaṃ gayha, ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Sampaṭicchi mahāvīro, buddho kāruṇiko isi <note>mayi (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Antalikkhe <pb ed="P" n="1.0143" /> ṭhito satthā, padumuttaranāmako;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā dakadānena, pītiuppādanena ca;
```

```
Kappasatasahassampi, duggatiṃ nupapajjati’ <note>nupapajjasi (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassarājanāmena<pb ed="T" n="1.0205" />, tayo te cakkavattino;
```

```
Pañcasaṭṭhikappasate, cāturantā janādhipā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Udakapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Naḷamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Tiṇatthare nisinnassa, upasantassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna, bandhitvā <note>bījitvā (ka.)</note> bījaniṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa upanāmesiṃ, dvipadindassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā sabbaññū, bījaniṃ lokanāyako;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathā <pb ed="M" n="1.0158" /> me kāyo nibbāti, pariḷāho na vijjati;
```

```
Tatheva tividhaggīhi, cittaṃ tava vimuccatu’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe <pb ed="V" n="1.0144" /> devā samāgacchuṃ, ye keci vananissitā;
```

```
Sossāma buddhavacanaṃ, hāsayantañca dāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Nisinno <pb ed="T" n="1.0206" /> bhagavā tattha, devasaṅghapurakkhato;
```

```
Dāyakaṃ sampahaṃsento, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā bījanidānena, cittassa paṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Subbato nāma nāmena, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena <pb ed="P" n="1.0144" /> kammāvasesena, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Māluto nāma nāmena, cakkavattī bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā bījanidānena, sammānavipulena ca;
```

```
Kappasatasahassampi, duggatiṃ nupapajjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, subbatā aṭṭhatiṃsa te;
```

```
Ekūnatiṃsasahasse, aṭṭha mālutanāmakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Naḷamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

Sattamabhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 8. Āsanupaṭṭhāhakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Kānanaṃ vanamogayha, appasaddaṃ nirākulaṃ;
```

```
Sīhāsanaṃ mayā dinnaṃ, atthadassissa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Mālāhatthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0207" /> gahetvāna, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Satthāraṃ payirupāsitvā, pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="1.0159" /> kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Sannibbāpemi <note>sandiṭṭhāpemi (ka.)</note> attānaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārasakappasate, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="V" n="1.0145" /> sattakappasate, sannibbāpaka <note>sanniṭṭho nāma (ka.)</note> khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āsanupaṭṭhāhako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Āsanupaṭṭhāhakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Biḷālidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="P" n="1.0145" />, vasāmi paṇṇasanthare;
```

```
Ghāsesu gedhamāpanno, seyyasīlo cahaṃ <note>seyasīlovahaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Khaṇantālu <note>khaṇamālu (syā.)</note> kalambāni, biḷālitakkalāni ca;
```

```
Kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ billaṃ, āhatvā paṭiyāditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="1.0208" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahānāgaṃ, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Biḷāliṃ paggahetvāna, pattamhi okiriṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Paribhuñji mahāvīro, tosayanto mamaṃ tadā;
```

```
Paribhuñjitvāna sabbaññū, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, biḷāliṃ me adā tuvaṃ;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjasi’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Carimaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0160" /> vattate mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Catupaññāsito kappe, sumekhaliyasavhayo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā biḷālidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Biḷālidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Reṇupūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0209" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0146" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0146" /> sambuddhaṃ, sataraṃsiṃva bhāṇumaṃ;
```

```
Obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā, uḷurājaṃva pūritaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Purakkhataṃ sāvakehi, sāgareheva medaniṃ;
```

```
Nāgaṃ paggayha reṇūhi, vipassissābhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ reṇumabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇatālīsito kappe, reṇu nāmāsi khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā reṇupūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Reṇupūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Bhikkhadāyivaggo ekādasamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Bhikkhadāyī ñāṇasaññī, hatthiyo padapūjako;
```

```
Muṭṭhipupphī udakado, naḷamāli upaṭṭhako;
```

```
Biḷālidāyī reṇu ca, gāthāyo cha ca saṭṭhi ca.
```

### 12. Mahāparivāravaggo

#### 1. Mahāparivārakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassī <pb ed="T" n="1.0210" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0161" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0147" /> nāma bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Aṭṭhasaṭṭhisahassehi, pāvisi bandhumaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Nagarā abhinikkhamma, agamaṃ dīpacetiyaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, yakkhā mayhaṃ upantike;
```

```
Upaṭṭhahanti sakkaccaṃ <note>maṃ niccaṃ (ka.)</note>, indaṃva tidasā gaṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavanā <pb ed="P" n="1.0147" /> abhinikkhamma, dussaṃ paggayhahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Sirasā abhivādesiṃ, tañcādāsiṃ mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthu sampadā;
```

```
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, vasudhāyaṃ pakampatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Buddhe cittaṃ pasādemi, dvipadindamhi tādine.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, dussaṃ datvāna satthuno;
```

```
Saraṇañca upāgacchiṃ, sāmacco saparijjano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Ito pannarase kappe, soḷasāsuṃ suvāhanā <note>soḷasāsiṃsu vāhano (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0211" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāparivārako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mahāparivārakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Sumaṅgalattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī <pb ed="M" n="1.0162" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0148" /> jinavaro, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Vihārā abhinikkhamma, taḷākaṃ upasaṅkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Nhatvā pitvā ca sambuddho, uttaritvekacīvaro;
```

```
Aṭṭhāsi bhagavā tattha, vilokento disodisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, apphoṭesiṃ ahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Sataraṃsiṃva jotantaṃ, pabhāsantaṃva kañcanaṃ <note>iminā pādadvayena purimapādadvayassa purato bhavitabbaṃ</note>;
```

```
Naccagīte payuttohaṃ, pañcaṅgatūriyamhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe satte abhibhomi, vipulo hoti me yaso <note>ayañca gāthā pariggahetigāthāya anantarameva ṭhātuṃ yuttā</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Namo <pb ed="P" n="1.0148" /> te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Attānaṃ tosayitvāna, pare tosesi tvaṃ muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Pariggahe <pb ed="T" n="1.0212" /> <note>pariggayha (sī.), pariggahitvā (syā.), pariggahena (ka.)</note> nisīditvā, hāsaṃ katvāna subbate;
```

```
Upaṭṭhahitvā sambuddhaṃ, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Soḷaseto kappasate, dvinavaekacintitā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumaṅgalo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sumaṅgalattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Saraṇagamaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Ubhinnaṃ devarājūnaṃ, saṅgāmo samupaṭṭhito;
```

```
Ahosi samupabyūḷho <note>samupabbūḷho (sī.)</note>, mahāghoso avattatha <note>pavattatha (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="1.0163" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, saṃvejesi mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe <pb ed="V" n="1.0149" /> devā attamanā, nikkhittakavacāvudhā;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, ekaggāsiṃsu tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Mayhaṃ <note>amhaṃ (sī.)</note> saṅkappamaññāya, vācāsabhimudīrayi;
```

```
Anukampako lokavidū, nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Paduṭṭhacitto <pb ed="T" n="1.0213" /> manujo, ekapāṇaṃ viheṭhayaṃ;
```

```
Tena cittappadosena, apāyaṃ upapajjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅgāmasīse nāgova, bahū pāṇe viheṭhayaṃ;
```

```
Nibbāpetha sakaṃ cittaṃ, mā haññittho punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Dvinnampi yakkharājūnaṃ, senā sā vimhitā ahu <note>senāyo vimhitā ahū (sī.), senāpi samitā ahu (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Saraṇañca upāgacchuṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ sutādinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Saññāpetvāna <pb ed="P" n="1.0149" /> janataṃ, padamuddhari <note>uddhari pana (sī. syā.)</note> cakkhumā;
```

```
Pekkhamānova devehi, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭhamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchiṃ, dvipadindassa tādino;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Mahādundubhināmā ca, soḷasāsuṃ rathesabhā;
```

```
Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, rājāno cakkavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saraṇagamaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Saraṇagamaniyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Ekāsaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Varuṇo nāma nāmena, devarājā ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Upaṭṭhahesiṃ sambuddhaṃ, sayoggabalavāhano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute <pb ed="T" n="1.0214" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0164" /> lokanāthamhi, atthadassīnaruttame;
```

```
Tūriyaṃ sabbamādāya, agamaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Vāditena ca naccena, sammatāḷasamāhito;
```

```
Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, upaṭṭhiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhahitvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0150" /> taṃ bodhiṃ, dharaṇīruhapādapaṃ;
```

```
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ, pasanno bodhimuttame;
```

```
Tena cittappasādena, nimmānaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhitūriyasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
```

```
Manussesu ca devesu, vattamānaṃ bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Tividhaggī nibbutā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāsane <note>ayañca gāthā paṭisambhidā catassetigāthāya ekasambandhā bhavitaṃ yuttā</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Subāhū <pb ed="P" n="1.0150" /> nāma nāmena, catuttiṃsāsu khattiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, pañcakappasate ito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekāsaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekāsaniyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Suvaṇṇapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassī <pb ed="T" n="1.0215" /> nāma bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Nisinno janakāyassa, desesi amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna, dvipadindassa tādino;
```

```
Soṇṇapupphāni cattāri, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ āsi, yāvatā parisā tadā;
```

```
Buddhābhā ca suvaṇṇābhā, āloko vipulo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Udaggacitto <pb ed="M" n="1.0165" /> sumano, vedajāto katañjalī;
```

```
Vittisañjanano tesaṃ, diṭṭhadhammasukhāvaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Āyācitvāna sambuddhaṃ, vanditvāna ca subbataṃ;
```

```
Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna, sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ;
```

```
Tena cittappasādena, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="V" n="1.0151" /> kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno, nemisammatanāmakā;
```

```
Tetālīse ito kappe, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0216" /> sudaṃ āyasmā suvaṇṇapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Suvaṇṇapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Citakapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Vasāmi <pb ed="P" n="1.0151" /> rājāyatane, sāmacco saparijjano;
```

```
Parinibbute bhagavati, sikhino lokabandhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, citakaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tūriyaṃ tattha vādetvā, gandhamālaṃ samokiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Citamhi pūjaṃ katvāna, vanditvā citakaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ, citapūjaṃ anussariṃ;
```

```
Tena kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Anubhotvāna sampattiṃ, devesu mānusesu ca;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse <pb ed="M" n="1.0166" /> ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, citapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Ekūnatiṃsakappamhi, ito soḷasa rājāno;
```

```
Uggatā nāma nāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0217" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Citakapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Buddhasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="V" n="1.0152" /> vipassī lokaggo, āyusaṅkhāramossaji;
```

```
Pathavī sampakampittha, medanī jalamekhalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Otataṃ vitthataṃ <note>otataṃ vitataṃ (syā.)</note> mayhaṃ, suvicittavaṭaṃsakaṃ <note>sucicittaṃ papañcakaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Bhavanampi pakampittha, buddhassa āyusaṅkhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Tāso <pb ed="P" n="1.0152" /> mayhaṃ samuppanno, bhavane sampakampite;
```

```
Uppādo <note>uppāto (?)</note> nu kimatthāya, āloko vipulo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Vessavaṇo idhāgamma, nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ;
```

```
Pāṇabhūte <note>pāṇabhutaṃ (syā.), pāṇabhūnaṃ (sī. ka.)</note> bhayaṃ natthi, ekaggā hotha saṃvutā <note>sagāravā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthu sampadā;
```

```
Yasmiṃ uppajjamānamhi, pathavī <note>paṭhavī (sī. syā.)</note> sampakampati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhānubhāvaṃ kittetvā, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ;
```

```
Avasesesu kappesu, kusalaṃ caritaṃ <note>karitaṃ (sī. syā.), kāritaṃ (ka.)</note> mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="T" n="1.0218" /> kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="M" n="1.0167" /> cuddasakappamhi, rājā āsiṃ patāpavā;
```

```
Samito nāma nāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Buddhasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Maggasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, sāvakā vanacārino;
```

```
Vippanaṭṭhā brahāraññe, andhāva anusuyyare <note>anusuyare (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Anussaritvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0153" /> sambuddhaṃ, padumuttaranāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tassa te munino puttā, vippanaṭṭhā mahāvane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavanā oruhitvāna, agamiṃ bhikkhusantikaṃ;
```

```
Tesaṃ maggañca ācikkhiṃ, bhojanañca adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Sacakkhū <pb ed="T" n="1.0219" /> nāma nāmena, dvādasa cakkavattino;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, pañcakappasate ito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="1.0153" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maggasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Maggasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Paccupaṭṭhānasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassimhi sugate, nibbute samanantarā;
```

```
Yakkhayoniṃ upapajjiṃ, yasaṃ patto cahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Dulladdhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0168" /> vata me āsi, duppabhātaṃ duruṭṭhitaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ me bhoge vijjamāne, parinibbāyi cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, sāgaro nāma sāvako;
```

```
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama santikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ nu socasi mā bhāyi, cara dhammaṃ sumedhasa;
```

```
Anuppadinnā buddhena, sabbesaṃ bījasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘So ce pūjeyya sambuddhaṃ, tiṭṭhantaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Dhātuṃ sāsapamattampi, nibbutassāpi pūjaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Same <pb ed="T" n="1.0220" /> cittappasādamhi, samaṃ puññaṃ mahaggataṃ;
```

```
Tasmā thūpaṃ karitvāna, pūjehi jinadhātuyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Sāgarassa vaco sutvā, buddhathūpaṃ akāsahaṃ;
```

```
Pañcavasse paricariṃ, munino thūpamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="1.0154" /> kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Bhūripaññā ca cattāro, sattakappasate ito;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paccupaṭṭhānasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Paccupaṭṭhānasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Jātipūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Jāyantassa <pb ed="P" n="1.0154" /> vipassissa, āloko vipulo ahu;
```

```
Pathavī ca pakampittha, sasāgarā sapabbatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Nemittā ca viyākaṃsu, buddho loke bhavissati;
```

```
Aggo ca sabbasattānaṃ, janataṃ uddharissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Nemittānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0221" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0169" /> suṇitvāna, jātipūjamakāsahaṃ;
```

```
Edisā pūjanā natthi, yādisā jātipūjanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkharitvāna <note>saṃharitvāna (sī. syā.), saṅkaritvāna (ka.)</note>
```

Kusalaṃ, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.

```
Jātipūjaṃ karitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe satte abhibhomi, jātipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Dhātiyo maṃ upaṭṭhanti, mama cittavasānugā;
```

```
Na tā sakkonti kopetuṃ, jātipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pūjamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, jātipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Supāricariyā nāma, catuttiṃsa janādhipā;
```

```
Ito tatiyakappamhi, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0155" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jātipūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Jātipūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Mahāparivāravaggo dvādasamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Parivārasumaṅgalā, saraṇāsanapupphiyā;
```

```
Citapūjī buddhasaññī, maggupaṭṭhānajātinā;
```

```
Gāthāyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0222" /> navuti vuttā, gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi.
```

### 13. Sereyyavaggo

#### 1. Sereyyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyako <pb ed="M" n="1.0170" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0156" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0155" /> mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Abbhokāse ṭhito santo, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhaṃ yathā vanacaraṃ, byaggharājaṃva nittasaṃ;
```

```
Tidhāpabhinnamātaṅgaṃ, kuñjaraṃva mahesinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Sereyyakaṃ gahetvāna, ākāse ukkhipiṃ <note>nikkhipiṃ (ka.)</note> ahaṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, parivārenti sabbaso <note>sabbato (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Adhiṭṭhahi mahāvīro, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
```

```
Samantā pupphacchadanā, okiriṃsu narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Tato sā pupphakañcukā, antovaṇṭā bahimukhā;
```

```
Sattāhaṃ chadanaṃ katvā, tato antaradhāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Buddhe cittaṃ pasādesiṃ, sugate lokanāyake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Tena cittappasādena, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Pannarasasahassamhi<pb ed="T" n="1.0223" />, kappānaṃ pañcavīsati;
```

```
Vītamalā <note>cittamālā (sī.), vilāmālā (syā.)</note> samānā ca, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sereyyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sereyyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Pupphathūpiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="M" n="1.0171" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0157" />, kukkuro nāma <note>kukkuṭo nāma (sī.)</note> pabbato;
```

```
Vemajjhe tassa vasati, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca sissasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
```

```
Pubbuṭṭhāyī ca te āsuṃ, mantesu ca visāradā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho <pb ed="P" n="1.0156" /> loke samuppanno, taṃ vijānātha no bhavaṃ;
```

```
Asītibyañjanānassa, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Byāmappabho jinavaro, ādiccova virocati;
```

```
Sissānaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Assamā abhinikkhamma, disaṃ pucchati sissake <note>brāhmaṇo (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Yamhi dese mahāvīro, vasati lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ disaṃ namassissaṃ, jinaṃ appaṭipuggalaṃ;
```

```
Udaggacitto sumano, pūjesiṃ taṃ tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Etha <pb ed="T" n="1.0224" /> sissā gamissāma, dakkhissāma tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, sossāma jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Ekāhaṃ abhinikkhamma, byādhiṃ paṭilabhiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Byādhinā pīḷito santo, sālaṃ vāsayituṃ gamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe sisse samānetvā, apucchiṃ te tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Kīdisaṃ lokanāthassa, guṇaṃ paramabuddhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Te me puṭṭhā viyākaṃsu, yathā dassāvino tathā;
```

```
Sakkaccaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ taṃ, desesuṃ <note>dassesuṃ (sī. syā.)</note> mama sammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Tesāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
```

```
Pupphehi thūpaṃ katvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Te me sarīraṃ jhāpetvā, agamuṃ buddhasantikaṃ;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, satthāramabhivādayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphehi thūpaṃ katvāna, sugatassa mahesino;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Cattālīsasahassamhi<pb ed="M" n="1.0172" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0158" />, kappe soḷasa khattiyā;
```

```
Nāmenaggisamā nāma, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Vīsakappasahassamhi, rājāno cakkavattino;
```

```
Ghatāsanasanāmāva, aṭṭhattiṃsa mahīpatī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0225" /> sudaṃ āyasmā pupphathūpiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pupphathūpiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Pāyasadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo <pb ed="P" n="1.0157" /> sambuddho, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
```

```
Pavanā <note>padhāno (ka.)</note> abhinikkhanto, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato <note>suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ …pe… purakkhataṃ-evaṃ dutiyantavasena sī. syā. potthakesu dissati</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Mahaccā <note>sahatthā (syā. ka.)</note> kaṃsapātiyā, vaḍḍhetvā pāyasaṃ <note>pāyāsaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> ahaṃ;
```

```
Āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmo so, upanesiṃ baliṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Caṅkamaṃ susamārūḷho, ambare anilāyane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Ṭhapayitvā kaṃsapātiṃ, vipassiṃ abhivādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Tuvaṃ devosi <note>buddhosi (syā.)</note> sabbaññū, sadeve sahamānuse;
```

```
Anukampaṃ upādāya, paṭigaṇha mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahesi bhagavā, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke mahāmuni <note>anuttaro (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pāyasassa <note>pāyāsassa (syā. ka.)</note> idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatālīsito <pb ed="M" n="1.0173" /> kappe, buddho nāmāsi khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0226" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāyasadāyako <note>pāyāsadāyako (syā. ka.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pāyasadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Gandhodakiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Nisajja <pb ed="V" n="1.0159" /> pāsādavare, vipassiṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ;
```

```
Kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃva, sabbaññuṃ tamanāsakaṃ <note>sabbaññuttamanāyakaṃ (syā.), sabbaññutamanāsavaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Pāsādassāvidūre ca, gacchati lokanāyako;
```

```
Pabhā niddhāvate tassa, yathā ca sataraṃsino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Gandhodakañca <pb ed="P" n="1.0158" /> paggayha, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ samokiriṃ;
```

```
Tena cittappasādena, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ gandhodakamākiriṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, sugandho nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0227" /> sudaṃ āyasmā gandhodakiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Gandhodakiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Sammukhāthavikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Jāyamāne vipassimhi, nimittaṃ byākariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
‘Nibbāpayiñca <note>nibbāpayaṃ ca (sī. syā.), nibbāpayanto (?)</note> janataṃ, buddho loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca <pb ed="M" n="1.0174" /> jāyamānasmiṃ, dasasahassi kampati;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ, āloko vipulo ahu;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ, saritāyo na sandayuṃ <note>sandisuṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ, avīcaggi na pajjali;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca <pb ed="V" n="1.0160" /> jāyamānasmiṃ, pakkhisaṅgho na saṃcari;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ, vātakkhandho na vāyati;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca <pb ed="T" n="1.0228" /> jāyamānasmiṃ, sabbaratanāni jotayuṃ <note>jotisuṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ, sattāsuṃ padavikkamā;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘‘Jātamatto <pb ed="P" n="1.0159" /> ca sambuddho, disā sabbā vilokayi;
```

```
Vācāsabhimudīresi, esā buddhāna dhammatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃvejayitvā janataṃ, thavitvā lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhithomayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, thomanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Ito navutikappamhi, sammukhāthavikavhayo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Pathavīdundubhi nāma <note>duddasi nāma (ka.)</note>, ekūnanavutimhito;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhāsītimhito <pb ed="M" n="1.0175" /> kappe, obhāso nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Sattāsītimhito kappe, saritacchedanavhayo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Agginibbāpano nāma, kappānaṃ chaḷasītiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Gatipacchedano nāma, kappānaṃ pañcasītiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Rājā <pb ed="T" n="1.0229" /> vātasamo nāma, kappānaṃ cullasītiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanapajjalo <pb ed="V" n="1.0161" /> nāma, kappānaṃ teasītiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Padavikkamano nāma, kappānaṃ dveasītiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Rājā vilokano nāma, kappānaṃ ekasītiyā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Girasāroti nāmena, kappesītimhi khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sammukhāthaviko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sammukhāthavikattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Kusumāsaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="T" n="1.0230" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0160" /> dhaññavatiyā, ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā;
```

```
Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Padako <pb ed="M" n="1.0176" /> veyyākaraṇo, nimittakovido ahaṃ;
```

```
Mante ca sisse vācesiṃ, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca uppalahatthāni, piṭṭhiyaṃ ṭhapitāni me;
```

```
Āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmohaṃ, pitumātusamāgame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā vipassī bhagavā, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
```

```
Obhāsento disā sabbā, āgacchati narāsabho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Āsanaṃ paññapetvāna, nimantetvā mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Santharitvāna taṃ pupphaṃ, abhinesiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ me atthi sake gehe, āmisaṃ paccupaṭṭhitaṃ;
```

```
Tāhaṃ buddhassa pādāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Bhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya, pupphahatthamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Anumoditvāna sabbaññū, pakkāmi uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="V" n="1.0162" /> kappe, yaṃ pupphamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Anantaraṃ ito kappe, rājāhuṃ varadassano;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0231" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kusumāsaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kusumāsaniyattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Phaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Himavantassāvidūre, vasāmi assame ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Aggihuttañca me atthi, puṇḍarīkaphalāni ca;
```

```
Puṭake nikkhipitvāna, dumagge laggitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="1.0177" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0161" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mamuddharitukāmo so, bhikkhanto mamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, phalaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Vittisañjanano mayhaṃ, diṭṭhadhammasukhāvaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo sambuddho, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā phaladānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ nupapajjasi’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva <pb ed="T" n="1.0232" /> sukkamūlena, anubhotvāna sampadā;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Ito sattasate kappe, rājā āsiṃ sumaṅgalo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0163" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0162" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Phaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Ñāṇasaññikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate himavantamhi, vasāmi pabbatantare;
```

```
Pulinaṃ sobhanaṃ disvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Ñāṇe upanidhā natthi, saṅkhāraṃ <note>saṅgāmaṃ (sī. syā.), saṅkhātaṃ (theragāthā aṭṭha.)</note> natthi satthuno;
```

```
Sabbadhammaṃ abhiññāya, ñāṇena adhimuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Namo te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Ñāṇena te samo natthi, yāvatā ñāṇamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Ñāṇe cittaṃ pasādetvā, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ;
```

```
Avasesesu kappesu, kusalaṃ caritaṃ <note>karitaṃ (sī. syā.), kiriyaṃ (ka.)</note> mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="T" n="1.0233" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0178" /> kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Ito sattatikappamhi <note>tesattatikappe (sī. syā.)</note>, eko pulinapupphiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇasaññiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ñāṇasaññikattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Gaṇṭhipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo sambuddho, vipassī dakkhiṇāraho;
```

```
Purakkhato sāvakehi, ārāmā abhinikkhami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Disvānahaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ, sabbaññuṃ tamanāsakaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, gaṇṭhipupphaṃ <note>gatamaggaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> apūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="1.0164" /> cittappasādena, dvipadindassa tādino;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, puna vandiṃ tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatālīsito <pb ed="T" n="1.0234" /> kappe, caraṇo nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gaṇṭhipupphiyo <note>gandhapupphiyo (syā. ka.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Gaṇṭhipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Padumapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="M" n="1.0179" />, gotamo nāma pabbato;
```

```
Nānārukkhehi sañchanno, mahābhūtagaṇālayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Vemajjhamhi ca tassāsi, assamo abhinimmito;
```

```
Purakkhato sasissehi, vasāmi assame ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Āyantu <pb ed="P" n="1.0163" /> me sissagaṇā, padumaṃ āharantu me;
```

```
Buddhapūjaṃ karissāmi, dvipadindassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Evanti te paṭissutvā, padumaṃ āhariṃsu me;
```

```
Tathā nimittaṃ katvāhaṃ, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Sisse tadā samānetvā, sādhukaṃ anusāsahaṃ;
```

```
Mā kho tumhe pamajjittha, appamādo sukhāvaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0235" /> samanusāsitvā, te sisse vacanakkhame;
```

```
Appamādaguṇe yutto, tadā kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapaññāsakappamhi, rājā āsiṃ jaluttamo;
```

```
Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0165" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Padumapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Sereyyavaggo terasamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sereyyako pupphathūpi, pāyaso gandhathomako;
```

```
Āsani phalasaññī ca, gaṇṭhipadumapupphiyo;
```

```
Pañcuttarasatā gāthā, gaṇitā atthadassibhi.
```

### 14. Sobhitavaggo

#### 1. Sobhitattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="1.0236" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0180" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0166" /> nāma jino, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Mahato janakāyassa, deseti amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, vācāsabhimudīritaṃ <note>vācāsabhimudīrayiṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, ekaggo āsahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="P" n="1.0164" /> samuddo udadhīnamaggo, nerū nagānaṃ pavaro siluccayo;
```

```
Tatheva ye cittavasena vattare, na buddhañāṇassa kalaṃ upenti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammavidhiṃ <note>dhamme vidhiṃ (sī.)</note> ṭhapetvāna, buddho kāruṇiko isi;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo so ñāṇaṃ pakittesi, buddhamhi lokanāyake;
```

```
Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ, duggatiṃ na gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kilese jhāpayitvāna, ekaggo susamāhito;
```

```
Sobhito nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Paññāse <pb ed="T" n="1.0237" /> kappasahasse, sattevāsuṃ yasuggatā <note>samuggatā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sobhito thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sobhitattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Sudassanattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Vinatā <pb ed="M" n="1.0181" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0167" /> nadiyā <note>vitthatāya nadiyā (syā.)</note> tīre, pilakkhu <note>pilakkho (sī. theragāthā aṭṭha.)</note> phalito ahu;
```

```
Tāhaṃ rukkhaṃ gavesanto, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ketakaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, vaṇṭe chetvānahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Yena ñāṇena pattosi, accutaṃ amataṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ ñāṇaṃ abhipūjemi, buddhaseṭṭha mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Ñāṇamhi pūjaṃ katvāna, pilakkhumaddasaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Paṭiladdhomhi taṃ paññaṃ <note>taṃ saññaṃ (syā.), taṃ puññaṃ (ka.)</note>, ñāṇapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse <pb ed="P" n="1.0165" /> ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="T" n="1.0238" /> terasakappamhi, dvādasāsuṃ phaluggatā;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, cakkavattī mahapphalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sudassano thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sudassanattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Candanapūjanakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre, ahosiṃ kinnaro tadā;
```

```
Pupphabhakkho cahaṃ āsiṃ, pupphānivasano tathā <note>pupphānaṃ vasano ahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī tu bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Vipinaggena niyyāsi, haṃsarājāva ambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Namo te purisājañña, cittaṃ te suvisodhitaṃ;
```

```
Pasannamukhavaṇṇosi, vippasannamukhindriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Orohitvāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0182" /> ākāsā, bhūripañño sumedhaso;
```

```
Saṅghāṭiṃ pattharitvāna, pallaṅkena upāvisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Vilīnaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0168" /> candanādāya, agamāsiṃ jinantikaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Abhivādetvāna <pb ed="T" n="1.0239" /> sambuddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna, pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, candanaṃ yaṃ apūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Catuddase kappasate, ito āsiṃsu te tayo;
```

```
Rohaṇī nāma <note>rohitā nāma (sī.), rohiṇī nāma (syā.)</note> nāmena, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā candanapūjanako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Candanapūjanakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

Aṭṭhamabhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 4. Pupphacchadaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Sunando <pb ed="P" n="1.0166" /> nāma nāmena, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
```

```
Ajjhāyako yācayogo, vājapeyyaṃ ayājayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, aggo kāruṇiko isi;
```

```
Janataṃ anukampanto, ambare caṅkamī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Caṅkamitvāna sambuddho, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
```

```
Mettāya aphari satte, appamāṇe <note>appamāṇaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> nirūpadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṇṭe <pb ed="T" n="1.0240" /> chetvāna pupphāni, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
```

```
Sabbe sisse samānetvā, ākāse ukkhipāpayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā <pb ed="M" n="1.0183" /> nagaraṃ āsi, pupphānaṃ chadanaṃ tadā;
```

```
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, sattāhaṃ na vigacchatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva sukkamūlena, anubhotvāna sampadā;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, tiṇṇo loke visattikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Ekārase <pb ed="V" n="1.0169" /> kappasate, pañcatiṃsāsu khattiyā;
```

```
Ambaraṃsasanāmā te, cakkavattī mahabbalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphacchadaniyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pupphacchadaniyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Rahosaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre, vasabho nāma pabbato;
```

```
Tasmiṃ pabbatapādamhi, assamo āsi māpito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Tīṇi sissasahassāni, vācesiṃ brāhmaṇo <note>brāhmaṇe (sī.)</note> tadā;
```

```
Saṃharitvāna <note>saṃsāvitvāna (syā.)</note> te sisse, ekamantaṃ upāvisiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Ekamantaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0241" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0167" /> nisīditvā, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
```

```
Buddhavedaṃ gavesanto <note>pavesanto (ka.)</note>, ñāṇe cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, nisīdiṃ paṇṇasanthare;
```

```
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

