```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0460" /> sudaṃ āyasmā sumanatālavaṇṭiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sumanatālavaṇṭiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Sumanadāmiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa bhagavato, nhātakassa tapassino;
```

```
Katvāna sumanadāmaṃ, dhārayiṃ purato ṭhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dāmaṃ dhārayiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sumanadhāraṇe phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0340" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanadāmiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sumanadāmiyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Kāsumāriphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva <pb ed="T" n="1.0461" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0294" /> jotantaṃ, nisinnaṃ pabbatantare;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto <pb ed="V" n="1.0322" /> sumano, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Kāsumāriphalaṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kāsumāriphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kāsumāriphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Bodhivandanavaggo aṭṭhatiṃsatimo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Bodhi pāṭali uppalī, paṭṭi ca sattapaṇṇiyo;
```

```
Gandhamuṭṭhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0462" /> ca citako, tālaṃ sumanadāmako;
```

```
Kāsumāriphalī ceva, gāthā ekūnasaṭṭhikā.
```

### 39. Avaṭaphalavaggo

#### 1. Avaṭaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Sataraṃsi <pb ed="M" n="1.0341" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0323" /> nāma bhagavā, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, gocarāyābhinikkhami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Phalahattho ahaṃ disvā, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, avaṭaṃ <note>avaṇṭaṃ (sī.), ambaṭaṃ (syā.)</note> adadiṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="1.0295" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0463" /> sudaṃ āyasmā avaṭaphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Avaṭaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Labujadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, āsiṃ ārāmiko tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Labujassa phalaṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Ākāse ṭhitako santo, paṭigaṇhi mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Vittisañjananaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0324" /> mayhaṃ, diṭṭhadhammasukhāvahaṃ;
```

```
Phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Adhigacchiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0342" /> tadā pītiṃ, vipulañca sukhuttamaṃ;
```

```
Uppajjateva ratanaṃ, nibbattassa tahiṃ tahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="1.0464" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā labujadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Labujadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Udumbaraphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Vinatānadiyā tīre, vihāsi purisuttamo;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmiṃ pasannamānaso, kilesamaladhovane;
```

```
Udumbaraphalaṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0465" /> sudaṃ āyasmā udumbaraphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Udumbaraphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Pilakkhaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Vanantare <pb ed="M" n="1.0343" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0325" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0296" /> buddhaṃ disvā, atthadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, pilakkhassādadiṃ phalaṃ <note>pilakkhassa phalaṃ adaṃ (sī.), pilakkhussa phalaṃ adaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

Pilakkhaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

```
Phalamanvesamānā te, alabhiṃsu phalaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0467" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0326" /> sambuddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva jalitaṃ, puṇṇamāyeva <note>puṇṇamāseva (sī. ka.)</note> candimaṃ;
```

```
Jalantaṃ dīparukkhaṃva, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Kadaliphalaṃ paggayha, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, vanditvāna apakkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse <pb ed="T" n="1.0468" /> ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kadaliphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kadaliphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Panasaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjuno <pb ed="M" n="1.0345" /> nāma sambuddho, himavante vasī tadā;
```

```
Caraṇena ca sampanno, samādhikusalo muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhamattaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0327" /> gahetvāna, panasaṃ jīvajīvakaṃ <note>devagandhikaṃ (41 vagge, 5 apadāne)</note>;
```

```
Chattapaṇṇe ṭhapetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0469" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā panasaphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Panasaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Soṇakoṭivīsattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassino <pb ed="P" n="1.0298" /> pāvacane, ekaṃ leṇaṃ mayā kataṃ;
```

```
Cātuddisassa saṅghassa, bandhumārājadhāniyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Dussehi bhūmiṃ leṇassa, santharitvā pariccajiṃ;
```

```
Udaggacitto sumano, akāsiṃ paṇidhiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Ārādhayeyyaṃ sambuddhaṃ, pabbajjañca labheyyahaṃ;
```

```
Anuttarañca nibbānaṃ, phuseyyaṃ santimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva sukkamūlena, kappe <note>kappaṃ (sī.), kappa (ka.)</note> navuti saṃsariṃ;
```

```
Devabhūto manusso ca, katapuñño virocahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="1.0470" /> kammāvasesena, idha pacchimake bhave;
```

```
Campāyaṃ aggaseṭṭhissa, jātomhi ekaputtako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Jātamattassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0346" /> me sutvā, pitu chando ayaṃ ahu;
```

```
Dadāmahaṃ kumārassa, vīsakoṭī anūnakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Caturaṅgulā ca me lomā, jātā pādatale ubho;
```

```
Sukhumā mudusamphassā, tūlāpicusamā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Atītā navuti kappā, ayaṃ eko ca uttari;
```

```
Nābhijānāmi nikkhitte, pāde bhūmyā asanthate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Ārādhito <pb ed="V" n="1.0328" /> me sambuddho, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Arahattañca me pattaṃ, sītibhūtomhi nibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Aggo āraddhavīriyānaṃ, niddiṭṭho sabbadassinā;
```

```
Khīṇāsavomhi arahā, chaḷabhiñño mahiddhiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, leṇadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Thero <pb ed="T" n="1.0471" /> koṭivīso <note>koṭiviso (syā. ka.), koḷiviso (aññaṭṭhānesu)</note> soṇo, bhikkhusaṅghassa aggato;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, anotatte mahāsare’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇo koṭivīso thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Soṇakoṭivīsattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Pubbakammapilotikabuddhaapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Anotattasarāsanne<pb ed="P" n="1.0299" />, ramaṇīye silātale;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, nānāgandhavanantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena, pareto <note>upeto (udānaṭṭhakathāyaṃ 4 vagge, 8 sutte)</note> lokanāyako;
```

```
Āsīno byākarī tattha, pubbakammāni attano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
<note>suṇātha bhikkhave mayhaṃ, yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā; ekaṃ araññikaṃ bhikkhuṃ, disvā dinnaṃ pilotikaṃ; patthitaṃ paṭhamaṃ buddhaṃ, buddhattāya mayā tadā; pilotiyassa kammassa, buddhattepi vipaccati; gopālako pure āsiṃ, gāviṃ pājeti gocaraṃ; pivantiṃ udakaṃ āvilaṃ, gāviṃ disvā nivārayiṃ; tena kammavipākena, idha pacchimake bhave; vipāsito yadicchakaṃ, na hi pātuṃ labhāmahaṃ (syā.)</note> ‘‘Suṇātha <pb ed="M" n="1.0347" /> bhikkhavo mayhaṃ, yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
```

```
Pilotikassa kammassa, buddhattepi vipaccati <note>suṇātha bhikkhave mayhaṃ, yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā; ekaṃ araññikaṃ bhikkhuṃ, disvā dinnaṃ pilotikaṃ; patthitaṃ paṭhamaṃ buddhaṃ, buddhattāya mayā tadā; pilotiyassa kammassa, buddhattepi vipaccati; gopālako pure āsiṃ, gāviṃ pājeti gocaraṃ; pivantiṃ udakaṃ āvilaṃ, gāviṃ disvā nivārayiṃ; tena kammavipākena, idha pacchimake bhave; vipāsito yadicchakaṃ, na hi pātuṃ labhāmahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

[1]

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Munāḷi <pb ed="T" n="1.0472" /> nāmahaṃ dhutto, pubbe aññāsu jātisu <note>aññāya jātiyā (udāna aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Paccekabuddhaṃ surabhiṃ <note>sarabhuṃ (sī.)</note>, abbhācikkhiṃ adūsakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ;
```

```
Bahūvassasahassāni, dukkhaṃ vedesi vedanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammāvasesena, idha pacchimake bhave;
```

```
Abbhakkhānaṃ mayā laddhaṃ, sundarikāya kāraṇā.
```

[2]

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbābhibhussa <pb ed="V" n="1.0329" /> buddhassa, nando nāmāsi sāvako;
```

```
Taṃ abbhakkhāya niraye, ciraṃ saṃsaritaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Dasavassasahassāni, niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ;
```

```
Manussabhāvaṃ laddhāhaṃ, abbhakkhānaṃ bahuṃ labhiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammāvasesena, ciñcamānavikā mamaṃ;
```

```
Abbhācikkhi abhūtena, janakāyassa aggato.
```

[3]

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Brāhmaṇo sutavā āsiṃ, ahaṃ sakkatapūjito;
```

```
Mahāvane pañcasate, mante vācemi māṇave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthāgato <pb ed="M" n="1.0348" /> <note>tamāgato (ka.)</note> isi bhīmo, pañcābhiñño mahiddhiko;
```

```
Taṃ cāhaṃ āgataṃ disvā, abbhācikkhiṃ adūsakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Tatohaṃ avacaṃ sisse, kāmabhogī ayaṃ isi;
```

```
Mayhampi bhāsamānassa, anumodiṃsu māṇavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Tato māṇavakā sabbe, bhikkhamānaṃ kule kule;
```

```
Mahājanassa āhaṃsu, kāmabhogī ayaṃ isi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="1.0473" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0300" /> kammavipākena, pañca bhikkhusatā ime;
```

```
Abbhakkhānaṃ labhuṃ sabbe, sundarikāya kāraṇā.
```

[4]

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Vemātubhātaraṃ pubbe, dhanahetu haniṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pakkhipiṃ giriduggasmiṃ, silāya ca apiṃsayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, devadatto silaṃ khipi;
```

```
Aṅguṭṭhaṃ piṃsayī pāde, mama pāsāṇasakkharā.
```

[5]

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Purehaṃ dārako hutvā, kīḷamāno mahāpathe;
```

```
Paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna, magge sakalikaṃ <note>sakkhalikaṃ (ka.)</note> khipiṃ <note>dahiṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, idha pacchimake bhave;
```

```
Vadhatthaṃ maṃ devadatto, abhimāre payojayi.
```

[6]

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthāroho <pb ed="V" n="1.0330" /> pure āsiṃ, paccekamunimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Piṇḍāya vicarantaṃ taṃ, āsādesiṃ gajenahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, bhanto <note>danto (ka.)</note> nāḷāgirī gajo;
```

```
Giribbaje puravare, dāruṇo samupāgami <note>maṃ upāgami (sī.)</note>.
```

[7]

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Rājāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0349" /> patthivo <note>pattiko (syā. ka.), khattiyo (udāna aṭṭha.)</note> āsiṃ, sattiyā purisaṃ haniṃ;
```

```
Tena kammavipākena, niraye paccisaṃ bhusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Kammuno tassa sesena, idāni sakalaṃ mama;
```

```
Pāde chaviṃ pakappesi <note>pakopesi (sī.)</note>, na hi kammaṃ vinassati.
```

[8]

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ kevaṭṭagāmasmiṃ, ahuṃ kevaṭṭadārako;
```

```
Macchake ghātite disvā, janayiṃ somanassakaṃ <note>somanassahaṃ (udāna aṭṭha.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="1.0474" /> kammavipākena, sīsadukkhaṃ ahū mama;
```

```
Sabbe sakkā ca haññiṃsu, yadā hani viṭaṭūbho <note>viṭaṭubho (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

[9]

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Phussassāhaṃ pāvacane, sāvake paribhāsayiṃ;
```

```
Yavaṃ khādatha bhuñjatha, mā ca bhuñjatha sālayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, temāsaṃ khāditaṃ yavaṃ;
```

```
Nimantito brāhmaṇena, verañjāyaṃ vasiṃ tadā.
```

[10]

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbuddhe vattamānamhi, mallaputtaṃ niheṭhayiṃ <note>nisedhayiṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tena kammavipākena, piṭṭhidukkhaṃ ahū mama.
```

[11]

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Tikicchako ahaṃ āsiṃ, seṭṭhiputtaṃ virecayiṃ;
```

```
Tena kammavipākena, hoti pakkhandikā mama.
```

[12]

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Avacāhaṃ jotipālo, sugataṃ kassapaṃ tadā;
```

```
Kuto nu bodhi muṇḍassa, bodhi paramadullabhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="1.0350" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0331" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0301" /> kammavipākena, acariṃ dukkaraṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Chabbassānuruveḷāyaṃ, tato bodhimapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ etena maggena, pāpuṇiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Kummaggena gavesissaṃ, pubbakammena vārito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Puññapāpaparikkhīṇo, sabbasantāpavajjito;
```

```
Asoko anupāyāso, nibbāyissamanāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ jino viyākāsi, bhikkhusaṅghassa aggato;
```

```
Sabbābhiññābalappatto, anotatte mahāsare’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0475" /> sudaṃ bhagavā attano pubbacaritaṃ kammapilotikaṃ nāma buddhāpadānadhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthāti.

Pubbakammapilotikaṃ nāma buddhāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Avaṭaphalavaggo ekūnacattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Avaṭaṃ labujañceva, udumbarapilakkhu ca;
```

```
Phāru vallī ca kadalī, panaso koṭivīsako.
```

```
Pubbakammapiloti ca, apadānaṃ mahesino;
```

```
Gāthāyo ekanavuti, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
```

Cuddasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

### 40. Pilindavacchavaggo

#### 1. Pilindavacchattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="T" n="1.0476" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0351" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0332" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0302" /> haṃsavatiyā, āsiṃ dovāriko ahaṃ;
```

```
Akkhobhaṃ amitaṃ bhogaṃ, ghare sannicitaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Rahogato nisīditvā, pahaṃsitvāna mānasaṃ <note>sampahaṃsitva mānasaṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Nisajja pāsādavare, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā.
```

(Cintanākāro)

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bahū medhigatā bhogā, phītaṃ antepuraṃ mama;
```

```
Rājāpi <note>rājisi (ka.)</note> sannimantesi, ānando pathavissaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ayañca buddho uppanno, adhiccuppattiko muni;
```

```
Saṃvijjanti ca me bhogā, dānaṃ dassāmi satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padumena rājaputtena, dinnaṃ dānavaraṃ jine;
```

```
Hatthināge ca pallaṅke, apassenañcanappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ahampi dānaṃ dassāmi, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Adinnapubbamaññesaṃ, bhavissaṃ ādikammiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cintetvāhaṃ bahuvidhaṃ, yāge yassa sukhaṃphalaṃ;
```

```
Parikkhāradānamaddakkhiṃ, mama saṅkappapūraṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘‘Parikkhārāni dassāmi, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Adinnapubbamaññesaṃ, bhavissaṃ ādikammiko’.
```

(Dānavatthusampādanaṃ)

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Naḷakāre <pb ed="T" n="1.0477" /> upāgamma, chattaṃ kāresi tāvade;
```

```
Chattasatasahassāni, ekato sannipātayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Dussasatasahassāni, ekato sannipātayiṃ;
```

```
Pattasatasahassāni, ekato sannipātayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Vāsiyo <pb ed="M" n="1.0352" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0333" /> satthake cāpi, sūciyo nakhachedane;
```

```
Heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapāpesiṃ, kāretvā tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Vidhūpane tālavaṇṭe, morahatthe ca cāmare;
```

```
Parissāvane teladhāre <note>teladhare (sī.)</note>, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Sūcighare aṃsabaddhe, athopi kāyabandhane;
```

```
Ādhārake ca sukate, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Paribhogabhājane ca, athopi lohathālake;
```

```
Bhesajje <pb ed="P" n="1.0303" /> pūrayitvāna, heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Vacaṃ usīraṃ laṭṭhimadhuṃ, pipphalī maricāni ca;
```

```
Harītakiṃ siṅgīveraṃ, sabbaṃ pūresi bhājane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Upāhanā pādukāyo, atho udakapuñchane;
```

```
Kattaradaṇḍe sukate, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Osadhañjananāḷī ca <note>osadhaṃ añjanāpica (syā.)</note>, salākā dhammakuttarā;
```

```
Kuñcikā pañcavaṇṇehi, sibbite kuñcikāghare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Āyoge dhūmanette ca, athopi dīpadhārake;
```

```
Tumbake ca karaṇḍe ca, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Saṇḍāse <pb ed="T" n="1.0478" /> pipphale ceva, athopi malahārake;
```

```
Bhesajjathavike ceva, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Āsandiyo pīṭhake ca, pallaṅke caturomaye;
```

```
Tadanucchave kārayitvā, heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Uṇṇābhisī tūlabhisī, athopi pīṭhikābhisī <note>pīṭhakābhisī (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Bimbohane <note>bibbohane (syā. ka.)</note> ca sukate, kārayiṃ tadanucchave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Kuruvinde madhusitthe, telaṃ hatthappatāpakaṃ;
```

```
Sipāṭiphalake sucī, mañcaṃ attharaṇena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Senāsane pādapuñche, sayanāsanadaṇḍake;
```

```
Dantapoṇe ca āṭalī <note>kathaliṃ (syā.)</note>, sīsālepanagandhake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Araṇī <pb ed="M" n="1.0353" /> phalapīṭhe <note>palālapīṭhe (sī.)</note> ca, pattapidhānathālake;
```

```
Udakassa kaṭacchū ca, cuṇṇakaṃ rajanambaṇaṃ <note>rajanammaṇaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Sammajjanaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0334" /> <note>sammuñjanaṃ (syā.), sammajjaniṃ, sammuñjaniṃ (?)</note> udapattaṃ, tathā vassikasāṭikaṃ;
```

```
Nisīdanaṃ kaṇḍucchādi, atha antaravāsakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Uttarāsaṅgasaṅghāṭī, natthukaṃ mukhasodhanaṃ;
```

```
Biḷaṅgaloṇaṃ pahūtañca <note>loṇabhūtañca (ka.)</note>, madhuñca dadhipānakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Dhūpaṃ <note>dhūmaṃ (ka.)</note> sitthaṃ pilotiñca, mukhapuñchanasuttakaṃ;
```

```
Dātabbaṃ nāma yaṃ atthi, yañca kappati satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbametaṃ samānetvā, ānandaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ;
```

```
Upasaṅkamma <pb ed="P" n="1.0304" /> rājānaṃ, janetāraṃ mahesino <note>mahesinaṃ (sī.), mahāyasaṃ (syā.), mahissaraṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sirasā <pb ed="T" n="1.0479" /> abhivādetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

(Dānokāsayācanā)

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ekato jātasaṃvaddhā, ubhinnaṃ ekato manaṃ <note>yaso (syā.), mano (?)</note>;
```

```
Sādhāraṇā sukhadukkhe, ubho ca anuvattakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atthi cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ, tavādheyyaṃ arindama;
```

```
Yadi sakkosi taṃ dukkhaṃ, vinodeyyāsi khattiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tava dukkhaṃ mama dukkhaṃ, ubhinnaṃ ekato mano <note>manaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Niṭṭhitanti vijānāhi, mamādheyyaṃ sace tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘‘Jānāhi kho mahārāja, dukkhaṃ me dubbinodayaṃ;
```

```
Pahu samāno gajjasu, ekaṃ te duccajaṃ varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā vijite atthi, yāvatā mama jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Etehi yadi te attho, dassāmi avikampito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gajjitaṃ kho tayā deva, micchā taṃ bahu gajjitaṃ;
```

```
Jānissāmi tuvaṃ ajja, sabbadhamme <note>saccadhamme (?)</note> patiṭṭhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atibāḷhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0354" /> nipīḷesi, dadamānassa me sato;
```

```
Kiṃ te me pīḷitenattho, patthitaṃ te kathehi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘‘Icchāmahaṃ mahārāja, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Bhojayissāmi sambuddhaṃ, vajjaṃ <note>vañcuṃ (?)</note> me māhu jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aññaṃ tehaṃ varaṃ dammi, mā yācittho tathāgataṃ <note>ayācito tathāgato (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Adeyyo kassaci buddho, maṇi jotiraso yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nanu <pb ed="V" n="1.0335" /> te gajjitaṃ deva, yāva jīvitamattano <note>vijitamatthitaṃ (ka.), jīvitamatthikaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Jīvitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0480" /> <note>vijitaṃ (ka.)</note> dadamānena, yuttaṃ dātuṃ tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ṭhapanīyo mahāvīro, adeyyo kassaci jino;
```

```
Na me paṭissuto buddho, varassu amitaṃ dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vinicchayaṃ pāpuṇāma, pucchissāma vinicchaye;
```

```
Yathāsaṇṭhaṃ <note>yathāsantaṃ (sī.)</note> kathessanti, paṭipucchāma taṃ tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rañño hatthe gahetvāna, agamāsiṃ vinicchayaṃ;
```

```
Purato akkhadassānaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘Suṇantu <pb ed="P" n="1.0305" /> me akkhadassā, rājā varamadāsi me;
```

```
Na kiñci ṭhapayitvāna, jīvitampi <note>vijitaṃpi (ka.)</note> pavārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa me varadinnassa, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ variṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Sudinno hoti me buddho, chindatha saṃsayaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sossāma tava vacanaṃ, bhūmipālassa rājino;
```

```
Ubhinnaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, chindissāmettha saṃsayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbaṃ deva tayā dinnaṃ, imassa sabbagāhikaṃ <note>sabbagāhitaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Na kiñci ṭhapayitvāna, jīvitampi pavārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kicchappattova hutvāna, yācī varamanuttaraṃ <note>yāvajīvamanuttaraṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Imaṃ sudukkhitaṃ ñatvā, adāsiṃ sabbagāhikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘‘Parājayo <pb ed="M" n="1.0355" /> tuvaṃ <note>tavaṃ (sī.)</note> deva, assa deyyo tathāgato;
```

```
Ubhinnaṃ saṃsayo chinno, yathāsaṇṭhamhi <note>yathāsantamhi (sī.)</note> tiṭṭhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rājā tattheva ṭhatvāna, akkhadassetadabravi;
```

```
Sammā <pb ed="T" n="1.0481" /> mayhampi deyyātha, puna buddhaṃ labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pūretvā tava saṅkappaṃ, bhojayitvā tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Puna deyyāsi <note>deyyātha (ka.)</note> sambuddhaṃ, ānandassa yasassino’.
```

(Nimantanakathā)

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhadassebhivādetvā, ānandañcāpi khattiyaṃ;
```

```
Tuṭṭho pamudito hutvā, sambuddhamupasaṅkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Sirasā abhivādetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘Vasīsatasahassehi<pb ed="V" n="1.0336" />, adhivāsehi cakkhuma;
```

```
Hāsayanto mama cittaṃ, nivesanamupehi me’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, adhivāsesi cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Adhivāsanamaññāya, abhivādiya satthuno;
```

```
Haṭṭho udaggacittohaṃ, nivesanamupāgamiṃ.
```

(Dānapaṭiyādanaṃ)

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Mittāmacce samānetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
```

```
‘Sudullabho mayā laddho, maṇi jotiraso yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kena taṃ pūjayissāma, appameyyo anūpamo;
```

```
Atulo asamo dhīro, jino appaṭipuggalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tathāsamasamo ceva, adutiyo narāsabho;
```

```
Dukkaraṃ adhikārañhi, buddhānucchavikaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nānāpupphe <pb ed="P" n="1.0306" /> samānetvā, karoma pupphamaṇḍapaṃ;
```

```
Buddhānucchavikaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0482" /> etaṃ, sabbapūjā bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Uppalaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0356" /> padumaṃ vāpi, vassikaṃ adhimuttakaṃ <note>atimuttakaṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Campakaṃ <note>candanaṃ (ka.)</note> nāgapupphañca, maṇḍapaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Satāsanasahassāni, chattacchāyāya paññapiṃ;
```

```
Pacchimaṃ āsanaṃ mayhaṃ, adhikaṃ satamagghati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Satāsanasahassāni, chattacchāyāya paññapiṃ;
```

```
Paṭiyādetvā annapānaṃ, kālaṃ ārocayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Ārocitamhi kālamhi, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, nivesanamupesi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Dhārentaṃ uparicchattaṃ <note>dhārentamuparicchatte (sī.)</note>, suphullapupphamaṇḍape;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Chattasatasahassāni, satasahassamāsanaṃ;
```

```
Kappiyaṃ anavajjañca, paṭigaṇhāhi cakkhuma’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mamaṃ tāretukāmo so, sampaṭicchi mahāmuni.
```

(Dānakathā)

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhuno <pb ed="V" n="1.0337" /> ekamekassa, paccekaṃ pattamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Jahiṃsu sumbhakaṃ <note>pubbakaṃ (sī.), sambhataṃ (syā.), mattikaṃ (?)</note> pattaṃ, lohapattaṃ adhārayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Sattarattindivaṃ buddho, nisīdi pupphamaṇḍape;
```

```
Bodhayanto bahū satte, dhammacakkaṃ pavattayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammacakkaṃ pavattento, heṭṭhato pupphamaṇḍape;
```

```
Cullāsītisahassānaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0483" />, dhammābhisamayo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Sattame divase patte, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Chattacchāyāyamāsīno, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

(Byākaraṇaṃ)

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anūnakaṃ dānavaraṃ, yo me pādāsi māṇavo;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthī <pb ed="M" n="1.0357" /> assā rathā pattī, senā ca caturaṅginī;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ <note>taṃ (syā.)</note> niccaṃ, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, sivikā sandamānikā;
```

```
Upaṭṭhissantimaṃ niccaṃ, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi rathasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="P" n="1.0307" /> tūriyasahassāni, bheriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Vajjayissantimaṃ niccaṃ, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘‘Chaḷāsītisahassāni, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā <note>āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0484" /> vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devaloke <pb ed="V" n="1.0338" /> vasantassa, puññakammasamaṅgino;
```

```
Devalokapariyantaṃ, ratanachattaṃ dharissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘‘Icchissati yadā chāyaṃ <note>yadā vāyaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>, chadanaṃ dussapupphajaṃ;
```

```
Imassa cittamaññāya, nibaddhaṃ chādayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyutto, brahmabandhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena <note>nāmena (sabbattha) evamuparipi; aṭṭhathāyaṃ pana pubbe gottenātipadaṃ vaṇṇitaṃ</note>, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pilindavacchanāmena <pb ed="M" n="1.0358" /> <note>pilindivacchanāmena (sī.)</note>, hessati satthusāvako;
```

```
Devānaṃ asurānañca, gandhabbānañca sakkato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnañca, gihīnañca tatheva so;
```

```
Piyo hutvāna sabbesaṃ, viharissatināsavo’.
```

(Dānānisaṃsakathā)

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
```

```
Sumutto saravegova, kilese jhāpayī mama <note>jhāpayissati (sī. ka.), jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ, puññakkhette anuttare;
```

```
Yattha kāraṃ karitvāna, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Anūnakaṃ dānavaraṃ, adāsi yo <note>so (ka.)</note> hi māṇavo;
```

```
Ādipubbaṅgamo <pb ed="T" n="1.0485" /> āsi, tassa dānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

(1. Chattānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Chatte ca sugate datvā <note>chatte sugate datvāna (sī. syā.)</note>, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Sītaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0308" /> uṇhaṃ na jānāmi, rajojallaṃ na limpati;
```

```
Anupaddavo anīti ca, homi apacito sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhumacchaviko homi, visadaṃ hoti mānasaṃ;
```

```
Chattasatasahassāni, bhave saṃsarato mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbālaṅkārayuttāni<pb ed="V" n="1.0339" />, tassa kammassa vāhasā;
```

```
Imaṃ jātiṃ ṭhapetvāna, matthake dhārayanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Kasmā <note>tasmā (syā. ka.)</note> imāya jātiyā, natthi me chattadhāraṇā;
```

```
Mama sabbaṃ kataṃ kammaṃ, vimuttichattapattiyā.
```

(2. Dussānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Dussāni sugate datvā, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo <pb ed="M" n="1.0359" /> virajo, sappabhāso patāpavā;
```

```
Siniddhaṃ hoti me gattaṃ, bhave saṃsarato mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Dussasatasahassāni, setā pītā ca lohitā;
```

```
Dhārenti matthake mayhaṃ, dussadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Koseyyakambaliyāni, khomakappāsikāni ca;
```

```
Sabbattha paṭilabhāmi, tesaṃ nissandato ahaṃ.
```

(3. Pattānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Patte sugate datvāna, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Dasānisaṃse <pb ed="T" n="1.0486" /> anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇathāle maṇithāle, rajatepi ca thālake;
```

```
Lohitaṅgamaye thāle, paribhuñjāmi sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Anupaddavo anīti ca, homi apacito sadā;
```

```
Lābhī annassa pānassa, vatthassa sayanassa ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Na vinassanti me bhogā, ṭhitacitto bhavāmahaṃ;
```

```
Dhammakāmo sadā homi, appakleso anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, anubandhā ime guṇā;
```

```
Chāyā yathāpi rukkhassa, sabbattha na jahanti maṃ.
```

(4. Vāsiānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Cittabandhanasambaddhā <note>cittabandhanasampannā (ka.)</note>, sukatā vāsiyo bahū;
```

```
Datvāna buddhaseṭṭhassa, saṅghassa ca tathevahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama;
```

```
Sūro <pb ed="P" n="1.0309" /> homavisārī ca, vesārajjesu pāramī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Dhitivīriyavā <pb ed="V" n="1.0340" /> homi, paggahītamano sadā;
```

```
Kilesacchedanaṃ ñāṇaṃ, sukhumaṃ atulaṃ suciṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha paṭilabhāmi, tassa nissandato ahaṃ.
```

(5. Satthakānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Akakkase <pb ed="M" n="1.0360" /> apharuse, sudhote satthake bahū;
```

```
Pasannacitto datvāna, buddhe saṅghe tatheva ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama;
```

```
Kalyāṇamittaṃ <note>kalyāṇacittaṃ (sī.)</note> vīriyaṃ, khantiñca mettasatthakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhāsallassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0487" /> chinnattā, paññāsatthaṃ anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Vajirena samaṃ ñāṇaṃ, tesaṃ nissandato labhe.
```

(6. Sūciānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Sūciyo sugate datvā, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Na saṃsayo kaṅkhacchedo, abhirūpo ca bhogavā;
```

```
Tikkhapañño sadā homi, saṃsaranto bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ, atthaṃ ñāṇena passayiṃ;
```

```
Vajiraggasamaṃ ñāṇaṃ, hoti me tamaghātanaṃ.
```

(7. Nakhacchedanānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Nakhacchedane sugate, datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame;
```

```
Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Dāsidāse <note>dāsidāsa (ka.)</note> gavasse ca, bhatake nāṭake <note>ārakkhake (sī.)</note> bahū;
```

```
Nhāpite bhattake sūde, sabbattheva labhāmahaṃ.
```

(8. Vidhūpanatālavaṇṭānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Vidhūpane sugate datvā, tālavaṇṭe ca sobhaṇe;
```

```
Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ na jānāmi, pariḷāho na vijjati;
```

```
Darathaṃ nābhijānāmi, cittasantāpanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Rāgaggi <pb ed="M" n="1.0361" /> dosamohaggi, mānaggi diṭṭhiaggi ca;
```

```
Sabbaggī nibbutā mayhaṃ, tassa nissandato mama.
```

(9. Morahattha-cāmaraṃ)

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Morahatthe <pb ed="V" n="1.0341" /> cāmariyo, datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame;
```

```
Upasantakilesohaṃ, viharāmi anaṅgaṇo.
```

(10. Parissāvana-dhammakaraṃ)

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Parissāvane <pb ed="T" n="1.0488" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0310" /> sugate, datvā dhammakaruttame <note>datvā sukate dhammakuttare (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbesaṃ samatikkamma, dibbaṃ āyuṃ labhāmahaṃ;
```

```
Appasayho sadā homi, corapaccatthikehi vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Satthena vā visena vā, vihesampi na kubbate;
```

```
Antarāmaraṇaṃ natthi, tesaṃ nissandato mama.
```

(11. Teladhārānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Teladhāre sugate datvā, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Sucārurūpo subhaddo <note>sugado (sī.), suvāco (?)</note>, susamuggatamānaso;
```

```
Avikkhittamano homi, sabbārakkhehi rakkhito.
```

(12. Sūcigharānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```

```

(13. Aṃsabaddhānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Aṃsabaddhe jine datvā, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Tīṇānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhamme <pb ed="M" n="1.0362" /> gādhaṃ <note>cetoñāṇaṃ ca (sī.)</note> vindāmi, sarāmi dutiyaṃ bhavaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha succhavī homi, tassa nissandato ahaṃ.
```

(14. Kāyabandhanānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Kāyabandhe jine datvā, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```

```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhīsu <pb ed="T" n="1.0489" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0342" /> na kampāmi, vasī homi samādhisu;
```

```
Abhejjapariso homi, ādeyyavacano sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhitasati homi, tāso mayhaṃ na vijjati;
```

```
Devaloke manusse vā, anubandhā ime guṇā.
```

(15. Ādhārakānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Ādhārake jine datvā, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Pañcavaṇṇehi dāyādo <note>pañcavaṇṇe bhayābhāvo (syā.)</note>, acalo homi kenaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="1.0311" /> keci me sutā dhammā, satiñāṇappabodhanā;
```

```
Dhatā <note>ṭhitā (ka.)</note> me na vinassanti, bhavanti suvinicchitā.
```

(16. Bhājanānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Bhājane paribhoge ca, datvā buddhe gaṇuttame;
```

```
Tīṇānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇamaye maṇimaye, athopi phalikāmaye;
```


<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Bhariyā dāsadāsī <note>sabbatthapi evameva dissati</note> ca, hatthissarathapattike;
```

```
Itthī patibbatā ceva, paribhogāni sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Vijjā mantapade ceva, vividhe āgame bahū;
```

```

```

(Sādhāraṇānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>


<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike <note>buddhaseṭṭhassa santike (?) evamuparipi; etadeva hi upālittherāpadānaṭṭhakathāyaṃ vaṇṇitaṃ</note>;
```

```

```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pilindavaccho thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pilindavacchattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Selattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, vīthisāmī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Mama ñātī samānetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, puññakkhetto anuttaro <note>puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Āsi so <note>āsīso (sī.), ādhāro (pī.)</note> sabbalokassa, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khattiyā negamā ceva, mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthārohā <pb ed="T" n="1.0498" /> anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘‘Uggā <pb ed="P" n="1.0317" /> ca rājaputtā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āḷārikā <pb ed="M" n="1.0371" /> kappakā <note>āḷārikā ca sūdā (syā.)</note> ca, nhāpakā mālakārakā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rajakā pesakārā ca, cammakārā ca nhāpitā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘‘Usukārā bhamakārā, cammakārā ca tacchakā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kammārā <pb ed="V" n="1.0350" /> soṇṇakārā ca, tipulohakarā tathā;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhatakā ceṭakā ceva, dāsakammakarā bahū;
```

```
Yathāsakena thāmena, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘‘Udahārā kaṭṭhahārā, kassakā tiṇahārakā;
```

```
Yathāsakena thāmena, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pupphikā mālikā ceva, paṇṇikā phalahārakā;
```

```
Yathāsakena thāmena, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gaṇikā kumbhadāsī ca, pūvikā <note>sūpikā (ka.)</note> macchikāpi ca;
```

```
Yathāsakena thāmena, pūgadhammaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etha <pb ed="T" n="1.0499" /> sabbe samāgantvā, gaṇaṃ bandhāma ekato;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ karissāma, puññakkhette anuttare’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Te me sutvāna vacanaṃ, gaṇaṃ bandhiṃsu tāvade;
```

```
Upaṭṭhānasālaṃ sukataṃ, bhikkhusaṅghassa kārayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘Niṭṭhāpetvāna taṃ sālaṃ, udaggo tuṭṭhamānaso;
```

```
Pareto tehi sabbehi, sambuddhamupasaṅkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ, lokanāthaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ime tīṇi satā vīra, purisā ekato gaṇā;
```

```
Upaṭṭhānasālaṃ sukataṃ, niyyādenti <note>niyyātenti (sī.)</note> tuvaṃ <note>tavaṃ (sī.), tava (syā.)</note> muni’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhusaṅghassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0372" /> purato, sampaṭicchatva cakkhumā;
```

```
Tiṇṇaṃ satānaṃ purato, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tisatāpi ca jeṭṭho ca, anuvattiṃsu ekato;
```

```
Sampattiñhi <note>sampattīhi (syā. ka.)</note> karitvāna, sabbe anubhavissatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="P" n="1.0318" /> bhave sampatte, sītibhāvamanuttaraṃ;
```

```
Ajaraṃ amataṃ santaṃ, nibbānaṃ phassayissatha’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ buddho viyākāsi, sabbaññū samaṇuttaro;
```

```
Buddhassa vacanaṃ sutvā, somanassaṃ pavedayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsa <pb ed="V" n="1.0351" /> kappasahassāni, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Devādhipo pañcasataṃ, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassakkhattuṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0500" /> rājā ca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Devarajjaṃ karontassa, mahādevā avandisuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Idha mānusake rajjaṃ <note>rajje (sī.)</note>, parisā honti bandhavā;
```

```
Pacchime bhave sampatte, vāseṭṭho nāma brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Asītikoṭi nicayo, tassa putto ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Selo iti mama nāmaṃ, chaḷaṅge pāramiṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, sasissehi purakkhato;
```

```
Jaṭābhārikabharitaṃ, keṇiyaṃ nāma tāpasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiyattāhutiṃ disvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
```

```
‘Āvāho vā vivāho vā, rājā vā te nimantito’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Āhutiṃ <note>nāhutiṃ (?)</note> yiṭṭhukāmohaṃ, brāhmaṇe devasammate;
```

```
Na nimantemi rājānaṃ, āhutī me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Na catthi mayhamāvāho, vivāho me na vijjati;
```

```
Sakyānaṃ nandijanano, seṭṭho loke sadevake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbalokahitatthāya, sabbasattasukhāvaho;
```

```
So me nimantito ajja, tassetaṃ paṭiyādanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘Timbarūsakavaṇṇābho<pb ed="M" n="1.0373" />, appameyyo anūpamo;
```

```
Rūpenāsadiso buddho, svātanāya nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Ukkāmukhapahaṭṭhova, khadiraṅgārasannibho;
```

```
Vijjūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbatagge <pb ed="T" n="1.0501" /> yathā acci, puṇṇamāyeva candimā;
```

```
Naḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāso, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Asambhīto bhayātīto, bhavantakaraṇo muni;
```

```
Sīhūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘Kusalo <pb ed="P" n="1.0319" /> buddhadhammehi, apasayho parehi so;
```

```
Nāgūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhammācārakusalo<pb ed="V" n="1.0352" />, buddhanāgo asādiso;
```

```
Usabhūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Anantavaṇṇo amitayaso, vicittasabbalakkhaṇo;
```

```
Sakkūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘Vasī gaṇī patāpī ca, tejassī ca durāsado;
```

```
Brahmūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘Pattadhammo dasabalo, balātibalapārago;
```

```
Dharaṇūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlavīcisamākiṇṇo, dhammaviññāṇakhobhito;
```

```
Udadhūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘Durāsado duppasaho, acalo uggato brahā;
```

```
Nerūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘Anantañāṇo asamasamo, atulo aggataṃ gato;
```

```
Gaganūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

Pannarasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘Patiṭṭhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0502" /> bhayabhītānaṃ, tāṇo saraṇagāminaṃ;
```

```
Assāsako mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘Āsayo <pb ed="M" n="1.0374" /> buddhimantānaṃ, puññakkhettaṃ sukhesinaṃ;
```

```
Ratanākaro mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘Assāsako vedakaro, sāmaññaphaladāyako;
```

```
Meghūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘Lokacakkhu mahātejo, sabbatamavinodano;
```

```
Sūriyūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘Ārammaṇavimuttīsu, sabhāvadassano muni;
```

```
Candūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho samussito loke, lakkhaṇehi alaṅkato;
```

```
Appameyyo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa ñāṇaṃ appameyyaṃ, sīlaṃ yassa anūpamaṃ;
```

```
Vimutti asadisā yassa, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa dhīti asadisā, thāmo yassa acintiyo;
```

```
Yassa parakkamo jeṭṭho, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘Rāgo <pb ed="V" n="1.0353" /> doso ca moho ca, visā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Agadūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘Klesabyādhibahudukkha <pb ed="P" n="1.0320" /> sabbatamavinodano <note>vinodako (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Vejjūpamo mahāvīro, so me buddho nimantito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhoti <pb ed="T" n="1.0503" /> bho yaṃ vadesi, ghosopeso sudullabho;
```

```
Buddho buddhoti sutvāna, pīti me udapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘Abbhantaraṃ agaṇhantaṃ, pīti me bahi nicchare;
```

```
Sohaṃ pītimano santo, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kahaṃ nu kho so bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Tattha gantvā namassissaṃ, sāmaññaphaladāyakaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paggayha dakkhiṇaṃ bāhuṃ, vedajāto katañjalī;
```

```
Ācikkhi me dhammarājaṃ, sokasallavinodanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘‘Udentaṃva <pb ed="M" n="1.0375" /> mahāmeghaṃ, nīlaṃ añjanasannibhaṃ;
```

```
Sāgaraṃ viya dissantaṃ, passasetaṃ mahāvanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ettha so vasate buddho, adantadamako muni;
```

```
Vinayanto ca veneyye, bodhento bodhipakkhiye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pipāsitova udakaṃ, bhojanaṃva jighacchito;
```

```
Gāvī yathā vacchagiddhā, evāhaṃ viciniṃ jinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ācāraupacāraññū, dhammānucchavisaṃvaraṃ;
```

```
Sikkhāpemi sake sisse, gacchante jinasantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘‘Durāsadā bhagavanto, sīhāva ekacārino;
```

```
Pade padaṃ nikkhipantā, āgaccheyyātha māṇavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āsīviso yathā ghoro, migarājāva kesarī;
```

```
Mattova kuñjaro dantī, evaṃ buddhā durāsadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ukkāsitañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0504" /> khipitaṃ, ajjhupekkhiya māṇavā;
```

```
Pade padaṃ nikkhipantā, upetha buddhasantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisallānagarukā, appasaddā durāsadā;
```

```
Durūpasaṅkamā buddhā, garū honti sadevake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadāhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0354" /> pañhaṃ pucchāmi, paṭisammodayāmi vā;
```

```
Appasaddā tadā hotha, munibhūtāva tiṭṭhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0321" /> so deseti sambuddho <note>saddhammaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, khemaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
```

```
Tamevatthaṃ nisāmetha, saddhammasavanaṃ sukhaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
‘‘Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ, sammodiṃ muninā ahaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ kathaṃ vītisāretvā, lakkhaṇe upadhārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘Lakkhaṇe dve ca kaṅkhāmi, passāmi tiṃsalakkhaṇe;
```

```
Kosohitavatthaguyhaṃ, iddhiyā dassayī muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Jivhaṃ ninnāmayitvāna, kaṇṇasote ca nāsike;
```

```
Paṭimasi nalāṭantaṃ, kevalaṃ chādayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0376" /> lakkhaṇe disvā, paripuṇṇe sabyañjane;
```

```
Buddhoti niṭṭhaṃ gantvāna, saha sissehi pabbajiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Satehi tīhi sahito, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Addhamāse asampatte, sabbe pattāmha nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘Ekato kammaṃ katvāna, puññakkhette anuttare;
```

```
Ekato saṃsaritvāna, ekato vinivattayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘Gopānasiyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0505" /> datvāna, pūgadhamme vasiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, aṭṭha hetū labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Disāsu pūjito homi, bhogā ca amitā mama;
```

```
Patiṭṭhā homi sabbesaṃ, tāso mama na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘Byādhayo me na vijjanti, dīghāyuṃ pālayāmi ca;
```

```
Sukhumacchaviko homi, āvāse patthite vase <note>āvāse patte vasse (syā.), āvāseva ṭhite vase (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭha gopānasī datvā, pūgadhamme vasiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Paṭisambhidārahattañca, etaṃ me aparaṭṭhamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbavositavosāno, katakicco anāsavo;
```

```
Aṭṭhagopānasī nāma, tava putto mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca thambhāni datvāna, pūgadhamme vasiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, pañca hetū labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Acalo <pb ed="V" n="1.0355" /> homi mettāya, anūnaṅgo bhavāmahaṃ;
```

```
Ādeyyavacano homi, na dhaṃsemi yathā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Abhantaṃ hoti me cittaṃ, akhilo homi kassaci;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, vimalo homi sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Sagāravo <pb ed="P" n="1.0322" /> sappatisso, katakicco anāsavo;
```

```
Sāvako te mahāvīra, bhikkhu taṃ vandate muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Katvā sukatapallaṅkaṃ, sālāyaṃ paññapesahaṃ;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, pañca hetū labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Ucce <pb ed="T" n="1.0506" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0377" /> kule pajāyitvā, mahābhogo bhavāmahaṃ;
```

```
Sabbasampattiko homi, maccheraṃ me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Gamane patthite mayhaṃ, pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati;
```

```
Saha pallaṅkaseṭṭhena, gacchāmi mama patthitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Tena pallaṅkadānena, tamaṃ sabbaṃ vinodayiṃ;
```

```
Sabbābhiññābalappatto, thero <note>selo (?)</note> vandati taṃ muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Parakiccattakiccāni, sabbakiccāni sādhayiṃ;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, pāvisiṃ abhayaṃ puraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Pariniṭṭhitasālamhi, paribhogamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, seṭṭhattaṃ ajjhupāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci damakā loke, hatthiasse damenti ye;
```

```
Karitvā kāraṇā nānā, dāruṇena damenti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Na hevaṃ tvaṃ mahāvīra, damesi naranāriyo;
```

```
Adaṇḍena asatthena, damesi uttame dame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Dānassa vaṇṇe kittento, desanākusalo muni;
```

```
Ekapañhaṃ kathentova, bodhesi tisate muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Dantā mayaṃ sārathinā, suvimuttā anāsavā;
```

```
Sabbābhiññābalapattā, nibbutā upadhikkhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Atikkantā bhayā sabbe, sālādānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="1.0356" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0507" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā selo sapariso bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Selattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Sabbakittikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva <pb ed="M" n="1.0378" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0323" /> jalitaṃ <note>jotantaṃ (sī.)</note>, dīparukkhaṃva ujjalaṃ <note>jotitaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Osadhiṃva virocantaṃ, vijjutaṃ gagane yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Asambhītaṃ anuttāsiṃ, migarājaṃva kesariṃ;
```

```
Ñāṇālokaṃ pakāsentaṃ, maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Uddharantaṃ imaṃ lokaṃ, chiddantaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃ;
```

```
Gajjantaṃ <note>asambhītaṃ (syā.), gacchantaṃ (ka.)</note> migarājaṃva, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṭājinadharo āsiṃ, brahā uju patāpavā;
```

```
Vākacīraṃ gahetvāna, pādamūle apatthariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Kāḷānusāriyaṃ gayha, anulimpiṃ tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhamanulimpetvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘Samuddharasimaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0508" /> lokaṃ, oghatiṇṇa <note>oghatiṇṇo (syā. ka.)</note> mahāmuni;
```

```
Ñāṇālokena jotesi, nāvaṭaṃ <note>pavaraṃ (syā.), vajira (pī.)</note> ñāṇamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammacakkaṃ <note>tuvaṃ cakkaṃ (ka.)</note> pavattesi, maddase paratitthiye;
```

```
Usabho jitasaṅgāmo, sampakampesi medaniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamudde ūmiyo, velantamhi pabhijjare;
```

```
Tatheva tava ñāṇamhi, sabbadiṭṭhī pabhijjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhumacchikajālena, saramhi sampatānite;
```

```
Antojālikatā <note>jālagatā (sī.)</note> pāṇā, pīḷitā honti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva titthiyā loke, puthupāsaṇḍanissitā <note>mūḷhā saccavinissaṭā (syā.), muṭṭhasaccavinissaṭā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Antoñāṇavare tuyhaṃ, parivattanti mārisa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘Patiṭṭhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0357" /> vuyhataṃ oghe, tvañhi nātho abandhunaṃ;
```

```
Bhayaṭṭitānaṃ saraṇaṃ, muttitthīnaṃ parāyaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘Ekavīro <pb ed="M" n="1.0379" /> asadiso, mettākaruṇasañcayo <note>saññuto (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Asamo susamo santo <note>susīlo asamo santo (sī.), paññavā yuttacāgo ca (syā.)</note>, vasī tādī jitañjayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘Dhīro <pb ed="P" n="1.0324" /> vigatasammoho, anejo akathaṃkathī;
```

```
Tusito <note>vusito (sī.)</note> vantadososi, nimmalo saṃyato suci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅgātigo hatamado <note>gatamado (syā.), tamanudo (ka.)</note>, tevijjo tibhavantago;
```

```
Sīmātigo dhammagaru, gatattho hitavabbhuto <note>hitavappatho (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘Tārako <pb ed="T" n="1.0509" /> tvaṃ yathā nāvā, nidhīvassāsakārako;
```

```
Asambhīto yathā sīho, gajarājāva dappito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Thometvā dasagāthāhi, padumuttaraṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, tuṇhī aṭṭhāsahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me sīlañca ñāṇañca, saddhammañcāpi vaṇṇayi <note>dhammañcāpi pakittayi (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi kappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Aññe devebhibhavitvā, issaraṃ kārayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsane pabbajissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjiya;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi megho thanayaṃ, tappeti mediniṃ imaṃ;
```

```
Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra, dhammena tappayī mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlaṃ paññañca dhammañca, thavitvā lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pattomhi paramaṃ santiṃ, nibbānaṃ padamaccutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Aho <pb ed="M" n="1.0380" /> nūna sa bhagavā, ciraṃ tiṭṭheyya cakkhumā;
```

```
Aññātañca vijāneyyuṃ, phuseyyuṃ <note>aññātañcāpi jāneyya, passeyya (ka.)</note> amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0510" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0358" /> me pacchimā jāti, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhithomayiṃ
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="1.0325" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbakittiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sabbakittikattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Madhudāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Sindhuyā nadiyā tīre, sukato assamo mama;
```

```
Tattha vācemahaṃ sisse, itihāsaṃ salakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammakāmā vinītā te, sotukāmā susāsanaṃ;
```

```
Chaḷaṅge pāramippattā, sindhukūle vasanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Uppātagamane <pb ed="T" n="1.0511" /> ceva, lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesantā, vasanti vipine tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, loke uppajji tāvade;
```

```
Amhākaṃ anukampanto, upāgacchi vināyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tiṇasanthārakaṃ katvā, lokajeṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘Vipināto <pb ed="M" n="1.0381" /> madhuṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Sambuddho paribhuñjitvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo taṃ adāsi madhuṃ me, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā madhudānena, tiṇasanthārakena ca;
```

```
Tiṃsa kappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsa <pb ed="V" n="1.0359" /> kappasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devalokā idhāgantvā, mātukucchiṃ upāgate;
```

```
Madhuvassaṃ pavassittha, chādayaṃ madhunā mahiṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘Mayi nikkhantamattamhi, kucchiyā ca suduttarā;
```

```
Tatrāpi madhuvassaṃ me, vassate niccakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘Agārā <pb ed="T" n="1.0512" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0326" /> abhinikkhamma, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Lābhī annassa pānassa, madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbakāmasamiddhohaṃ, bhavitvā devamānuse;
```

```
Teneva madhudānena, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘Vuṭṭhamhi deve caturaṅgule tiṇe, sampupphite <note>supupphite (syā.)</note> dharaṇīruhe sañchanne <note>vappadese (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Suññe ghare maṇḍaparukkhamūlake, vasāmi niccaṃ sukhito anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhe mahante hīne ca <note>majjhe mayhaṃ bhavā assu (syā. pī. ka.)</note>, bhave sabbe atikkamiṃ <note>ye bhave samatikkamiṃ (syā. ka.), yo bhavesu pakittayi (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ajja me āsavā khīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="1.0382" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā madhudāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Madhudāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Padumakūṭāgāriyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘Piyadassī <pb ed="T" n="1.0513" /> nāma bhagavā, sayambhū lokanāyako;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, samādhikusalo muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘Vanasaṇḍaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0360" /> samogayha, piyadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Paṃsukūlaṃ pattharitvā, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo pure āsiṃ, araññe <note>vipine (sī.), irine (syā. ka.)</note> kānane ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasadaṃ migamesanto, āhiṇḍāmi ahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Pupphitaṃ sālarājaṃva, sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ, piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Jātassaraṃ samogayha, padumaṃ āhariṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘Āharitvāna padumaṃ, satapattaṃ manoramaṃ;
```

```
Kūṭāgāraṃ karitvāna, chādayiṃ padumenahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako <pb ed="P" n="1.0327" /> kāruṇiko, piyadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Sattarattindivaṃ buddho, kūṭāgāre vasī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘Purāṇaṃ chaḍḍayitvāna, navena chādayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, aṭṭhāsiṃ tāvade ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘Vuṭṭhahitvā <pb ed="M" n="1.0383" /> samādhimhā, piyadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Disaṃ anuvilokento, nisīdi lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="T" n="1.0514" /> sudassano nāma, upaṭṭhāko mahiddhiko;
```

```
Cittamaññāya buddhassa, piyadassissa satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
‘‘Asītiyā sahassehi, bhikkhūhi parivārito;
```

```
Vanante sukhamāsīnaṃ, upesi lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi, adhivatthā ca devatā;
```

```
Buddhassa cittamaññāya, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
‘‘Samāgatesu yakkhesu, kumbhaṇḍe saharakkhase;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe ca sampatte, gāthā pabyāharī <note>sabyāharī (syā.), mābyāharī (sī.)</note> jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo maṃ sattāhaṃ pūjesi, āvāsañca akāsi me;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sududdasaṃ sunipuṇaṃ, gambhīraṃ suppakāsitaṃ;
```

```
Ñāṇena kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
‘‘‘Catuddasāni <pb ed="V" n="1.0361" /> kappāni, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Kūṭāgāraṃ mahantassa <note>brahaṃ tassa (sī. syā.)</note>, padmapupphehi chāditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ākāse dhārayissati, pupphakammassidaṃ <note>pubbakammassidaṃ (syā.)</note> phalaṃ;
```

```
Catubbīse <note>catuddase (syā.)</note> kappasate, vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tattha pupphamayaṃ byamhaṃ, ākāse dhārayissati;
```

```
Yathā padumapattamhi, toyaṃ na upalimpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tathevīmassa ñāṇamhi, kilesā nopalimpare;
```

```
Manasā vinivaṭṭetvā, pañca nīvaraṇe ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cittaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0515" /> janetvā nekkhamme, agārā pabbajissati;
```

```
Tato pupphamaye byamhe, dhārente <note>pupphamayaṃ byamhaṃ, dhārentaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> nikkhamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rukkhamūle vasantassa, nipakassa satīmato;
```

```
Tattha pupphamayaṃ byamhaṃ, matthake dhārayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cīvaraṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0384" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0328" /> piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Datvāna bhikkhusaṅghassa, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārena caratā <note>caraṇā (sī. pī. ka.), carite (syā.)</note>, pabbajjaṃ abhinikkhamiṃ;
```

```
Rukkhamūle vasantampi <note>vasantamhi (sī.), vasatopi (?)</note>, kūṭāgāraṃ dharīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
‘‘Cīvare piṇḍapāte ca, cetanā me na vijjati;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyutto, labhāmi pariniṭṭhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
‘‘Gaṇanāto asaṅkheyyā, kappakoṭī bahū mama;
```

```
Rittakā te atikkantā, pamuttā lokanāyakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, piyadassī vināyako;
```

```
Tamahaṃ payirupāsitvā, imaṃ yoniṃ upāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§379.</p>

```
‘‘Idha passāmi <note>idhaddasāsiṃ (sī.)</note> sambuddhaṃ, anomaṃ nāma cakkhumaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ upagantvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§380.</p>

```
‘‘Dukkhassantakaro buddho, maggaṃ me desayī jino;
```

```
Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§381.</p>

```
‘‘Tosayitvāna sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§382.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase <pb ed="T" n="1.0516" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0362" /> kappasate, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§383.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§384.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§385.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumakūṭāgāriyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Padumakūṭāgāriyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Bākulattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§386.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="M" n="1.0385" />, sobhito nāma pabbato;
```

```
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, sakasissehi māpito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§387.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍapā ca bahū tattha, pupphitā sinduvārakā;
```

```
Kapitthā ca bahū tattha, pupphitā jīvajīvakā <note>campakā nāgaketakā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§388.</p>

```
‘‘Nigguṇḍiyo bahū tattha, badarāmalakāni ca;
```

```
Phārusakā alābū ca, puṇḍarīkā ca pupphitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§389.</p>

```
‘‘Āḷakā <pb ed="T" n="1.0517" /> <note>aḷakkā (syā.)</note> beluvā tattha, kadalī mātuluṅgakā;
```

```
Mahānāmā bahū tattha, ajjunā ca piyaṅgukā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§390.</p>

```
‘‘Kosambā <pb ed="P" n="1.0329" /> saḷalā nimbā <note>nīpā (sī.)</note>, nigrodhā ca kapitthanā;
```

```
Ediso assamo mayhaṃ, sasissohaṃ tahiṃ vasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§391.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, sayambhū lokanāyako;
```

```
Gavesaṃ paṭisallānaṃ, mamassamamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§392.</p>

```
‘‘Upetamhi mahāvīre, anomadassimahāyase;
```

```
Khaṇena lokanāthassa, vātābādho samuṭṭhahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§393.</p>

```
‘‘Vicaranto araññamhi, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ, cakkhumantaṃ mahāyasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§394.</p>

```
‘‘Iriyañcāpi disvāna, upalakkhesahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Asaṃsayañhi buddhassa, byādhi no udapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§395.</p>

```
‘‘Khippaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0363" /> assamamāgañchiṃ, mama sissāna santike;
```

```
Bhesajjaṃ kattukāmohaṃ, sisse āmantayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§396.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭissuṇitvāna me vākyaṃ, sissā sabbe sagāravā;
```

```
Ekajjhaṃ sannipatiṃsu, satthugāravatā mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§397.</p>

```
‘‘Khippaṃ pabbatamāruyha, sabbosadhamahāsahaṃ <note>makāsahaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Pānīyayogaṃ <note>pānīyayoggaṃ (sī.)</note> katvāna, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§398.</p>

```
‘‘Paribhutte <pb ed="M" n="1.0386" /> mahāvīre, sabbaññulokanāyake;
```

```
Khippaṃ vāto vūpasami, sugatassa mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§399.</p>

```
‘‘Passaddhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0518" /> darathaṃ disvā, anomadassī mahāyaso;
```

```
Sakāsane nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§400.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me pādāsi bhesajjaṃ, byādhiñca samayī mama;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§401.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Vādite tūriye tattha, modissati sadā ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§402.</p>

```
‘‘‘Manussalokamāgantvā, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§403.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcapaññāsakappamhi, anomo nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa <note>jambudīpassa (syā.)</note> issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§404.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattaratanasampanno, cakkavattī mahabbalo;
```

```
Tāvatiṃsepi khobhetvā, issaraṃ kārayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§405.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devabhūto <pb ed="P" n="1.0330" /> manusso vā, appābādho bhavissati;
```

```
Pariggahaṃ vivajjetvā, byādhiṃ loke tarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§406.</p>

```
‘‘‘Apparimeyye ito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§407.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§408.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kilese jhāpayitvāna, taṇhāsotaṃ tarissati;
```

```
Bākulo <note>bakkulo (sī. syā.)</note> nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§409.</p>

```
‘‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0519" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0364" /> sabbaṃ abhiññāya, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapessati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§410.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, sayambhū lokanāyako;
```

```
Vivekānuvilokento, mamassamamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§411.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0387" /> mahāvīraṃ, sabbaññuṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Sabbosadhena tappesiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§412.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa me sukataṃ kammaṃ, sukhette bījasampadā;
```

```
Khepetuṃ neva sakkomi, tadā hi sukataṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§413.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā mama suladdhaṃ me, yohaṃ addakkhi nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tena kammāvasesena, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§414.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§415.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§416.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§417.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§418.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0520" /> sudaṃ āyasmā bākulo <note>bakkulo (sī. syā.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Bākulattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Girimānandattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§419.</p>

```
‘‘Bhariyā me kālaṅkatā, putto sīvathikaṃ gato;
```

```
Mātā pitā matā bhātā, ekacitamhi <note>mātā pitā ca bhātā ca, ekacitakamhi (sī. syā.)</note> ḍayhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§420.</p>

```
‘‘Tena sokena santatto, kiso paṇḍu ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Cittakkhepo ca me āsi, tena sokena aṭṭito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§421.</p>

```
‘‘Sokasallaparetohaṃ<pb ed="P" n="1.0331" />, vanantamupasaṅkamiṃ;
```

```
Pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā, rukkhamūle vasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§422.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho <pb ed="M" n="1.0388" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0365" /> nāma sambuddho, dukkhassantakaro jino;
```

```
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgañchi mama santikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§423.</p>

```
‘‘Padasaddaṃ suṇitvāna, sumedhassa mahesino;
```

```
Paggahetvānahaṃ sīsaṃ, ullokesiṃ mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§424.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgate mahāvīre, pīti me udapajjatha;
```

```
Tadāsimekaggamano, disvā taṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§425.</p>

```
‘‘Satiṃ paṭilabhitvāna, paṇṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Nisīdi bhagavā tattha, anukampāya cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§426.</p>

```
‘‘Nisajja <pb ed="T" n="1.0521" /> tattha bhagavā, sumedho lokanāyako;
```

```
Dhammaṃ me kathayī buddho, sokasallavinodanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§427.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anavhitā tato āguṃ, ananuññātā ito gatā;
```

```
Yathāgatā tathā gatā, tattha kā paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§428.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathāpi pathikā sattā, vassamānāya vuṭṭhiyā;
```

```
Sabhaṇḍā upagacchanti, vassassāpatanāya te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§429.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vasse ca te oramite, sampayanti yadicchakaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ, tattha kā paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§430.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āgantukā pāhunakā, caliteritakampitā;
```

```
Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ, tattha kā paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§431.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathāpi urago jiṇṇaṃ, hitvā gacchati saṃ tacaṃ <note>saṃtanuṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ, saṃ tanuṃ idha hīyare’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§432.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, sokasallaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
```

```
Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§433.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvāna mahānāgaṃ, pūjayiṃ girimañjariṃ <note>girimañjarimapūjayiṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantaṃ <note>dibbagandhena sampannaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§434.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjayitvāna sambuddhaṃ, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Anussaraṃ guṇaggāni, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§435.</p>

```
‘‘Nittiṇṇosi <pb ed="M" n="1.0389" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0332" /> <note>nittaṇhosi (sī.), vitiṇṇosi (syā.)</note> mahāvīra, sabbaññu lokanāyaka;
```

```
Sabbe satte uddharasi, ñāṇena tvaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§436.</p>

```
‘‘Vimatiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0522" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0366" /> dveḷhakaṃ vāpi, sañchindasi mahāmune;
```

```
Paṭipādesi me maggaṃ, tava ñāṇena cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§437.</p>

```
‘‘Arahā vasipattā <note>siddhipattā (sī. syā.)</note> ca, chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā;
```

```
Antalikkhacarā dhīrā, parivārenti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§438.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭipannā ca sekhā ca, phalaṭṭhā santi sāvakā;
```

```
Sūrodayeva padumā, pupphanti tava sāvakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§439.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamuddovakkhobho, atulopi <note>yathā samuddo akkhobho, atulo ca (sī.)</note> duruttaro;
```

```
Evaṃ ñāṇena sampanno, appameyyosi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§440.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvāhaṃ lokajinaṃ, cakkhumantaṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Puthu disā namassanto, paṭikuṭiko agañchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§441.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, sampajāno patissato;
```

```
Okkamiṃ mātuyā kucchiṃ, sandhāvanto bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§442.</p>

```
‘‘Agārā abhinikkhamma, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Ātāpī nipako jhāyī, paṭisallānagocaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§443.</p>

```
‘‘Padhānaṃ padahitvāna, tosayitvā mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Candovabbhaghanā mutto, vicarāmi ahaṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§444.</p>

```
‘‘Vivekamanuyuttomhi, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§445.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§446.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="1.0523" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§447.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§448.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0390" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā girimānando thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Girimānandattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Saḷalamaṇḍapiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§449.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute <pb ed="V" n="1.0367" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0333" /> kakusandhamhi, brāhmaṇamhi vusīmati;
```

```
Gahetvā saḷalaṃ mālaṃ, maṇḍapaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§450.</p>

```
‘‘Tāvatiṃsagato santo, labhāmi byamhamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Aññe devetirocāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§451.</p>

```
‘‘Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ, caṅkamanto ṭhito cahaṃ;
```

```
Channo saḷalapupphehi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§452.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappamhi, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§453.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="1.0524" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§454.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§455.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saḷalamaṇḍapiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Saḷalamaṇḍapiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Sabbadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§456.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamuddaṃ ogayha, bhavanaṃ me sunimmitaṃ;
```

```
Sunimmitā pokkharaṇī, cakkavākapakūjitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§457.</p>

```
‘‘Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca;
```

```
Nadī ca sandate tattha, supatitthā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§458.</p>

```
‘‘Macchakacchapasañchannā<pb ed="M" n="1.0391" />, nānādijasamotthatā;
```

```
Mayūrakoñcābhirudā, kokilādīhi vagguhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§459.</p>

```
‘‘Pārevatā ravihaṃsā ca, cakkavākā nadīcarā;
```

```
Dindibhā sāḷikā cettha, pammakā <note>pampakā (sī.), cappakā (syā.)</note> jīvajīvakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§460.</p>

```
‘‘Haṃsā <pb ed="T" n="1.0525" /> koñcāpi naditā <note>koñcābhinaditā (sī. syā.)</note>, kosiyā piṅgalā bahū;
```

```
Sattaratanasampannā, maṇimuttikavālukā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§461.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbasoṇṇamayā <pb ed="V" n="1.0368" /> rukkhā, nānāgandhasameritā;
```

```
Ujjotenti divārattiṃ, bhavanaṃ sabbakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§462.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="P" n="1.0334" /> tūriyasahassāni, sāyaṃ pāto pavajjare;
```

```
Soḷasitthisahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§463.</p>

```
‘‘Abhinikkhamma bhavanā, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, vandayiṃ taṃ mahāyasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§464.</p>

```
‘‘Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, sasaṅghaṃ taṃ nimantayiṃ;
```

```
Adhivāsesi so dhīro, sumedho lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§465.</p>

```
‘‘Mama dhammakathaṃ katvā, uyyojesi mahāmuni;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, bhavanaṃ me upāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§466.</p>

```
‘‘Āmantayiṃ parijanaṃ, sabbe sannipatātha <note>sannipatattha (ka.)</note> vo;
```

```
Pubbaṇhasamayaṃ buddho, bhavanaṃ āgamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§467.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā amhaṃ suladdhaṃ no, ye vasāma tavantike;
```

```
Mayampi buddhaseṭṭhassa, pūjaṃ kassāma satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§468.</p>

```
‘‘Annapanaṃ paṭṭhapetvā, kālaṃ ārocayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, upesi lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§469.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcaṅgikehi tūriyehi, paccuggamanamakāsahaṃ;
```

```
Sabbasoṇṇamaye pīṭhe, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§470.</p>

```
‘‘Uparicchadanaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0526" /> āsi, sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ tadā;
```

