Bījaniyo pavāyanti, bhikkhusaṅghassa antare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§471.</p>

```
‘‘Pahūtenannapānena<pb ed="M" n="1.0392" />, bhikkhusaṅghamatappayiṃ;
```

```
Paccekadussayugaḷe, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§472.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti, lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§473.</p>

```
‘‘Yo me annena pānena, sabbe ime ca tappayiṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§474.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§475.</p>

```
‘‘Uppajjati <pb ed="V" n="1.0369" /> <note>upagacchati (sī.)</note> yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbadā sabbasovaṇṇaṃ, chadanaṃ dhārayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§476.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, okkākakusalasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§477.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="1.0335" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§478.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, sīhanādaṃ nadissati;
```

```
Citake chattaṃ dhārenti, heṭṭhā chattamhi ḍayhatha’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§479.</p>

```
‘‘Sāmaññaṃ me anuppattaṃ, kilesā jhāpitā mayā;
```

```
Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, santāpo me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§480.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi<pb ed="T" n="1.0527" />, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§481.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§482.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§483.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sabbadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Ajitattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§484.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="1.0393" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ajjhogāhetvā himavantaṃ, nisīdi lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§485.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ addakkhiṃ <note>passāmi (?)</note> sambuddhaṃ, napi saddaṃ suṇomahaṃ;
```

```
Mama bhakkhaṃ gavesanto, āhiṇḍāmi vane ahaṃ <note>tadā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§486.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddassāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ;
```

```
Disvāna vittimāpajjiṃ <note>cittamāpajji (sī.), cittamāpajjiṃ (syā.)</note>, satto ko nāmayaṃ bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§487.</p>

```
‘‘Lakkhaṇāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0528" /> viloketvā, mama vijjaṃ anussariṃ;
```

```
Sutañhi metaṃ vuḍḍhānaṃ, paṇḍitānaṃ subhāsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§488.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0370" /> yathā taṃ vacanaṃ, ayaṃ buddho bhavissati;
```

```
Yaṃnūnāhaṃ sakkareyyaṃ, gatiṃ me sodhayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§489.</p>

```
‘‘Khippaṃ assamamāgantvā, madhutelaṃ gahiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Kolambakaṃ gahetvāna, upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ <note>narāsabhaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§490.</p>

```
‘‘Tidaṇḍake gahetvāna, abbhokāse ṭhapesahaṃ;
```

```
Padīpaṃ pajjalitvāna, aṭṭhakkhattuṃ avandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§491.</p>

```
‘‘Sattarattindivaṃ <pb ed="P" n="1.0336" /> buddho, nisīdi purisuttamo;
```

```
Tato ratyā vivasāne, vuṭṭhāsi lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§492.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, sabbarattindivaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Dīpaṃ buddhassa pādāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§493.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe vanā gandhamayā, pabbate gandhamādane;
```

```
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, āgacchuṃ buddhasantikaṃ <note>upagacchuṃ tadā jinaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§494.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci pupphagandhāse, pupphitā dharaṇīruhā;
```

```
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§495.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā himavantamhi, nāgā ca garuḷā ubho;
```

```
Dhammañca sotukāmā te, āgacchuṃ buddhasantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§496.</p>

```
‘‘Devalo <pb ed="M" n="1.0394" /> nāma samaṇo, buddhassa aggasāvako;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, buddhasantikupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§497.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="1.0529" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§498.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me dīpaṃ padīpesi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§499.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi kappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

Soḷasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§500.</p>

```
‘‘‘Chattisakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Pathaviyaṃ sattasataṃ, vipulaṃ rajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§501.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0371" /> vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Iminā dīpadānena, dibbacakkhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§502.</p>

```
‘‘‘Samantato aṭṭhakosaṃ <note>aḍḍhakosaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, passissati ayaṃ sadā;
```

```
Devalokā cavantassa, nibbattantassa jantuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§503.</p>

```
‘‘‘Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ, padīpaṃ dhārayissati;
```

```
Jāyamānassa sattassa, puññakammasamaṅgino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§504.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā nagaraṃ āsi, tāvatā jotayissati;
```

```
Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§505.</p>

```
‘‘‘Asseva dīpadānassa, <note>aṭṭhadīpaphalena hi; upaṭṭhissantimaṃ jantuṃ (syā.), aṭṭha dīpā phalena hi; na jahissanti’maṃ jantuṃ (?)</note> aṭṭhadīpaphalena hi;
```

```
Na jayissantimaṃ jantū <note>aṭṭhadīpaphalena hi; upaṭṭhissantimaṃ jantuṃ (syā.), aṭṭha dīpā phalena hi; na jahissanti’maṃ jantuṃ (?)</note>, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§506.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi<pb ed="T" n="1.0530" /><pb ed="P" n="1.0337" />, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§507.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§508.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tosayitvāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0395" /> sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Ajito nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§509.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi kappasahassāni, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tatrāpi me dīpasataṃ, jotate niccakālikaṃ <note>sabbakālikaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§510.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, niddhāvanti pabhā mama;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, bhiyyo hāsaṃ janesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§511.</p>

```
‘‘Tusitāhaṃ cavitvāna, okkamiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ;
```

```
Jāyamānassa santassa, āloko vipulo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§512.</p>

```
‘‘Agārā abhinikkhamma, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Bāvariṃ upasaṅkamma, sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§513.</p>

```
‘‘Himavante vasantohaṃ, assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto, upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§514.</p>

```
‘‘Danto buddho dametāvī, oghatiṇṇo nirūpadhi;
```

```
Nibbānaṃ kathayī buddho, sabbadukkhappamocanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§515.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0372" /> me āgamanaṃ siddhaṃ, tositohaṃ mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§516.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="T" n="1.0531" /> kappe, yaṃ dīpamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§517.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§518.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§519.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ajito thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ajitattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

Pilindavacchavaggo cattālīsamo.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0396" /> –

```
Pilindavaccho selo ca, sabbakittī madhuṃdado;
```

```
Kūṭāgārī bākulo ca, giri saḷalasavhayo.
```

```
Sabbado <pb ed="P" n="1.0338" /> ajito ceva, gāthāyo gaṇitā iha;
```

```
Satāni pañca gāthānaṃ, vīsati ca taduttarīti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Padumārakkhado <pb ed="T" n="1.0532" /> ceva, umā gandhodakena ca;
```

```
Ekapadma saddasaññī, mandāraṃ bodhivandako.
```

```
Avaṭañca pilindi <note>evameva dissati</note> ca, gāthāyo gaṇitā iha;
```

```
Catusattati gāthāyo, ekādasa satāni ca.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Padumavaggadasakaṃ.</trailer>

Catutthasatakaṃ samattaṃ.

### 41. Metteyyavaggo

#### 1. Tissametteyyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbhārakūṭaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0533" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0397" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0373" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0339" /> nissāya, sobhito nāma tāpaso;
```

```
Pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā, vasati pabbatantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Aggiṃ dāruṃ āharitvā, ujjālesiṃ ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto, brahmalokūpapattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ karosi mahāpuñña, dehi me aggidārukaṃ;
```

```
Ahamaggiṃ paricare, tato me suddhi hohiti <note>hehiti (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Subhaddako tvaṃ manuje, devate tvaṃ pajānasi;
```

```
Tuvaṃ aggiṃ paricara, handa te aggidārukaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Tato kaṭṭhaṃ gahetvāna, aggiṃ ujjālayī jino;
```

```
Na tattha kaṭṭhaṃ pajjhāyi, pāṭiheraṃ mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Na te aggi pajjalati, āhutī te na vijjati;
```

```
Niratthakaṃ vataṃ tuyhaṃ, aggiṃ paricarassu me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Kīdiso so <note>te (syā. ka.)</note> mahāvīra, aggi tava pavuccati;
```

```
Mayhampi kathayassetaṃ, ubho paricarāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Hetudhammanirodhāya<pb ed="T" n="1.0534" />, kilesasamaṇāya ca;
```

```
Issāmacchariyaṃ hitvā, tayo ete mamāhutī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Kīdiso tvaṃ mahāvīra, kathaṃ gottosi mārisa;
```

```
Ācārapaṭipatti te, bāḷhaṃ kho mama ruccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Khattiyamhi <pb ed="P" n="2.0340" /> kule jāto, abhiññāpāramiṃ gato;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Yadi <pb ed="M" n="1.0398" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0374" /> buddhosi sabbaññū, pabhaṅkara tamonuda;
```

```
Namassissāmi taṃ deva, dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Pattharitvājinacammaṃ, nisīdanamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Nisīda nātha sabbaññu, upaṭṭhissāmahaṃ tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Nisīdi bhagavā tattha, ajinamhi suvitthate;
```

```
Nimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ, pabbataṃ agamāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Khāribhārañca pūretvā, tindukaphalamāhariṃ;
```

```
Madhunā yojayitvāna, phalaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Mama nijjhāyamānassa, paribhuñji tadā jino;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādesiṃ, pekkhanto lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mamassame nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo maṃ phalena tappesi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcavīsatikkhattuṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0535" /> so, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa saṅkappamaññāya, pubbakammasamaṅgino;
```

```
Annaṃ pānañca vatthañca, sayanañca mahārahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘‘Puññakammena saṃyuttā, nibbattissanti tāvade;
```

```
Sadā pamudito cāyaṃ, bhavissati anāmayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘‘Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, manussattaṃ gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ upagantvāna, arahā so bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Varadhammamanuppatto, rāgadose samūhaniṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="1.0399" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="1.0375" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0536" /> sudaṃ āyasmā tissametteyyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Tissametteyyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Puṇṇakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbhārakūṭaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0341" /> nissāya, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Ābādhiko ca so <note>ābādhiko garu (sī.)</note> buddho, vasati pabbatantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Mama assamasāmantā, panādo āsi tāvade;
```

```
Buddhe nibbāyamānamhi, āloko udapajjatha <note>āsi tāvade (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā vanasaṇḍasmiṃ, acchakokataracchakā;
```

```
Vāḷā ca <note>byagghā (sī.)</note> kesarī sabbe, abhigajjiṃsu tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Uppātaṃ tamahaṃ disvā, pabbhāraṃ agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tatthaddassāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Suphullaṃ sālarājaṃva, sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃ;
```

```
Vītaccikaṃva aṅgāraṃ, nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṇaṃ kaṭṭhañca pūretvā, citakaṃ tatthakāsahaṃ;
```

```
Citakaṃ sukataṃ katvā, sarīraṃ jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Sarīraṃ jhāpayitvāna, gandhatoyaṃ samokiriṃ;
```

```
Antalikkhe ṭhito yakkho, nāmamaggahi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0537" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0400" /> pūritaṃ <note>taṃ pūritaṃ (syā.), sappurisa (ka.)</note> tayā kiccaṃ, sayambhussa mahesino;
```

```
Puṇṇako nāma nāmena, sadā hohi tuvaṃ <note>yadā hosi tuvaṃ (syā.), sadā hohiti tvaṃ (ka.)</note> mune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna, devalokaṃ agacchahaṃ;
```

```
Tattha dibbamayo gandho, antalikkhā pavassati <note>antalikkhe pavāyati (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Tatrāpi nāmadheyyaṃ me, puṇṇakoti ahū tadā;
```

```
Devabhūto manusso vā, saṅkappaṃ pūrayāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Idhāpi puṇṇako nāma, nāmadheyyaṃ pakāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Tosayitvāna <pb ed="V" n="1.0376" /> sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tanukiccassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Puṇṇakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Mettaguttheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="T" n="1.0538" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0342" />, asoko nāma pabbato;
```

```
Tatthāsi assamo mayhaṃ, vissakammena <note>visukammena (sī. syā. ka.)</note> māpito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Nivāsayitvā pubbaṇhe, piṇḍāya me <note>maṃ (sī.)</note> upāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0401" /> mahāvīraṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Paggayha sugatapattaṃ <note>sugataṃ pattaṃ (sī.), subhakaṃ pattaṃ (pī.)</note>, sappitelaṃ apūrayiṃ <note>sappitelena pūrayiṃ (sī.), sappitelassa’pūrayiṃ (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Datvānahaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe, sumedhe lokanāyake;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, bhiyyo <note>bhīyo (sī.), bhīyyo (pī.)</note> hāsaṃ janesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Iminā sappidānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Devabhūto manusso vā, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Vinipātaṃ vivajjetvā, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ paṇidhitvā, labhāmi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā tuyhaṃ suladdhaṃ te, yaṃ maṃ addakkhi brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Mama dassanamāgamma, arahattaṃ bhavissati <note>arahā tvaṃ bhavissasi (sī. pī.), arahattaṃ gamissasi (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Vissattho <note>vissaṭṭho (syā. pī.), visaṭṭho (ka.)</note> hohi mā bhāyi, adhigantvā mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Mamañhi sappiṃ datvāna, parimokkhasi jātiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Iminā <pb ed="V" n="1.0377" /> sappidānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Devabhūto manusso vā, labhase vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Iminā <pb ed="T" n="1.0539" /> sappidānena, mettacittavatāya ca;
```

```
Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhatiṃsatikkhattuñca, devarājā bhavissasi;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissasi;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa <note>jambusaṇḍassa (sī. pī.)</note> issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamuddovakkhobho, duddharo pathavī yathā;
```

```
Evameva ca te bhogā, appameyyā bhavissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhikoṭī hiraññassa, cajitvā <note>catvāna (sī. ka.), datvāna (syā. pī.)</note> pabbajiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ kusalaṃ gavesanto, bāvariṃ upasaṅkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha <pb ed="M" n="1.0402" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0343" /> mante adhīyāmi, chaḷaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃ;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ, uppajji tvaṃ mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Tava dassanakāmohaṃ, āgatomhi mahāmuni;
```

```
Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, sappiṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Etthantare nābhijāne, sappiṃ viññāpitaṃ <note>viññāpitā (?)</note> mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, uppajjati yadicchakaṃ;
```

```
Cittamaññāya nibbattaṃ, sabbe santappayāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Aho buddhā aho dhammā <note>aho buddho aho dhammo (sī.) theragā. 201 theragāthāya tadaṭṭhakathāya ca saṃsandetabbaṃ</note>, aho no satthu sampadā;
```

```
Thokañhi sappiṃ datvāna, appameyyaṃ labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamudde <pb ed="T" n="1.0540" /> udakaṃ, yāvatā nerupassato;
```

```
Mama sappiṃ upādāya, kalabhāgaṃ na hessati <note>hissati (syā. ka.), essati (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā cakkavāḷassa, kariyantassa <note>kārayantassa (syā.), kayirantassa (pī.), āharantassa (ka.)</note> rāsito;
```

```
Mama nibbattavatthānaṃ <note>mayā nivatthavatthānaṃ (pī.)</note>, okāso so na sammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbatarājā himavā, pavaropi siluccayo;
```

```
Mamānulittagandhassa, upanidhiṃ <note>upanidhaṃ (sī. syā. ka.), upanīyaṃ (pī.)</note> na hessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Vatthaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0378" /> gandhañca sappiñca, aññañca diṭṭhadhammikaṃ;
```

```
Asaṅkhatañca nibbānaṃ, sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Satipaṭṭhānasayano, samādhijhānagocaro;
```

```
Bojjhaṅgabhojano <note>… janano (syā. ka.)</note> ajja, sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mettagū thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Mettaguttherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Dhotakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Gaṅgā <pb ed="T" n="1.0541" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0403" /> bhāgīrathī nāma, himavantā pabhāvitā <note>himavantappabhāvitā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Haṃsavatiyā dvārena, anusandati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Sobhito nāma ārāmo, gaṅgākūle sumāpito;
```

```
Tattha padumuttaro buddho, vasate lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Tidasehi <pb ed="P" n="2.0344" /> yathā indo, manujehi purakkhato;
```

```
Nisīdi tattha bhagavā, asambhītova kesarī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, vasāmi <note>ahosiṃ (syā.)</note> brāhmaṇo ahaṃ;
```

```
Chaḷaṅgo nāma nāmena, evaṃnāmo mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārasa sissasatā, parivārenti maṃ tadā;
```

```
Tehi sissehi samito, gaṅgātīraṃ upāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ samaṇe, nikkuhe dhotapāpake;
```

```
Bhāgīrathiṃ tarantehaṃ <note>tarantohaṃ (syā. pī.)</note>, evaṃ cintesi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Sāyaṃ pātaṃ <note>sāyapātaṃ (pī.)</note> tarantāme, buddhaputtā mahāyasā;
```

```
Vihesayanti attānaṃ, tesaṃ attā vihaññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, buddho aggo pavuccati;
```

```
Natthi me dakkhiṇe kāraṃ, gatimaggavisodhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃnūna <pb ed="V" n="1.0379" /> buddhaseṭṭhassa, setuṃ gaṅgāya kāraye;
```

```
Kārāpetvā imaṃ kammaṃ <note>setuṃ (syā.)</note>, santarāmi imaṃ bhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0542" /> datvāna, setuṃ kārāpayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Saddahanto kataṃ kāraṃ, vipulaṃ me bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Kārāpetvāna taṃ setuṃ, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Sirasi añjaliṃ katvā, imaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassassa vayaṃ <note>vayaṃ satasahassaṃva (ka.)</note>, datvā <note>katvā (sī. pī.)</note> kārāpito mayā;
```

```
Tavatthāya mahāsetu, paṭiggaṇha mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="1.0404" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me setuṃ akāresi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

(Setudānaānisaṃso)

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘‘Darito pabbatato vā, rukkhato patitopiyaṃ;
```

```
Cutopi lacchatī ṭhānaṃ, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘‘Virūḷhamūlasantānaṃ, nigrodhamiva māluto;
```

```
Amittā nappasahanti, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nāssa corā pasahanti, nātimaññanti khattiyā;
```

```
Sabbe tarissatāmitte, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘‘Abbhokāsagataṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0345" /> santaṃ, kaṭhinātapatāpitaṃ;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyuttaṃ, na bhavissati vedanā <note>tāvade (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, hatthiyānaṃ sunimmitaṃ;
```

```
Tassa saṅkappamaññāya, nibbattissati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sahassassā <pb ed="T" n="1.0543" /> vātajavā, sindhavā sīghavāhanā;
```

```
Sāyaṃ pātaṃ upessanti, setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āgantvāna manussattaṃ, sukhitoyaṃ bhavissati;
```

```
Vehāsaṃ <note>ihāpi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> manujasseva, hatthiyānaṃ bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0380" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ, jalajuttamanāmake;
```

```
Tattha kāraṃ karitvāna, pattohaṃ āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Padhānaṃ pahitattomhi, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="1.0405" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhotako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Dhotakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Upasīvattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="T" n="1.0544" />, anomo nāma pabbato;
```

```
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Nadī ca sandatī tattha, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Anūpatitthe jāyanti, padumuppalakā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
```

```
Macchakacchapasañchannā <note>macchakacchapasampannā (?)</note>, nadikā sandate tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Timirā pupphitā tattha, asokā khuddamālakā;
```

```
Punnāgā giripunnāgā, sampavanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṭajā <pb ed="P" n="2.0346" /> pupphitā tattha, tiṇasūlavanāni ca;
```

```
Sālā ca saḷalā tattha, campakā pupphitā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjunā atimuttā ca, mahānāmā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Asanā madhugandhī ca, pupphitā te mamassame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Uddālakā pāṭalikā, yūthikā ca piyaṅgukā;
```

```
Bimbijālakasañchannā, samantā aḍḍhayojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Mātaggārā <pb ed="V" n="1.0381" /> <note>mātaṅgavā (sī.), mātakarā (syā.), mātaṅgā vā (pī.)</note> sattaliyo, pāṭalī sinduvārakā;
```

```
Aṅkolakā bahū tattha, tālakuṭṭhi <note>tālakūṭā (sī. syā.), tālakuṭṭhā (pī.)</note> ca pupphitā;
```

```
Seleyyakā bahū tattha, pupphitā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Etesu <pb ed="M" n="1.0406" /> pupphajātesu <note>pupphamānesu (sī. pī.)</note>, sobhanti pādapā bahū;
```

```
Samantā <pb ed="T" n="1.0545" /> tena gandhena, vāyate mama assamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Harītakā āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā <note>vibhiṭakā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phārusakaphalāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Tindukā ca piyālā ca, madhukā kāsumārayo;
```

```
Labujā panasā tattha, kadalī badarīphalā <note>mandariphalā (ka.), candarīphalā (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Ambāṭakā bahū tattha, vallikāraphalāni ca;
```

```
Bījapūrasapāriyo <note>cirasaṃrasapākā ca (syā.), viṭapā ca sapākā ca (pī), vidaparapadādayo (ka.)</note>, phalitā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Āḷakā isimuggā ca, tato modaphalā bahū;
```

```
Avaṭā pakkabharitā <note>sakkarāritā (ka.)</note>, pilakkhudumbarāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Pipphilī marīcā tattha, nigrodhā ca kapitthanā;
```

```
Udumbarakā bahavo, kaṇḍupaṇṇā ca hariyo <note>kaṇḍapakkā ca pāriyo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Ete caññe ca bahavo, phalitā assame mama;
```

```
Puppharukkhāpi bahavo, pupphitā mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Āluvā ca kaḷambā ca, biḷālī takkalāni ca;
```

```
Ālakā tālakā ceva, vijjanti assame mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Assamassāvidūre me, mahājātassaro ahu;
```

```
Acchodako sītajalo, supatittho manoramo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuppalā bahū tattha, puṇḍarīkasamāyutā;
```

```
Mandālakehi <pb ed="P" n="2.0347" /> sañchannā, nānāgandhasameritā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā, aññe pupphanti kesarī;
```

```
Opupphapattā <pb ed="T" n="1.0546" /> tiṭṭhanti, padumākaṇṇikā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Madhu bhisamhā savati, khīraṃ sappi mulāḷibhi;
```

```
Samantā tena gandhena, nānāgandhasameritā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Kumudā <pb ed="M" n="1.0407" /> ambagandhi ca, nayitā dissare bahū;
```

```
Jātassarassānukūlaṃ, ketakā pupphitā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Suphullā <pb ed="V" n="1.0382" /> bandhujīvā ca, setavārī sugandhikā;
```

```
Kumbhilā susumārā ca, gahakā tattha jāyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Uggāhakā ajagarā, tattha jātassare bahū;
```

```
Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Macchakacchapasañchannā, atho papaṭakāhi <note>pampaṭakehi (sī.), sapaṭakehi (syā.), pappaṭakehi (pī)</note> ca;
```

```
Pārevatā ravihaṃsā, kukutthā <note>kukkutthā (syā. ka.), kutthakā (pī.)</note> ca nadīcarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Dindibhā <note>ṭiṭṭibhā (pī.)</note> cakkavākā ca, pampakā jīvajīvakā;
```

```
Kalandakā ukkusā ca, senakā uddharā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Koṭṭhakā sukapotā ca, tuliyā camarā bahū;
```

```
Kāreniyo <note>kāseniyā (syā.)</note> ca tilakā <note>kilakā (ka.)</note>, upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhā byagghā ca dīpī ca, acchakokataracchakā;
```

```
Vānarā kinnarā ceva, dissanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Tāni gandhāni ghāyanto, bhakkhayanto phalānahaṃ;
```

```
Gandhodakaṃ pivanto ca, vasāmi mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Eṇīmigā varāhā ca, pasadā khuddarūpakā;
```

```
Aggikā <pb ed="T" n="1.0547" /> jotikā ceva, vasanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca, sālikāpi ca kokilā;
```

```
Majjārikā <note>mañjarikā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bahū tattha, kosikā poṭṭhasīsakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Pisācā dānavā ceva, kumbhaṇḍā rakkhasā bahū;
```

```
Garuḷā pannagā ceva, vasanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Mahānubhāvā isayo, santacittā samāhitā;
```

```
Kamaṇḍaludharā <pb ed="P" n="2.0348" /> sabbe, ajinuttaravāsanā;
```

```
Jaṭābhārabharitāva <note>te jaṭābhārabharitā (sī. pī.), jaṭābhārabharitā ca (syā.)</note>, vasanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Yugamattañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0408" /> pekkhantā, nipakā santavuttino;
```

```
Lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā, vasanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Vākacīraṃ dhunantā te, phoṭentājinacammakaṃ;
```

```
Sabalehi upatthaddhā, gacchanti ambare tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Na te dakaṃ āharanti, kaṭṭhaṃ vā aggidārukaṃ;
```

```
Sayañca upasampannā, pāṭihīrassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Lohadoṇiṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0383" /> gahetvāna, vanamajjhe vasanti te;
```

```
Kuñjarāva mahānāgā, asambhītāva kesarī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Aññe gacchanti goyānaṃ, aññe pubbavidehakaṃ <note>pubbavidehanaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Aññe ca uttarakuruṃ, sakaṃ balamavassitā <note>balamapassitā (syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Tato piṇḍaṃ āharitvā, paribhuñjanti ekato;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ pakkamantānaṃ, uggatejāna tādinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Ajinacammasaddena<pb ed="T" n="1.0548" />, vanaṃ saddāyate tadā;
```

```
Edisā te mahāvīra, sissā uggatapā mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Parivuto ahaṃ tehi, vasāmi mama assame;
```

```
Tositā sakakammena, vinītāpi samāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Ārādhayiṃsu maṃ ete, sakakammābhilāsino;
```

```
Sīlavanto ca nipakā, appamaññāsu kovidā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Samayaṃ saṃviditvāna, upagacchi vināyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Upagantvāna sambuddho, ātāpī nipako muni;
```

```
Pattaṃ paggayha sambuddho, bhikkhāya mamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ, jalajuttamanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tiṇasantharaṃ <note>tiṇattharaṃ (syā.), tiṇatthataṃ (ka.)</note> paññāpetvā, sālapupphehi okiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Nisādetvāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0409" /> <note>nisīdetvāna (sī.), nisīditvāna (syā. pī.)</note> sambuddhaṃ, haṭṭho saṃviggamānaso;
```

```
Khippaṃ pabbatamāruyha, agaḷuṃ <note>agaruṃ (sī.)</note> aggahiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhamattaṃ gahetvāna, panasaṃ devagandhikaṃ;
```

```
Khandhe āropayitvāna, upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Phalaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0349" /> buddhassa datvāna, agaḷuṃ anulimpahaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Isimajjhe <pb ed="T" n="1.0549" /> nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me phalañca agaḷuṃ, āsanañca adāsi me;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gāme <pb ed="V" n="1.0384" /> vā yadi vāraññe, pabbhāresu guhāsu vā;
```

```
Imassa cittamaññāya, nibbattissati bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, upapanno ayaṃ naro;
```

```
Bhojanehi ca vatthehi, parisaṃ tappayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘‘Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Akkhobhabhogo hutvāna, saṃsarissatiyaṃ naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ekasattatikkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito <note>(upasīvo nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako) (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Suladdhalābho laddho me, yohaṃ addakkhiṃ nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Gāme <pb ed="T" n="1.0550" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0410" /> vā yadi vāraññe, pabbhāresu guhāsu vā;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, bhojanaṃ hoti me sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upasīvo <note>upasivo (ka.)</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Upasīvattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Nandakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="P" n="2.0350" /> pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasadaṃ migamesanto, sayambhuṃ addasaṃ ahaṃ <note>jinaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Anuruddho <pb ed="V" n="1.0385" /> nāma sambuddho, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Vivekakāmo so dhīro, vanamajjhogahī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Catudaṇḍe gahetvāna, catuṭṭhāne ṭhapesahaṃ;
```

```
Maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā, padmapupphehi chādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍapaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0551" /> chādayitvāna, sayambhuṃ abhivādayiṃ;
```

```
Dhanuṃ tattheva nikkhippa, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Naciraṃ pabbajitassa <note>pabbajitassa aciraṃ (sī.)</note>, byādhi me udapajjatha;
```

```
Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbakammena saṃyutto, tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tattha soṇṇamayaṃ byamhaṃ, nibbattati yadicchakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ, dibbayānamadhiṭṭhito;
```

```
Āruhitvāna taṃ yānaṃ, gacchāmahaṃ yadicchakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="M" n="1.0411" /> me niyyamānassa, devabhūtassa me sato;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, maṇḍapo me dharīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭāmi, acchanne <note>accantaṃ (sī.), accanta (pī.)</note> pupphasanthate;
```

```
Antalikkhā ca padumā, vassante niccakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Marīcike phandamāne, tappamāne ca ātape;
```

```
Na maṃ tāpeti ātāpo, maṇḍapassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Duggatiṃ samatikkanto, apāyā pihitā mama;
```

```
Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, santāpo me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Mahīsaññaṃ adhiṭṭhāya, loṇatoyaṃ tarāmahaṃ;
```

```
Tassa me sukataṃ kammaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Apathampi <note>abbhamhi (syā. ka.)</note> pathaṃ katvā, gacchāmi anilañjase;
```

```
Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0552" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0351" /> jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Āsavā me parikkhīṇā, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Jahitā purimā jāti, buddhassa oraso ahaṃ;
```

```
Dāyādomhi ca saddhamme, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Ārādhitomhi <pb ed="V" n="1.0386" /> sugataṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Dhammadhajo dhammadāyādo <note>dhammādāso (ka.)</note>, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhitvāna sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Pāraṅgamaniyaṃ maggaṃ, apucchiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhiṭṭho kathayī buddho, gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ, parimuttomhi jātiyā;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0412" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nandako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Nandakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Hemakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbhārakūṭaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0553" /> nissāya, anomo nāma tāpaso;
```

```
Assamaṃ sukataṃ katvā, paṇṇasāle vasī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhaṃ tassa tapo kammaṃ, siddhipatto sake bale;
```

```
Sakasāmaññavikkanto, ātāpī nipako muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Visārado sasamaye, paravāde ca kovido;
```

```
Paṭṭho bhūmantalikkhamhi, uppātamhi ca kovido.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Vītasoko nirārambho, appāhāro alolupo;
```

```
Lābhālābhena santuṭṭho, jhāyī jhānarato muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Piyadassī nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Satte tāretukāmo so, karuṇāya pharī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Bodhaneyyaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0352" /> janaṃ disvā, piyadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Cakkavāḷasahassampi, gantvā ovadate muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Mamuddharitukāmo <pb ed="V" n="1.0387" /> so, mamassamamupāgami;
```

```
Na diṭṭho me jino pubbe, na sutopi ca kassaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘Uppātā supinā mayhaṃ, lakkhaṇā suppakāsitā;
```

```
Paṭṭho bhūmantalikkhamhi, nakkhattapadakovido.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ buddhassa sutvāna, tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
```

```
Tiṭṭhanto <note>bhuñjanto (sī. pī. ka.)</note> vā nisinno vā, sarāmi niccakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Mayi <pb ed="T" n="1.0554" /> evaṃ sarantamhi, bhagavāpi anussari;
```

```
Buddhaṃ anussarantassa, pīti me hoti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Kālañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0413" /> punarāgamma, upesi maṃ mahāmuni;
```

```
Sampattepi na jānāmi, ayaṃ buddho mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, piyadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Sañjānāpesi attānaṃ, ‘ahaṃ buddho sadevake’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Sañjānitvāna sambuddhaṃ, piyadassiṃ mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aññe <note>sabbe (syā.)</note> pīṭhe ca pallaṅke, āsandīsu nisīdare;
```

```
Tuvampi sabbadassāvī, nisīda ratanāsane’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaratanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ, nimminitvāna tāvade;
```

```
Piyadassissa munino, adāsiṃ iddhinimmitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Ratane ca nisinnassa, pīṭhake iddhinimmite;
```

```
Kumbhamattaṃ jambuphalaṃ, adāsiṃ tāvade ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Mama hāsaṃ janetvāna, paribhuñji mahāmuni;
```

```
Tadā cittaṃ pasādetvā, satthāraṃ abhivādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘Piyadassī tu bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Ratanāsanamāsīno, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me ratanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ, amatañca phalaṃ adā;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattasattati <pb ed="T" n="1.0555" /> kappāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Pañcasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dvattiṃsakkhattuṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0388" /> devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘‘Soṇṇamayaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0353" /> rūpimayaṃ, pallaṅkaṃ sukataṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Lohitaṅgamayañceva, lacchati ratanāmayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘‘Caṅkamantampi manujaṃ, puññakammasamaṅginaṃ;
```

```
Pallaṅkāni anekāni, parivāressare tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="M" n="1.0414" /> ca pāsādā, sayanañca mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Imassa cittamaññāya, nibbattissanti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi nāgasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā, hemakappanavāsasā <note>hemakappanivāsanā (sī. syā.), hemakappanivāsasā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, tomaraṅkusapāṇibhi;
```

```
Imaṃ paricarissanti, ratnapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi assasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Ājānīyāva jātiyā, sindhavā sīghavāhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, illiyācāpadhāribhi;
```

```
Tepimaṃ paricarissanti, ratnapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi rathasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Dīpā athopi veyagghā, sannaddhā ussitaddhajā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0556" /> gāmaṇīyehi, cāpahatthehi vammibhi;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, ratnapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi dhenusahassāni, dohaññā puṅgavūsabhe;
```

```
Vacchake janayissanti, ratnapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘‘Soḷasitthisahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, ratnapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, gotamo nāma cakkhumā;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamitvā, buddho loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0389" /> dassanamāgamma, pabbajissatikiñcano;
```

```
Tosayitvāna satthāraṃ, sāsanebhiramissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="2.0354" /> dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, kilese ghātayissati;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘Vīriyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0415" /> me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ patthayanto, sāsane viharāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0557" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā hemako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Hemakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

Sattarasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 8. Todeyyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘Rājā ajitañjayo <note>rājāsi vijayo (sī. aṭṭha.), rājā vijitajayo (syā.)</note> nāma, ketumatīpuruttame;
```

```
Sūro vikkamasampanno, puramajjhāvasī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa rañño pamattassa, aṭaviyo samuṭṭhahuṃ;
```

```
Otārā <note>uttarā (syā.), ocarā (pī.)</note> tuṇḍikā ceva, raṭṭhaṃ viddhaṃsayuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Paccante kupite khippaṃ, sannipātesirindamo;
```

```
Bhaṭe ceva balatthe ca, ariṃ niggāhayi tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, sūrā ca cammayodhino;
```

```
Dhanuggahā ca uggā ca, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘Āḷārikā ca kappakā, nhāpakā mālakārakā;
```

```
Sūrā vijitasaṅgāmā, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Khaggahatthā <pb ed="T" n="1.0558" /> ca purisā, cāpahatthā ca vammino;
```

```
Luddā vijitasaṅgāmā, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Tidhāpabhinnā <pb ed="M" n="1.0416" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0390" /> mātaṅgā, kuñjarā saṭṭhihāyanā;
```

```
Suvaṇṇakacchālaṅkārā, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Khamā sītassa uṇhassa, ukkāruharaṇassa ca;
```

```
Yodhājīvā katakammā, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhasaddaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0355" /> bherisaddaṃ, atho utuja <note>uddhava (sī.), uddaṭa (syā.)</note> saddakaṃ;
```

```
Etehi te hāsayantā, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Tisūlakontimantehi <note>tisūlakontamantehi (sī.), kavacehi tomarehi (sī.), dhanūhi tomarehi (syā.)</note> ca;
```

```
Koṭṭentānaṃ nipātentā <note>koṭṭayantā nivattentā (syā.)</note>, sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘Kimevātinisāmetvā <note>kavacānivāsetvā (syā.)</note>, sarājā ajitañjayo <note>ajinaṃ jino (sī.), ajitañjino (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Saṭṭhi pāṇasahassāni, sūle uttāsayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘Saddaṃ mānusakākaṃsu, aho rājā adhammiko;
```

```
Niraye paccamānassa, kadā anto bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭento, passāmi niraye tadā;
```

```
Na supāmi divārattiṃ, sūlena tajjayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ pamādena rajjena, vāhanena balena ca;
```

```
Na te pahonti dhāretuṃ, tāpayanti <note>tāsayanti (sī. syā.)</note> mamaṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ me puttehi dārehi, rajjena sakalena ca;
```

```
Yaṃnūna pabbajeyyāhaṃ, gatimaggaṃ visodhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0559" /> nāgasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsite;
```

```
Suvaṇṇakacche mātaṅge, hemakappanavāsase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Ārūḷhe gāmaṇīyehi, tomaraṅkusapāṇibhi;
```

```
Saṅgāmāvacare ṭhāne, anapekkho vihāyahaṃ;
```

```
Sakakammena santatto, nikkhamiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="M" n="1.0417" /> assasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsite;
```

```
Ājānīyeva jātiyā, sindhave sīghavāhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Ārūḷhe gāmaṇīyehi, cāpahatthehi vammibhi;
```

```
Pahāretvāna <note>pahāyitvāna (sī. pī.), chaḍḍayitvāna (syā.)</note> te sabbe, nikkhamiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="V" n="1.0391" /> rathasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsite;
```

```
Dīpe athopi veyagghe, sannaddhe ussitaddhaje;
```

```
Te sabbe parihāretvā <note>parivajjetvā (syā.), parihāyitvā (pī.)</note>, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="P" n="2.0356" /> dhenusahassāni, sabbā kaṃsūpadhāraṇā;
```

```
Tāyopi <note>gāviyo (syā.), dhenuyo (ka.)</note> chaḍḍayitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi itthisahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
```

```
Tā hitvā kandamānāyo, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhi gāmasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni sabbaso;
```

```
Chaḍḍayitvāna taṃ rajjaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘Nagarā <pb ed="T" n="1.0560" /> nikkhamitvāna, himavantamupāgamiṃ;
```

```
Bhāgīrathīnadītīre, assamaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna, agyāgāraṃ akāsahaṃ;
```

```
Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, vasāmi assame ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, suññāgāre ca jhāyato;
```

```
Na tu vijjati tāso me, na passe bhayabheravaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Ñāṇālokena jotanto, loke uppajji tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘Mama assamasāmantā, yakkho āsi mahiddhiko;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhamhi uppanne, ārocesi mamaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho <pb ed="M" n="1.0418" /> loke samuppanno, sumedho nāma cakkhumā;
```

```
Tāreti janataṃ sabbaṃ, tampi so tārayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘Yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvā, saṃviggo āsi tāvade;
```

```
Buddho buddhoti cintento, assamaṃ paṭisāmayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘Aggidāruñca chaḍḍetvā, saṃsāmetvāna santhataṃ;
```

```
Assamaṃ abhivanditvā, nikkhamiṃ vipinā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
‘‘Tato candanamādāya, gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ;
```

```
Devadevaṃ gavesanto, upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā <pb ed="V" n="1.0392" /> tamhi samaye, sumedho lokanāyako;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāsento, bodheti janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘Añjaliṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0561" /> paggahetvāna, sīse katvāna candanaṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, imā gāthā abhāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vassike pupphamānamhi, santike upavāyati;
```

```
Tvaṃ vīra guṇagandhena, disā sabbā pavāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘‘Campake nāgavanike, atimuttakaketake;
```

```
Sālesu pupphamānesu, anuvātaṃ pavāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tava <pb ed="P" n="2.0357" /> gandhaṃ suṇitvāna, himavantā idhāgamiṃ;
```

```
Pūjemi taṃ mahāvīra, lokajeṭṭha mahāyasa’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘Varacandanenānulimpiṃ, sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, tuṇhī aṭṭhāsi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho nāma bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me guṇe pakittesi, candanañca apūjayi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ādeyyavākyavacano, brahmā uju patāpavā;
```

```
Pañcavīsatikappāni, sappabhāso bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘‘Chabbīsatikappasate, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0419" /> devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="1.0562" /> cutoyaṃ manujo, manussattaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyutto, brahmabandhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ajjhāyako mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Tilakkhaṇena sampanno, bāvarī nāma brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa sisso bhavitvāna, hessati mantapāragū;
```

```
Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pucchitvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0393" /> nipuṇe pañhe, bhāvayitvāna añjasaṃ <note>hāsayitvāna mānasaṃ (syā.), bhāvayitvāna sañcayaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘Tividhaggi nibbutā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā todeyyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Todeyyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Jatukaṇṇittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="T" n="1.0563" /> haṃsavatiyā, seṭṭhiputto ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Samappito kāmaguṇe, paricāremahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="P" n="2.0358" /> <note>tayo (sī.)</note> pāsādamāruyha, mahābhoge valañjako <note>ubbiddhā gehaluñjakā (ka.), ubbiddhāgehalañchakā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Tattha naccehi gītehi, paricāremahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Tūriyā <pb ed="M" n="1.0420" /> āhatā mayhaṃ, sammatāḷasamāhitā;
```

```
Naccantā <note>rañjantī (syā.), rajjantā (ka.)</note> itthiyo sabbā, harantiyeva me mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Celāpikā <note>celāvakā (syā.), velāmikā (pī.)</note> lāmaṇikā <note>vāmanikā (syā. pī.)</note>, kuñjavāsī timajjhikā <note>kuñjavā sīhimajjhitā (syā.), kujjā vā sīhimajjhikā (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Laṅghikā sokajjhāyī ca, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘Vetāḷino kumbhathūnī, naṭā ca naccakā bahū;
```

```
Naṭakā nāṭakā ceva, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘Kappakā nhāpakā sūdā, mālākārā supāsakā <note>sumāpakā (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Jallā mallā ca te sabbe, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Etesu kīḷamānesu, sikkhite katupāsane;
```

```
Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi, indova tidasaṅgaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘Addhikā pathikā sabbe, yācakā varakā bahū;
```

```
Upagacchanti te niccaṃ, bhikkhayantā mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇā <pb ed="V" n="1.0394" /> brāhmaṇā ceva, puññakkhettā anuttarā;
```

```
Vaḍḍhayantā mamaṃ puññaṃ, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭagā <note>paṭakā (sī. syā.), padakā (pī.)</note> laṭukā <note>laṭakā (sī.)</note> sabbe, nigaṇṭhā pupphasāṭakā;
```

```
Tedaṇḍikā <pb ed="T" n="1.0564" /> ekasikhā, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘Ājīvakā viluttāvī, godhammā devadhammikā;
```

```
Rajojalladharā ete, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Parittakā santipattā <note>parivattakā siddhipattā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kodhapugganikā <note>koṇḍapuggaṇikā (sī.), koṇḍapuggalikā (pī.)</note> bahū;
```

```
Tapassī vanacārī ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Oḍḍakā damiḷā ceva, sākuḷā malavāḷakā <note>malayālakā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Savarā yonakā ceva, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Andhakā <pb ed="M" n="1.0421" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0359" /> muṇḍakā sabbe, koṭalā hanuvindakā <note>kolakā sānuvindakā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ārāvacīnaraṭṭhā ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Alasandakā <note>alasantā (ka.)</note> pallavakā, dhammarā niggamānusā <note>babbarā bhaggakārusā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Gehikā <note>rohitā (sī.), bāhikā (pī.)</note> cetaputtā ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Mādhurakā kosalakā, kaliṅgā <note>kāsikā (sī.)</note> hatthiporikā;
```

```
Isiṇḍā makkalā ceva, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Celāvakā ārabbhā <note>arammā (sī. pī.)</note> ca, oghuḷhā <note>okkalā (sī.)</note> meghalā bahū;
```

```
Khuddakā suddakā ceva, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Rohaṇā sindhavā ceva, citakā ekakaṇṇikā;
```

```
Suraṭṭhā aparantā ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Suppārakā kumārā <note>kikumārā (sī. pī.)</note> ca, mallasovaṇṇabhūmikā <note>malayā soṇṇabhūmikā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Vajjītaṅgā <note>vajjī tārā (sī.), vajjīhārā (syā. pī.)</note> ca te sabbe, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Naḷakārā <pb ed="T" n="1.0565" /> pesakārā, cammakārā ca tacchakā;
```

```
Kammārā kumbhakārā ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇikārā lohakārā, soṇṇakārā ca dussikā;
```

```
Tipukārā ca te sabbe, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Usukārā bhamakārā, pesakārā ca gandhikā;
```

```
Rajakā tunnavāyā ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Telikā <pb ed="V" n="1.0395" /> kaṭṭhahārā ca, udahārā ca pessikā;
```

```
Sūpikā sūparakkhā ca, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Dovārikā <pb ed="P" n="2.0360" /> anīkaṭṭhā, bandhikā <note>vandikā (sī.), ganthikā (syā.), sandikā (pī.)</note> pupphachaḍḍakā;
```

```
Hatthāruhā hatthipālā, āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Ānandassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0422" /> mahārañño <note>ānandassa nāma rañño (syā.), arindamanāma rañño (pī.)</note>, mamatthassa <note>pamattassa (sī. pī.), samaggassa (syā.)</note> adāsahaṃ;
```

```
Sattavaṇṇena ratanena, ūnatthaṃ <note>ūnattaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pūrayāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Ye mayā kittitā sabbe, nānāvaṇṇā bahū janā;
```

```
Tesāhaṃ cittamaññāya, tappayiṃ ratanenahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Vaggūsu bhāsamānāsu, vajjamānāsu bherisu;
```

```
Saṅkhesu dhamayantesu, sakagehe ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, padumuttaranāyako;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, parikkhīṇāsavehi so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhūhi sahito vīthiṃ, paṭipajjittha cakkhumā;
```

```
Obhāsento disā sabbā, dīparukkhova jotati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Vajjanti <pb ed="T" n="1.0566" /> bheriyo sabbā, gacchante lokanāyake;
```

```
Pabhā niddhāvate tassa, sataraṃsīva uggato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Kavāṭantarikāyāpi, paviṭṭhena ca rasminā;
```

```
Antogharesu vipulo, āloko āsi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Pabhaṃ disvāna buddhassa, pārisajje avocahaṃ;
```

```
Nissaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho, imaṃ vīthimupāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Khippaṃ oruyha pāsādā, agamiṃ antarāpaṇaṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anukampatu me buddho, jalajuttamanāyako;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, adhivāsesi so muni’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Nimantetvāna sambuddhaṃ, abhinesiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ;
```

```
Tattha annena pānena, santappesiṃ mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Bhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya, buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Sataṅgikena tūriyena, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Antoghare nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0423" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0396" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0361" /> maṃ tūriyehupaṭṭhāsi, annapānañcadāsi me;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pahūtabhakkho hutvāna, sahirañño sabhojano;
```

```
Catudīpe ekarajjaṃ, kārayissatiyaṃ naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcasīle <pb ed="T" n="1.0567" /> samādāya, dasakammapathe tato;
```

```
Samādāya pavattento, parisaṃ sikkhāpayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tūriyasatasahassāni, bheriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Vajjayissantimaṃ niccaṃ, upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘‘Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ rājā, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappasatasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘‘Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Anūnabhogo hutvāna, manussattaṃ gamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ajjhāyako bhavitvāna, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto, carissati mahiṃ imaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘‘So pacchā pabbajitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Gotamassa bhagavato, sāsanebhiramissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārādhayitvāna sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Kilese jhāpayitvāna, arahāyaṃ bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘Vipine byaggharājāva, migarājāva kesarī;
```

```
Abhīto viharāmajja, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke <pb ed="T" n="1.0568" /> manusse vā, dalidde duggatimhi vā;
```

```
Nibbattiṃ me na passāmi, upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Vivekamanuyuttomhi<pb ed="V" n="1.0397" />, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="1.0424" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jatukaṇṇitthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Jatukaṇṇittherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Udenattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="P" n="2.0362" />, padumo nāma pabbato;
```

```
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Nadiyo sandare tattha, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Acchodakā sītajalā, sandare nadiyo sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṭhīnā <pb ed="T" n="1.0569" /> pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
```

```
Sobhentā nadiyo ete, vasanti nadiyā sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Ambajambūhi sañchannā, kareritilakā tathā;
```

```
Uddālakā pāṭaliyo, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅkolakā bimbijālā, māyākārī ca pupphitā;
```

```
Gandhena upavāyantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Atimuttā sattalikā, nāgā sālā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Kosambā saḷalā nīpā, aṭṭhaṅgāpi ca pupphitā <note>aṭṭhaṅgā ca supupphitā (sī.), kaṭṭhaṅgā ca supupphitā (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘Harītakā āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā;
```

```
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phalāni bahu assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘Kalambā <pb ed="M" n="1.0425" /> kandalī tattha, pupphanti mama assame;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ <note>dibbagandhā (sī. syā. pī.) evaṃ paratthapi</note> sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘Asokapiṇḍivārī <pb ed="V" n="1.0398" /> ca <note>asokapiṇḍī ca varī (sī. syā.), asokapiṇḍī ca vārī (pī.)</note>, nimbarukkhā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘Punnāgā giripunnāgā, timirā tattha pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘Nigguṇḍī sirinigguṇḍī, camparukkhettha pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘Avidūre <pb ed="T" n="1.0570" /> pokkharaṇī, cakkavākūpakūjitā;
```

```
Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘Acchodakā <pb ed="P" n="2.0363" /> sītajalā, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Acchā phalikasamānā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘Padumā pupphare tattha, puṇḍarīkā ca uppalā;
```

```
Mandālakehi sañchannā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
```

```
Vicarantāva te tattha, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhīlā susumārā ca, kacchapā ca gahā bahū;
```

```
Ogahā ajagarā ca, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘Pārevatā ravihaṃsā, cakkavākā nadīcarā;
```

```
Dindibhā sāḷikā cettha, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘Nayitā ambagandhī ca, ketakā tattha pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhā byagghā ca dīpī ca, acchakokataracchakā;
```

```
Anusañcarantā pavane, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṭābhārena bharitā, ajinuttaravāsanā;
```

```
Anusañcarantā pavane, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘Ajinānidharā <pb ed="M" n="1.0426" /> ete, nipakā santavuttino;
```

```
Appāhārāva te sabbe, sobhenti mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘Khāribhāraṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0571" /> gahetvāna, ajjhogayha vanaṃ tadā;
```

```
Mūlaphalāni bhuñjantā, vasanti assame tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0399" /> te dāruṃ āharanti, udakaṃ pādadhovanaṃ;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ ānubhāvena, sayamevāharīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, isayettha samāgatā;
```

```
Sabbeva jhāyino ete, uttamatthagavesakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘Tapassino brahmacārī, codentā appanāva te;
```

```
Ambarāvacarā sabbe, vasanti assame tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcāhaṃ sannipatanti, ekaggā santavuttino;
```

```
Aññoññaṃ abhivādetvā, pakkamanti disāmukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ, uppajji tāvade jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘Mama <pb ed="P" n="2.0364" /> assamasāmantā, yakkho āsi mahiddhiko;
```

```
So me saṃsittha sambuddhaṃ, jalajuttamanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘Esa buddho samuppanno, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Khippaṃ gantvāna sambuddhaṃ, payirūpāsa mārisa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘Yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvā, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Assamaṃ saṃsāmetvāna, nikkhamiṃ vipinā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘Ceḷeva ḍayhamānamhi, nikkhamitvāna assamā;
```

```
Ekarattiṃ nivāsetvā <note>nivasitvā (sī.), nivāsena (?)</note>, upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="1.0572" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāsento, desesi amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
‘‘Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha, upagantvā mahesino;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, buddhassa abhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjayitvāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0427" /> sambuddhaṃ, jalajuttamanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
‘‘Yena ñāṇena sambuddho, vasatīha anāsavo;
```

```
Taṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṃsārasotaṃ chinditvā, tāresi sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, taṇhāsotaṃ taranti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tuvaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0400" /> satthā ca ketu ca, dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Parāyaṇo patiṭṭhā ca, dīpo ca dvipaduttama <note>dipaduttama (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā gaṇino loke, satthavāhā pavuccare;
```

```
Tuvaṃ aggosi sabbaññu, tava antogadhāva te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tava ñāṇena sabbaññu, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Tava dassanamāgamma, dukkhassantaṃ karissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ye kecime gandhajātā, loke vāyanti cakkhuma;
```

```
Tava gandhasamo natthi, puññakkhette mahāmune’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiracchānayoniṃ nirayaṃ, parimocesi <note>parimocehi (syā. ka.)</note> cakkhuma;
```

```
Asaṅkhataṃ padaṃ santaṃ, desesi <note>desehi (syā. ka.)</note> tvaṃ mahāmune’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="1.0573" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo <pb ed="P" n="2.0365" /> me ñāṇaṃ apūjesi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
‘‘Suladdhalābhaṃ laddhomhi, tosayitvāna subbataṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="1.0428" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udeno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Udenattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Metteyyavaggo ekacattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Metteyyo puṇṇako thero, mettagū dhotakopi ca;
```

```
Upasivo <pb ed="T" n="1.0574" /> ca nando ca, hemako sattamo tahiṃ.
```

```
Todeyyo jatukaṇṇī ca, udeno ca mahāyaso;
```

```
Tīṇi gāthāsatānettha, asīti tīṇi cuttariṃ.
```

### 42. Bhaddālivaggo

#### 1. Bhaddālittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho <pb ed="T" n="2.0001" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0429" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0401" /> nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Vivekakāmo lokaggo, himavantamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā himavaṃ, sumedho lokanāyako;
```

```
Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhiṃ so samāpanno, sumedho lokanāyako;
```

```
Sattarattindivaṃ buddho, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Khāribhāraṃ <note>khārikājaṃ (sī.)</note> gahetvāna, vanamajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna, sammajjitvāna assamaṃ;
```

```
Catudaṇḍe ṭhapetvāna, akāsiṃ maṇḍapaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Sālapupphaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0366" /> āharitvā, maṇḍapaṃ chādayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, abhivandiṃ tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0002" /> vadanti sumedhoti, bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddhassa giramaññāya, sabbe devā samāgamuṃ;
```

```
Asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Devasaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me sattāhaṃ maṇḍapaṃ, dhārayī sālachāditaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devabhūto manusso vā, hemavaṇṇo bhavissati;
```

```
Pahūtabhogo hutvāna, kāmabhogī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi <pb ed="M" n="1.0430" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0402" /> nāgasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā, hemakappanavāsasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, tomaraṅkusapāṇibhi;
```

```
Sāyaṃ pāto <note>sāyapāto (pī.)</note> upaṭṭhānaṃ, āgamissantimaṃ naraṃ;
```

```
Tehi nāgehi parivuto, ramissati ayaṃ naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi assasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Ājānīyāva jātiyā, sindhavā sīghavāhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, illiyācāpadhāribhi;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi rathasahassāni, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
```

```
Dīpā <pb ed="T" n="2.0003" /> athopi veyagghā, sannaddhā ussitaddhajā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, cāpahatthehi vammibhi;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhi gāmasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni sabbaso;
```

```
Pahūtadhanadhaññāni, susamiddhāni sabbaso;
```

```
Sadā pātubhavissanti, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthī assā rathā pattī, senā ca caturaṅginī;
```

```
Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0367" /> tīṇikkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi<pb ed="M" n="1.0431" />, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Etthantaramupādāya, gavesiṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0403" /> mayhaṃ suladdhaṃ me, yamahaññāsi sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Namo <pb ed="T" n="2.0004" /> te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Tava ñāṇaṃ pakittetvā, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito homi, phalaṃ me ñāṇakittane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddālitthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhaddālittherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ekachattiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre, assamo sukato mama;
```

```
Susuddhapulinākiṇṇo, pannasālā sumāpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Uttānakūlā nadikā, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Macchakacchapasampannā <note>… sañchannā (ka.)</note>, susumāranisevitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Acchā <pb ed="T" n="2.0005" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0432" /> dīpī ca mayūrā, karavīkā ca sāḷikā;
```

```
Kūjanti sabbadā ete, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Kokilā mañjubhāṇī ca, haṃsā ca madhurassarā;
```

```
Abhikūjanti te tattha, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhā byagghā varāhā ca, accha <note>vaka (sī. pī.), bakā (syā.), vakā (ka.)</note> kokataracchakā;
```

```
Giriduggamhi nādenti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Eṇīmigā <pb ed="V" n="1.0404" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0368" /> ca sarabhā, bheraṇḍā sūkarā bahū;
```

```
Giriduggamhi nādenti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Uddālakā campakā ca, pāṭalī sinduvārakā;
```

```
Atimuttā asokā ca, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ <note>pupphanti mama assame (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅkolā yūthikā ceva, sattalī bimbijālikā;
```

```
Kaṇikārā ca pupphanti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ <note>kaṇikākaṇikārā ca, pupphanti mama assame (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Nāgā sālā ca saḷalā, puṇḍarīkettha pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjunā asanā cettha, mahānāmā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Sālā ca kaṅgupupphā ca, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Ambā jambū ca tilakā, nimbā ca sālakalyāṇī;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Asokā ca kapiṭṭhā ca, girimālettha <note>bhaginimālettha (sī. pī.), bhaginimālā ca (syā.)</note> pupphitā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Kadambā <pb ed="T" n="2.0006" /> kadalī ceva, isimuggā ca ropitā;
```

```
Dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Harītakā āmalakā, ambajambuvibhītakā;
```

```
Kolā bhallātakā billā, phalino mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Avidūre <pb ed="M" n="1.0433" /> pokkharaṇī, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā, aññe pupphanti kesarī;
```

```
Opattakaṇṇikā ceva, pupphanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā, balajā muñjarohitā;
```

```
Acchodakamhi vicaraṃ, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Nayitā ambagandhī ca, anukūle ca ketakā;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Madhu bhisamhā savati, khīrasappi muḷālibhi;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Pulinā <pb ed="V" n="1.0405" /> sobhanā tattha, ākiṇṇā jalasevitā;
```

```
Opupphā pupphitā senti, sobhayantā mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṭābhārena <pb ed="P" n="2.0369" /> bharitā, ajinuttaravāsanā;
```

```
Vākacīradharā sabbe, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Yugamattamapekkhantā, nipakā santavuttino;
```

```
Kāmabhoge anapekkhā, vasanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā<pb ed="T" n="2.0007" />, paṅkadantā rajassirā;
```

```
Rajojalladharā sabbe, vasanti mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Abhiññāpāramippattā, antalikkhacarā ca te;
```

```
Uggacchantā nabhaṃ ete, sobhayanti mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi sissehi parivuto, vasāmi vipine tadā;
```

```
Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi, sadā jhānasamappito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, atthadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsento, uppajji lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Atha aññataro sisso, āgacchi mama santikaṃ;
```

```
Mante ajjhetukāmo so, chaḷaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho <pb ed="M" n="1.0434" /> loke samuppanno, atthadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāsento, deseti amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Tuṭṭhahaṭṭho pamudito, dhammantaragatāsayo;
```

```
Assamā abhinikkhamma, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
```

```
Etha sabbe gamissāma, sammāsambuddhasantikaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādapaṭikarā te, sadhamme pāramiṃ gatā;
```

```
Sādhūti sampaṭicchiṃsu, uttamatthagavesakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṭābhārabharitā te <note>jaṭābhārena bharitā (ka.)</note>, ajinuttaravāsanā;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesantā, nikkhamiṃsu vanā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā <pb ed="T" n="2.0008" /> tamhi samaye, atthadassī mahāyaso;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāsento, deseti amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Setacchattaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0406" /> gahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃ;
```

```
Ekāhaṃ dhārayitvāna, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī tu bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me chattaṃ adhāresi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘‘Imassa jāyamānassa, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Dhāressati sadā chattaṃ, chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattasattatikappāni<pb ed="P" n="2.0370" />, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattasattatikkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, gotamo sakyapuṅgavo;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsento, uppajjissati cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0435" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Yato ahaṃ kammamakaṃ, chattaṃ buddhassa dhārayaṃ;
